===== FILE: ./benches/phase35.rs =====
     1	use criterion::{BenchmarkId, Criterion, criterion_group, criterion_main};
     2	use ecs::prelude::*;
     3	use scheduler::{ScheduleLabel, SystemSet};
     4	use std::hint::black_box;
     5	
     6	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
     7	struct Position {
     8	    x: f32,
     9	    y: f32,
    10	}
    11	
    12	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
    13	struct Velocity {
    14	    x: f32,
    15	    y: f32,
    16	}
    17	
    18	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
    19	struct Simulated;
    20	
    21	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
    22	struct Disabled;
    23	
    24	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
    25	struct Health(i32);
    26	
    27	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
    28	struct ChurnTag;
    29	
    30	#[derive(Debug, Default, ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
    31	struct MixedStats(u64);
    32

    38

    41	#[derive(Debug, Default, ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
    42	struct R1(u64);
    43	#[derive(Debug, Default, ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
    44	struct R2(u64);
    45	#[derive(Debug, Default, ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
    46	struct R3(u64);
    47	#[derive(Debug, Default, ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]

    50	#[derive(Copy, Clone)]
    51	struct W2;
    52	impl ScheduleLabel for W2 {
    53	    fn name() -> &'static str {
    54	        "W2"
    55	    }
    56	}

    59	struct W3;
    60	impl ScheduleLabel for W3 {

    79	    }

    83	struct SetA;

    86	        "SetA"

    94	        "SetB"

   105	
   106	fn build_world_for_w1(entity_count: usize) -> World {
   107	    let mut world = World::new();
   108	    for i in 0..entity_count {
   109	        world.spawn((
   110	            Position {
   111	                x: i as f32,
   112	                y: (i as f32) * 0.5,
   113	            },
   114	            Velocity { x: 1.0, y: -0.5 },
   115	        ));
   116	    }
   117	    world
   118	}
   119	
   120	fn workload_w1(c: &mut Criterion) {
   121	    let mut group = c.benchmark_group("w1_broad_transform_update");
   122	    for &size in &[10_000_usize, 50_000, 200_000] {
   123	        let mut world = build_world_for_w1(size);
   124	        let query = world.query_state::<(&mut Position, &Velocity), ()>();
   125	        group.bench_with_input(BenchmarkId::new("entities", size), &size, |b, _| {
   126	            b.iter(|| {
   127	                let mut checksum = 0.0_f32;
   128	                for _ in 0..4 {
   129	                    for (position, velocity) in query.iter(&mut world) {
   130	                        position.x += velocity.x;
   131	                        position.y += velocity.y;
   132	                        checksum += position.x + position.y;
   133	                    }
   134	                }
   135	                black_box(checksum)
   136	            });
   137	        });
   138	    }
   139	    group.finish();
   140	}
   141	
   142	fn w2_move(mut query: Query<(&mut Position, &Velocity), (With<Simulated>, Without<Disabled>)>) {
   143	    for (position, velocity) in query.iter() {
   144	        position.x += velocity.x;
   145	        position.y += velocity.y;
   146	    }
   147	}
   148	
   149	fn w2_mutate_health(mut query: Query<&mut Health, With<Simulated>>) {
   150	    for health in query.iter() {
   151	        health.0 = health.0.saturating_sub(1);
   152	    }
   153	}
   154	
   155	fn w2_scan_changed(
   156	    mut query: Query<(Entity, &Health), Changed<Health>>,
   157	    mut stats: ResMut<MixedStats>,
   158	) {
   159	    let mut seen = 0_u64;
   160	    for _ in query.iter() {
   161	        seen = seen.saturating_add(1);
   162	    }
   163	    (*stats).0 = (*stats).0.wrapping_add(seen);
   164	}
   165	
   166	fn w2_scan_added(
   167	    mut query: Query<(Entity, &Health), Added<Health>>,
   168	    mut stats: ResMut<MixedStats>,
   169	) {
   170	    let mut seen = 0_u64;
   171	    for _ in query.iter() {
   172	        seen = seen.saturating_add(1);
   173	    }
   174	    (*stats).0 = (*stats).0.wrapping_add(seen);
   175	}
   176	
   177	fn build_runtime_for_w2(entity_count: usize) -> (World, Runtime) {
   178	    let mut world = World::new();
   179	    world.insert_resource(MixedStats::default());
   180	
   181	    for i in 0..entity_count {
   182	        let disabled = i % 8 == 0;
   183	        if disabled {
   184	            world.spawn((
   185	                Position {
   186	                    x: i as f32,
   187	                    y: 0.0,
   188	                },
   189	                Velocity { x: 1.0, y: 0.25 },
   190	                Health(100),
   191	                Simulated,
   192	                Disabled,
   193	            ));
   194	        } else {
   195	            world.spawn((
   196	                Position {
   197	                    x: i as f32,
   198	                    y: 0.0,
   199	                },
   200	                Velocity { x: 1.0, y: 0.25 },
   201	                Health(100),
   202	                Simulated,
   203	            ));
   204	        }
   205	    }
   206	
   207	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   208	    runtime.add_systems::<W2, _, _>(
   209	        &mut world,
   210	        (w2_move, w2_mutate_health, w2_scan_changed, w2_scan_added),
   211	    );
   212	    (world, runtime)
   213	}
   214	
   215	fn workload_w2(c: &mut Criterion) {
   216	    let mut group = c.benchmark_group("w2_gameplay_mixed");
   217	    for &size in &[5_000_usize, 20_000] {
   218	        let (mut world, mut runtime) = build_runtime_for_w2(size);
   219	        group.bench_with_input(BenchmarkId::new("entities", size), &size, |b, _| {
   220	            b.iter(|| {
   221	                runtime
   222	                    .run_schedule::<W2>(&mut world)
   223	                    .expect("w2 schedule should run");
   224	                black_box(world.resource::<MixedStats>().expect("stats resource").0)
   225	            });
   226	        });
   227	    }
   228	    group.finish();
   229	}
   230	
   231	fn w3_spawn(mut commands: Commands) {
   232	    for i in 0..128_u32 {
   233	        commands.spawn((
   234	            ChurnTag,
   235	            Position {
   236	                x: i as f32,
   237	                y: i as f32,
   238	            },
   239	            Velocity { x: 0.1, y: -0.1 },
   240	        ));
   241	    }
   242	}
   243	
   244	fn w3_despawn(mut commands: Commands, mut query: Query<(Entity, &ChurnTag)>) {
   245	    for (idx, (entity, _)) in query.iter().enumerate() {
   246	        if idx >= 128 {
   247	            break;
   248	        }
   249	        commands.despawn(entity);
   250	    }
   251	}
   252	
   253	fn build_runtime_for_w3(entity_count: usize) -> (World, Runtime) {
   254	    let mut world = World::new();
   255	    for i in 0..entity_count {
   256	        world.spawn((
   257	            ChurnTag,
   258	            Position {
   259	                x: i as f32,
   260	                y: 0.0,
   261	            },
   262	            Velocity { x: 0.0, y: 0.0 },
   263	        ));
   264	    }
   265	
   266	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   267	    runtime.add_systems::<W3, _, _>(&mut world, (w3_spawn, w3_despawn));
   268	    (world, runtime)
   269	}
   270	
   271	fn workload_w3(c: &mut Criterion) {
   272	    let mut group = c.benchmark_group("w3_structural_churn");
   273	    let (mut world, mut runtime) = build_runtime_for_w3(20_000);
   274	    group.bench_function("spawn_insert_remove_despawn_commands", |b| {
   275	        b.iter(|| {
   276	            runtime
   277	                .run_schedule::<W3>(&mut world)
   278	                .expect("w3 schedule should run");
   279	            black_box(world.current_change_tick())
   280	        });
   281	    });
   282	    group.finish();
   283	}
   284	
   285	fn w4_write_events(mut writer: EventWriter<BenchEvent>) {
   286	    for i in 0..256_u32 {
   287	        writer.send(BenchEvent(i));
   288	    }
   289	}
   290	
   291	fn w4_read_events(
   292	    reader: EventReader<BenchEvent>,
   293	    mut query: Query<&Position>,
   294	    mut stats: ResMut<EventStats>,
   295	) {
   296	    let events_seen = reader
   297	        .iter()
   298	        .fold(0_u64, |acc, event| acc.wrapping_add(event.0 as u64));
   299	    let entities_seen = query.iter().count() as u64;
   300	    (*stats).0 = (*stats)
   301	        .0
   302	        .wrapping_add(events_seen)
   303	        .wrapping_add(entities_seen);
   304	}
   305	
   306	fn build_runtime_for_w4(entity_count: usize) -> (World, Runtime) {
   307	    let mut world = World::new();
   308	    world.insert_resource(EventStats::default());
   309	    for i in 0..entity_count {
   310	        world.spawn((
   311	            Position {
   312	                x: i as f32,
   313	                y: i as f32,
   314	            },
   315	            Velocity { x: 0.0, y: 0.0 },
   316	        ));
   317	    }
   318	
   319	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   320	    runtime.add_systems::<W4, _, _>(&mut world, (w4_write_events, w4_read_events));
   321	    (world, runtime)
   322	}
   323	
   324	fn workload_w4(c: &mut Criterion) {
   325	    let mut group = c.benchmark_group("w4_event_heavy");
   326	    let (mut world, mut runtime) = build_runtime_for_w4(10_000);
   327	    group.bench_function("event_reader_writer_interleaved_query", |b| {
   328	        b.iter(|| {
   329	            runtime
   330	                .run_schedule::<W4>(&mut world)
   331	                .expect("w4 schedule should run");
   332	            world.clear_events::<BenchEvent>();
   333	            black_box(world.resource::<EventStats>().expect("event stats").0)
   334	        });
   335	    });
   336	    group.finish();
   337	}
   338	
   339	fn w5_write_r0(mut r0: ResMut<R0>) {
   340	    (*r0).0 = (*r0).0.wrapping_add(1);
   341	}
   342	
   343	fn w5_write_r1(mut r1: ResMut<R1>) {
   344	    (*r1).0 = (*r1).0.wrapping_add(1);
   345	}
   346	
   347	fn w5_write_r2(mut r2: ResMut<R2>) {
   348	    (*r2).0 = (*r2).0.wrapping_add(1);
   349	}
   350	
   351	fn w5_write_r3(mut r3: ResMut<R3>) {
   352	    (*r3).0 = (*r3).0.wrapping_add(1);
   353	}
   354	
   355	fn w5_read_mix(r0: Res<R0>, r1: Res<R1>, r2: Res<R2>, mut sink: ResMut<Sink>) {
   356	    (*sink).0 = (*sink)
   357	        .0
   358	        .wrapping_add((*r0).0)
   359	        .wrapping_add((*r1).0)
   360	        .wrapping_add((*r2).0);
   361	}
   362	
   363	fn w5_read_mix_alt(r1: Res<R1>, r3: Res<R3>, mut sink: ResMut<Sink>) {
   364	    (*sink).0 = (*sink).0.wrapping_add((*r1).0).wrapping_add((*r3).0);
   365	}
   366	
   367	fn register_w5_systems(runtime: &mut Runtime, world: &mut World, repeats: usize) {
   368	    for _ in 0..repeats {
   369	        runtime.add_systems::<W5, _, _>(
   370	            world,
   371	            (
   372	                w5_write_r0.in_set(SetA),
   373	                w5_write_r1.in_set(SetA),
   374	                w5_read_mix.after(SetA).in_set(SetB),
   375	                w5_write_r2.after(SetB).in_set(SetC),
   376	                w5_read_mix_alt.after(SetC),
   377	                w5_write_r3.in_set(SetA),
   378	            ),
   379	        );
   380	    }
   381	}
   382	
   383	fn build_runtime_for_w5(repeats: usize) -> (World, Runtime) {
   384	    let mut world = World::new();
   385	    world.insert_resource(R0::default());
   386	    world.insert_resource(R1::default());
   387	    world.insert_resource(R2::default());
   388	    world.insert_resource(R3::default());
   389	    world.insert_resource(Sink::default());
   390	
   391	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   392	    register_w5_systems(&mut runtime, &mut world, repeats);
   393	    (world, runtime)
   394	}
   395	
   396	fn workload_w5(c: &mut Criterion) {
   397	    let mut group = c.benchmark_group("w5_scheduler_stress");
   398	
   399	    group.bench_function("scheduler_plan_build_96_systems", |b| {
   400	        b.iter(|| {
   401	            let (world, mut runtime) = build_runtime_for_w5(16);
   402	            let plan = runtime.plan_for::<W5>().map(|plan| plan.stages.len());
   403	            black_box(plan);
   404	            black_box(world.resource::<Sink>().expect("sink resource").0)
   405	        });
   406	    });
   407	
   408	    let (mut world, mut runtime) = build_runtime_for_w5(16);
   409	    group.bench_function("scheduler_stage_execution_96_systems", |b| {
   410	        b.iter(|| {
   411	            runtime
   412	                .run_schedule::<W5>(&mut world)
   413	                .expect("w5 schedule should run");
   414	            black_box(world.resource::<Sink>().expect("sink resource").0)
   415	        });
   416	    });
   417	
   418	    group.finish();
   419	}
   420	
   421	fn phase35_benches(c: &mut Criterion) {
   422	    workload_w1(c);
   423	    workload_w2(c);
   424	    workload_w3(c);
   425	    workload_w4(c);
   426	    workload_w5(c);
   427	}
   428	
   429	criterion_group!(phase35, phase35_benches);
   430	criterion_main!(phase35);

===== END FILE: ./benches/phase35.rs =====

   131	                        position.y += velocity.y;

   142	fn workload_c2_broad_read(c: &mut Criterion) {
   143	    let mut group = c.benchmark_group("c2_broad_read_only");
   144	    for &size in &[10_000_usize, 50_000, 200_000] {
   145	        let world = build_world_for_w1(size);
   146	        let query = world.query_state::<&Position, ()>();
   147	        group.bench_with_input(BenchmarkId::new("entities", size), &size, |b, _| {
   148	            b.iter(|| {
   149	                let mut checksum = 0.0_f32;
   150	                for _ in 0..4 {
   151	                    for position in query.iter(&world) {
   152	                        checksum += position.x + position.y;
   153	                    }
   154	                }
   155	                black_box(checksum)
   156	            });
   157	        });
   158	    }
   159	    group.finish();
   160	}
   161	
   162	fn workload_c3_broad_write(c: &mut Criterion) {
   163	    let mut group = c.benchmark_group("c3_broad_write_only");
   164	    for &size in &[10_000_usize, 50_000, 200_000] {
   165	        let mut world = build_world_for_w1(size);
   166	        let query = world.query_state::<&mut Velocity, ()>();
   167	        group.bench_with_input(BenchmarkId::new("entities", size), &size, |b, _| {
   168	            b.iter(|| {
   169	                let mut checksum = 0.0_f32;
   170	                for _ in 0..4 {
   171	                    for velocity in query.iter(&mut world) {
   172	                        velocity.x += 0.01;
   173	                        velocity.y -= 0.01;
   174	                        checksum += velocity.x + velocity.y;
   175	                    }
   176	                }
   177	                black_box(checksum)
   178	            });
   179	        });
   180	    }
   181	    group.finish();
   182	}
   183	
   184	fn w2_move(mut query: Query<(&mut Position, &Velocity), (With<Simulated>, Without<Disabled>)>) {
   185	    for (position, velocity) in query.iter() {
   186	        position.x += velocity.x;
   187	        position.y += velocity.y;
   188	    }
   189	}
   190	
   191	fn w2_mutate_health(mut query: Query<&mut Health, With<Simulated>>) {
   192	    for health in query.iter() {
   193	        health.0 = health.0.saturating_sub(1);
   194	    }
   195	}
   196	
   197	fn w2_scan_changed(
   198	    mut query: Query<(Entity, &Health), Changed<Health>>,
   199	    mut stats: ResMut<MixedStats>,
   200	) {
   201	    let mut seen = 0_u64;
   202	    for _ in query.iter() {
   203	        seen = seen.saturating_add(1);
   204	    }
   205	    (*stats).0 = (*stats).0.wrapping_add(seen);
   206	}
   207	
   208	fn w2_scan_added(
   209	    mut query: Query<(Entity, &Health), Added<Health>>,
   210	    mut stats: ResMut<MixedStats>,
   211	) {
   212	    let mut seen = 0_u64;
   213	    for _ in query.iter() {
   214	        seen = seen.saturating_add(1);
   215	    }
   216	    (*stats).0 = (*stats).0.wrapping_add(seen);
   217	}
   218	
   219	fn build_runtime_for_w2(entity_count: usize) -> (World, Runtime) {
   220	    let mut world = World::new();
   221	    world.insert_resource(MixedStats::default());
   222	
   223	    for i in 0..entity_count {
   224	        let disabled = i % 8 == 0;
   225	        if disabled {
   226	            world.spawn((
   227	                Position {
   228	                    x: i as f32,
   229	                    y: 0.0,
   230	                },
   231	                Velocity { x: 1.0, y: 0.25 },
   232	                Health(100),
   233	                Simulated,
   234	                Disabled,
   235	            ));
   236	        } else {
   237	            world.spawn((
   238	                Position {
   239	                    x: i as f32,
   240	                    y: 0.0,
   241	                },
   242	                Velocity { x: 1.0, y: 0.25 },
   243	                Health(100),
   244	                Simulated,
   245	            ));
   246	        }
   247	    }
   248	
   249	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   250	    runtime.add_systems::<W2, _, _>(
   251	        &mut world,
   252	        (w2_move, w2_mutate_health, w2_scan_changed, w2_scan_added),
   253	    );
   254	    (world, runtime)
   255	}
   256	
   257	fn workload_w2(c: &mut Criterion) {
   258	    let mut group = c.benchmark_group("w2_gameplay_mixed");
   259	    for &size in &[5_000_usize, 20_000] {
   260	        let (mut world, mut runtime) = build_runtime_for_w2(size);
   261	        group.bench_with_input(BenchmarkId::new("entities", size), &size, |b, _| {
   262	            b.iter(|| {
   263	                runtime
   264	                    .run_schedule::<W2>(&mut world)
   265	                    .expect("w2 schedule should run");
   266	                black_box(world.resource::<MixedStats>().expect("stats resource").0)
   267	            });
   268	        });
   269	    }
   270	    group.finish();
   271	}
   272	
   273	fn w3_spawn(mut commands: Commands) {
   274	    for i in 0..128_u32 {
   275	        commands.spawn((
   276	            ChurnTag,
   277	            Position {
   278	                x: i as f32,
   279	                y: i as f32,
   280	            },
   281	            Velocity { x: 0.1, y: -0.1 },
   282	        ));
   283	    }
   284	}
   285	
   286	fn w3_despawn(mut commands: Commands, mut query: Query<(Entity, &ChurnTag)>) {
   287	    for (idx, (entity, _)) in query.iter().enumerate() {
   288	        if idx >= 128 {
   289	            break;
   290	        }
   291	        commands.despawn(entity);
   292	    }
   293	}
   294	
   295	fn build_runtime_for_w3(entity_count: usize) -> (World, Runtime) {
   296	    let mut world = World::new();
   297	    for i in 0..entity_count {
   298	        world.spawn((
   299	            ChurnTag,
   300	            Position {
   301	                x: i as f32,
   302	                y: 0.0,
   303	            },
   304	            Velocity { x: 0.0, y: 0.0 },
   305	        ));
   306	    }
   307	
   308	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   309	    runtime.add_systems::<W3, _, _>(&mut world, (w3_spawn, w3_despawn));
   310	    (world, runtime)
   311	}
   312	
   313	fn workload_w3(c: &mut Criterion) {
   314	    let mut group = c.benchmark_group("w3_structural_churn");
   315	    let (mut world, mut runtime) = build_runtime_for_w3(20_000);
   316	    group.bench_function("spawn_insert_remove_despawn_commands", |b| {
   317	        b.iter(|| {
   318	            runtime
   319	                .run_schedule::<W3>(&mut world)
   320	                .expect("w3 schedule should run");
   321	            black_box(world.current_change_tick())
   322	        });
   323	    });
   324	    group.finish();
   325	}
   326	
   327	fn w4_write_events(mut writer: EventWriter<BenchEvent>) {
   328	    for i in 0..256_u32 {
   329	        writer.send(BenchEvent(i));
   330	    }
   331	}
   332	
   333	fn w4_read_events(
   334	    reader: EventReader<BenchEvent>,
   335	    mut query: Query<&Position>,
   336	    mut stats: ResMut<EventStats>,
   337	) {
   338	    let events_seen = reader
   339	        .iter()
   340	        .fold(0_u64, |acc, event| acc.wrapping_add(event.0 as u64));
   341	    let entities_seen = query.iter().count() as u64;
   342	    (*stats).0 = (*stats)
   343	        .0
   344	        .wrapping_add(events_seen)
   345	        .wrapping_add(entities_seen);
   346	}
   347	
   348	fn build_runtime_for_w4(entity_count: usize) -> (World, Runtime) {
   349	    let mut world = World::new();
   350	    world.insert_resource(EventStats::default());
   351	    for i in 0..entity_count {
   352	        world.spawn((
   353	            Position {
   354	                x: i as f32,
   355	                y: i as f32,
   356	            },
   357	            Velocity { x: 0.0, y: 0.0 },
   358	        ));
   359	    }
   360	
   361	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   362	    runtime.add_systems::<W4, _, _>(&mut world, (w4_write_events, w4_read_events));
   363	    (world, runtime)
   364	}
   365	
   366	fn workload_w4(c: &mut Criterion) {
   367	    let mut group = c.benchmark_group("w4_event_heavy");
   368	    let (mut world, mut runtime) = build_runtime_for_w4(10_000);
   369	    group.bench_function("event_reader_writer_interleaved_query", |b| {
   370	        b.iter(|| {
   371	            runtime
   372	                .run_schedule::<W4>(&mut world)
   373	                .expect("w4 schedule should run");
   374	            world.clear_events::<BenchEvent>();
   375	            black_box(world.resource::<EventStats>().expect("event stats").0)
   376	        });
   377	    });
   378	    group.finish();
   379	}
   380	
   381	fn w5_write_r0(mut r0: ResMut<R0>) {
   382	    (*r0).0 = (*r0).0.wrapping_add(1);
   383	}
   384	
   385	fn w5_write_r1(mut r1: ResMut<R1>) {
   386	    (*r1).0 = (*r1).0.wrapping_add(1);
   387	}
   388	
   389	fn w5_write_r2(mut r2: ResMut<R2>) {
   390	    (*r2).0 = (*r2).0.wrapping_add(1);
   391	}
   392	
   393	fn w5_write_r3(mut r3: ResMut<R3>) {
   394	    (*r3).0 = (*r3).0.wrapping_add(1);
   395	}
   396	
   397	fn w5_read_mix(r0: Res<R0>, r1: Res<R1>, r2: Res<R2>, mut sink: ResMut<Sink>) {
   398	    (*sink).0 = (*sink)
   399	        .0
   400	        .wrapping_add((*r0).0)
   401	        .wrapping_add((*r1).0)
   402	        .wrapping_add((*r2).0);
   403	}
   404	
   405	fn w5_read_mix_alt(r1: Res<R1>, r3: Res<R3>, mut sink: ResMut<Sink>) {
   406	    (*sink).0 = (*sink).0.wrapping_add((*r1).0).wrapping_add((*r3).0);
   407	}
   408	
   409	fn register_w5_systems(runtime: &mut Runtime, world: &mut World, repeats: usize) {
   410	    for _ in 0..repeats {
   411	        runtime.add_systems::<W5, _, _>(
   412	            world,
   413	            (
   414	                w5_write_r0.in_set(SetA),
   415	                w5_write_r1.in_set(SetA),
   416	                w5_read_mix.after(SetA).in_set(SetB),
   417	                w5_write_r2.after(SetB).in_set(SetC),
   418	                w5_read_mix_alt.after(SetC),
   419	                w5_write_r3.in_set(SetA),
   420	            ),
   421	        );
   422	    }
   423	}
   424	
   425	fn build_runtime_for_w5(repeats: usize) -> (World, Runtime) {
   426	    let mut world = World::new();
   427	    world.insert_resource(R0::default());
   428	    world.insert_resource(R1::default());
   429	    world.insert_resource(R2::default());
   430	    world.insert_resource(R3::default());
   431	    world.insert_resource(Sink::default());
   432	
   433	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   434	    register_w5_systems(&mut runtime, &mut world, repeats);
   435	    (world, runtime)
   436	}
   437	
   438	fn workload_w5(c: &mut Criterion) {
   439	    let mut group = c.benchmark_group("w5_scheduler_stress");
   440	
   441	    group.bench_function("scheduler_plan_build_96_systems", |b| {
   442	        b.iter(|| {
   443	            let (world, mut runtime) = build_runtime_for_w5(16);
   444	            let plan = runtime.plan_for::<W5>().map(|plan| plan.stages.len());
   445	            black_box(plan);
   446	            black_box(world.resource::<Sink>().expect("sink resource").0)
   447	        });
   448	    });
   449	
   450	    let (mut world, mut runtime) = build_runtime_for_w5(16);
   451	    group.bench_function("scheduler_stage_execution_96_systems", |b| {
   452	        b.iter(|| {
   453	            runtime
   454	                .run_schedule::<W5>(&mut world)
   455	                .expect("w5 schedule should run");
   456	            black_box(world.resource::<Sink>().expect("sink resource").0)
   457	        });
   458	    });
   459	
   460	    group.finish();
   461	}
   462	
   463	fn phase4_benches(c: &mut Criterion) {
   464	    workload_w1(c);
   465	    workload_c2_broad_read(c);
   466	    workload_c3_broad_write(c);
   467	    workload_w2(c);
   468	    workload_w3(c);
   469	    workload_w4(c);
   470	    workload_w5(c);
   471	}
   472	
   473	criterion_group!(phase4, phase4_benches);
   474	criterion_main!(phase4);

===== END FILE: ./benches/phase4.rs =====

   106	fn build_world_for_w1(entity_count: usize) -> World {

   117	    world
   118	}

   281	fn workload_w2(c: &mut Criterion) {

   289	                    .expect("w2 schedule should run");
   290	                black_box(world.resource::<MixedStats>().expect("stats resource").0)
   291	            });
   292	        });
   293	    }
   294	    group.finish();
   295	}

   298	    for i in 0..128_u32 {
   299	        commands.spawn((
   300	            ChurnTag,
   301	            Position {
   302	                x: i as f32,
   303	                y: i as f32,
   304	            },
   305	            Velocity { x: 0.1, y: -0.1 },
   306	        ));
   307	    }
   308	}

   310	fn w3_despawn(mut commands: Commands, mut query: Query<(Entity, &ChurnTag)>) {
   311	    for (idx, (entity, _)) in query.iter().enumerate() {
   312	        if idx >= 128 {
   313	            break;
   314	        }
   315	        commands.despawn(entity);
   316	    }
   317	}

   319	fn build_runtime_for_w3(entity_count: usize) -> (World, Runtime) {
   320	    let mut world = World::new();
   321	    for i in 0..entity_count {
   322	        world.spawn((
   323	            ChurnTag,
   324	            Position {
   325	                x: i as f32,
   326	                y: 0.0,
   327	            },
   328	            Velocity { x: 0.0, y: 0.0 },
   329	        ));
   330	    }
   331	
   332	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   333	    runtime.add_systems::<W3, _, _>(&mut world, (w3_spawn, w3_despawn));
   334	    (world, runtime)
   335	}

   337	fn workload_w3(c: &mut Criterion) {
   338	    let mut group = c.benchmark_group("w3_structural_churn");
   339	    let (mut world, mut runtime) = build_runtime_for_w3(20_000);
   340	    group.bench_function("spawn_insert_remove_despawn_commands", |b| {
   341	        b.iter(|| {
   342	            runtime
   343	                .run_schedule::<W3>(&mut world)
   344	                .expect("w3 schedule should run");
   345	            black_box(world.current_change_tick())
   346	        });
   347	    });
   348	    group.finish();
   349	}

   351	fn w4_write_events(mut writer: EventWriter<BenchEvent>) {
   352	    for i in 0..256_u32 {
   353	        writer.send(BenchEvent(i));
   354	    }
   355	}
   356	
   357	fn w4_read_events(
   358	    reader: EventReader<BenchEvent>,
   359	    mut query: Query<&Position>,
   360	    mut stats: ResMut<EventStats>,
   361	) {
   362	    let events_seen = reader
   363	        .iter()
   364	        .fold(0_u64, |acc, event| acc.wrapping_add(event.0 as u64));
   365	    let entities_seen = query.iter().count() as u64;
   366	    (*stats).0 = (*stats)
   367	        .0
   368	        .wrapping_add(events_seen)
   369	        .wrapping_add(entities_seen);
   370	}
   371	
   372	fn build_runtime_for_w4(entity_count: usize) -> (World, Runtime) {
   373	    let mut world = World::new();
   374	    world.insert_resource(EventStats::default());
   375	    for i in 0..entity_count {
   376	        world.spawn((
   377	            Position {
   378	                x: i as f32,
   379	                y: i as f32,
   380	            },
   381	            Velocity { x: 0.0, y: 0.0 },
   382	        ));
   383	    }
   384	
   385	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   386	    runtime.add_systems::<W4, _, _>(&mut world, (w4_write_events, w4_read_events));
   387	    (world, runtime)
   388	}
   389	
   390	fn workload_w4(c: &mut Criterion) {
   391	    let mut group = c.benchmark_group("w4_event_heavy");
   392	    let (mut world, mut runtime) = build_runtime_for_w4(10_000);
   393	    group.bench_function("event_reader_writer_interleaved_query", |b| {
   394	        b.iter(|| {
   395	            runtime
   396	                .run_schedule::<W4>(&mut world)
   397	                .expect("w4 schedule should run");
   398	            world.clear_events::<BenchEvent>();
   399	            black_box(world.resource::<EventStats>().expect("event stats").0)
   400	        });
   401	    });
   402	    group.finish();
   403	}
   404	
   405	fn w5_write_r0(mut r0: ResMut<R0>) {
   406	    (*r0).0 = (*r0).0.wrapping_add(1);
   407	}
   408	
   409	fn w5_write_r1(mut r1: ResMut<R1>) {
   410	    (*r1).0 = (*r1).0.wrapping_add(1);
   411	}
   412	
   413	fn w5_write_r2(mut r2: ResMut<R2>) {
   414	    (*r2).0 = (*r2).0.wrapping_add(1);
   415	}
   416	
   417	fn w5_write_r3(mut r3: ResMut<R3>) {
   418	    (*r3).0 = (*r3).0.wrapping_add(1);
   419	}
   420	
   421	fn w5_read_mix(r0: Res<R0>, r1: Res<R1>, r2: Res<R2>, mut sink: ResMut<Sink>) {
   422	    (*sink).0 = (*sink)
   423	        .0
   424	        .wrapping_add((*r0).0)
   425	        .wrapping_add((*r1).0)
   426	        .wrapping_add((*r2).0);
   427	}
   428	
   429	fn w5_read_mix_alt(r1: Res<R1>, r3: Res<R3>, mut sink: ResMut<Sink>) {
   430	    (*sink).0 = (*sink).0.wrapping_add((*r1).0).wrapping_add((*r3).0);
   431	}
   432	
   433	fn register_w5_systems(runtime: &mut Runtime, world: &mut World, repeats: usize) {
   434	    for _ in 0..repeats {
   435	        runtime.add_systems::<W5, _, _>(
   436	            world,
   437	            (
   438	                w5_write_r0.in_set(SetA),
   439	                w5_write_r1.in_set(SetA),
   440	                w5_read_mix.after(SetA).in_set(SetB),
   441	                w5_write_r2.after(SetB).in_set(SetC),
   442	                w5_read_mix_alt.after(SetC),
   443	                w5_write_r3.in_set(SetA),
   444	            ),
   445	        );
   446	    }
   447	}
   448	
   449	fn build_runtime_for_w5(repeats: usize) -> (World, Runtime) {
   450	    let mut world = World::new();
   451	    world.insert_resource(R0::default());
   452	    world.insert_resource(R1::default());
   453	    world.insert_resource(R2::default());
   454	    world.insert_resource(R3::default());
   455	    world.insert_resource(Sink::default());
   456	
   457	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   458	    register_w5_systems(&mut runtime, &mut world, repeats);
   459	    (world, runtime)
   460	}
   461	
   462	fn workload_w5(c: &mut Criterion) {
   463	    let mut group = c.benchmark_group("w5_scheduler_stress");
   464	
   465	    group.bench_function("scheduler_plan_build_96_systems", |b| {
   466	        b.iter(|| {
   467	            let (world, mut runtime) = build_runtime_for_w5(16);
   468	            let plan = runtime.plan_for::<W5>().map(|plan| plan.stages.len());
   469	            black_box(plan);
   470	            black_box(world.resource::<Sink>().expect("sink resource").0)
   471	        });
   472	    });
   473	
   474	    let (mut world, mut runtime) = build_runtime_for_w5(16);
   475	    group.bench_function("scheduler_stage_execution_96_systems", |b| {
   476	        b.iter(|| {
   477	            runtime
   478	                .run_schedule::<W5>(&mut world)
   479	                .expect("w5 schedule should run");
   480	            black_box(world.resource::<Sink>().expect("sink resource").0)
   481	        });
   482	    });
   483	
   484	    group.finish();
   485	}
   486	
   487	fn phase5b_benches(c: &mut Criterion) {
   488	    workload_w1(c);
   489	    workload_c2_broad_read(c);
   490	    workload_c3_broad_write(c);
   491	    workload_c4_broad_double_mut(c);
   492	    workload_w2(c);
   493	    workload_w3(c);
   494	    workload_w4(c);
   495	    workload_w5(c);
   496	}
   497	
   498	criterion_group!(phase5b, phase5b_benches);
   499	criterion_main!(phase5b);

   106	fn build_world_for_w1(entity_count: usize) -> World {
   107	    let mut world = World::new();
   108	    for i in 0..entity_count {
   109	        world.spawn((
   110	            Position {
   111	                x: i as f32,
   112	                y: (i as f32) * 0.5,
   113	            },
   114	            Velocity { x: 1.0, y: -0.5 },
   115	        ));
   116	    }
   117	    world
   118	}

   120	fn workload_w1(c: &mut Criterion) {
   121	    let mut group = c.benchmark_group("w1_broad_transform_update");
   122	    for &size in &[10_000_usize, 50_000, 200_000] {
   123	        let mut world = build_world_for_w1(size);
   124	        let query = world.query_state::<(&mut Position, &Velocity), ()>();
   125	        group.bench_with_input(BenchmarkId::new("entities", size), &size, |b, _| {
   126	            b.iter(|| {
   127	                let mut checksum = 0.0_f32;
   128	                for _ in 0..4 {
   129	                    for (position, velocity) in query.iter(&mut world) {
   130	                        position.x += velocity.x;
   131	                        position.y += velocity.y;
   132	                        checksum += position.x + position.y;
   133	                    }
   134	                }
   135	                black_box(checksum)
   136	            });
   137	        });
   138	    }
   139	    group.finish();
   140	}

   186	    for &size in &[10_000_usize, 50_000, 200_000] {
   187	        let mut world = build_world_for_w1(size);
   188	        let query = world.query_state::<(&mut Position, &mut Velocity), ()>();
   189	        group.bench_with_input(BenchmarkId::new("entities", size), &size, |b, _| {
   190	            b.iter(|| {
   191	                let mut checksum = 0.0_f32;
   192	                for _ in 0..4 {
   193	                    for (position, velocity) in query.iter(&mut world) {
   194	                        velocity.x += 0.01;
   195	                        velocity.y -= 0.01;
   196	                        position.x += velocity.x;
   197	                        position.y += velocity.y;
   198	                        checksum += position.x + position.y + velocity.x + velocity.y;
   199	                    }
   200	                }
   201	                black_box(checksum)
   202	            });
   203	        });
   204	    }
   205	    group.finish();

   208	fn w2_move(mut query: Query<(&mut Position, &Velocity), (With<Simulated>, Without<Disabled>)>) {
   209	    for (position, velocity) in query.iter() {
   210	        position.x += velocity.x;
   211	        position.y += velocity.y;
   212	    }
   213	}

   215	fn w2_mutate_health(mut query: Query<&mut Health, With<Simulated>>) {
   216	    for health in query.iter() {
   217	        health.0 = health.0.saturating_sub(1);
   218	    }
   219	}
   220	
   221	fn w2_scan_changed(
   222	    mut query: Query<(Entity, &Health), Changed<Health>>,
   223	    mut stats: ResMut<MixedStats>,
   224	) {
   225	    let mut seen = 0_u64;
   226	    for _ in query.iter() {
   227	        seen = seen.saturating_add(1);
   228	    }
   229	    (*stats).0 = (*stats).0.wrapping_add(seen);
   230	}
   231	
   232	fn w2_scan_added(
   233	    mut query: Query<(Entity, &Health), Added<Health>>,
   234	    mut stats: ResMut<MixedStats>,
   235	) {
   236	    let mut seen = 0_u64;
   237	    for _ in query.iter() {
   238	        seen = seen.saturating_add(1);
   239	    }
   240	    (*stats).0 = (*stats).0.wrapping_add(seen);
   241	}

   243	fn build_runtime_for_w2(entity_count: usize) -> (World, Runtime) {
   244	    let mut world = World::new();
   245	    world.insert_resource(MixedStats::default());
   246	
   247	    for i in 0..entity_count {
   248	        let disabled = i % 8 == 0;
   249	        if disabled {
   250	            world.spawn((
   251	                Position {
   252	                    x: i as f32,
   253	                    y: 0.0,
   254	                },
   255	                Velocity { x: 1.0, y: 0.25 },
   256	                Health(100),
   257	                Simulated,
   258	                Disabled,
   259	            ));
   260	        } else {
   261	            world.spawn((
   262	                Position {
   263	                    x: i as f32,
   264	                    y: 0.0,
   265	                },
   266	                Velocity { x: 1.0, y: 0.25 },
   267	                Health(100),
   268	                Simulated,
   269	            ));
   270	        }
   271	    }
   272	
   273	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   274	    runtime.add_systems::<W2, _, _>(
   275	        &mut world,
   276	        (w2_move, w2_mutate_health, w2_scan_changed, w2_scan_added),
   277	    );
   278	    (world, runtime)
   279	}

   373	    let mut world = World::new();
   374	    world.insert_resource(EventStats::default());
   375	    for i in 0..entity_count {
   376	        world.spawn((
   377	            Position {
   378	                x: i as f32,
   379	                y: i as f32,
   380	            },
   381	            Velocity { x: 0.0, y: 0.0 },
   382	        ));
   383	    }
   384	
   385	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   386	    runtime.add_systems::<W4, _, _>(&mut world, (w4_write_events, w4_read_events));
   387	    (world, runtime)
   388	}
   389	
   390	fn workload_w4(c: &mut Criterion) {
   391	    let mut group = c.benchmark_group("w4_event_heavy");
   392	    let (mut world, mut runtime) = build_runtime_for_w4(10_000);
   393	    group.bench_function("event_reader_writer_interleaved_query", |b| {
   394	        b.iter(|| {
   395	            runtime
   396	                .run_schedule::<W4>(&mut world)
   397	                .expect("w4 schedule should run");
   398	            world.clear_events::<BenchEvent>();
   399	            black_box(world.resource::<EventStats>().expect("event stats").0)
   400	        });
   401	    });
   402	    group.finish();
   403	}
   404	
   405	fn w5_write_r0(mut r0: ResMut<R0>) {
   406	    (*r0).0 = (*r0).0.wrapping_add(1);
   407	}
   408	
   409	fn w5_write_r1(mut r1: ResMut<R1>) {
   410	    (*r1).0 = (*r1).0.wrapping_add(1);
   411	}
   412	
   413	fn w5_write_r2(mut r2: ResMut<R2>) {
   414	    (*r2).0 = (*r2).0.wrapping_add(1);
   415	}
   416	
   417	fn w5_write_r3(mut r3: ResMut<R3>) {
   418	    (*r3).0 = (*r3).0.wrapping_add(1);
   419	}
   420	
   421	fn w5_read_mix(r0: Res<R0>, r1: Res<R1>, r2: Res<R2>, mut sink: ResMut<Sink>) {
   422	    (*sink).0 = (*sink)
   423	        .0
   424	        .wrapping_add((*r0).0)
   425	        .wrapping_add((*r1).0)
   426	        .wrapping_add((*r2).0);
   427	}
   428	
   429	fn w5_read_mix_alt(r1: Res<R1>, r3: Res<R3>, mut sink: ResMut<Sink>) {
   430	    (*sink).0 = (*sink).0.wrapping_add((*r1).0).wrapping_add((*r3).0);
   431	}
   432	
   433	fn register_w5_systems(runtime: &mut Runtime, world: &mut World, repeats: usize) {
   434	    for _ in 0..repeats {
   435	        runtime.add_systems::<W5, _, _>(
   436	            world,
   437	            (
   438	                w5_write_r0.in_set(SetA),
   439	                w5_write_r1.in_set(SetA),
   440	                w5_read_mix.after(SetA).in_set(SetB),
   441	                w5_write_r2.after(SetB).in_set(SetC),
   442	                w5_read_mix_alt.after(SetC),
   443	                w5_write_r3.in_set(SetA),
   444	            ),
   445	        );
   446	    }
   447	}
   448	
   449	fn build_runtime_for_w5(repeats: usize) -> (World, Runtime) {
   450	    let mut world = World::new();
   451	    world.insert_resource(R0::default());
   452	    world.insert_resource(R1::default());
   453	    world.insert_resource(R2::default());
   454	    world.insert_resource(R3::default());
   455	    world.insert_resource(Sink::default());
   456	
   457	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   458	    register_w5_systems(&mut runtime, &mut world, repeats);
   459	    (world, runtime)
   460	}
   461	
   462	fn workload_w5(c: &mut Criterion) {
   463	    let mut group = c.benchmark_group("w5_scheduler_stress");
   464	
   465	    group.bench_function("scheduler_plan_build_96_systems", |b| {
   466	        b.iter(|| {
   467	            let (world, mut runtime) = build_runtime_for_w5(16);
   468	            let plan = runtime.plan_for::<W5>().map(|plan| plan.stages.len());
   469	            black_box(plan);
   470	            black_box(world.resource::<Sink>().expect("sink resource").0)
   471	        });
   472	    });
   473	
   474	    let (mut world, mut runtime) = build_runtime_for_w5(16);
   475	    group.bench_function("scheduler_stage_execution_96_systems", |b| {
   476	        b.iter(|| {
   477	            runtime
   478	                .run_schedule::<W5>(&mut world)
   479	                .expect("w5 schedule should run");
   480	            black_box(world.resource::<Sink>().expect("sink resource").0)
   481	        });
   482	    });
   483	
   484	    group.finish();
   485	}
   486	
   487	fn phase6_benches(c: &mut Criterion) {
   488	    workload_w1(c);
   489	    workload_c2_broad_read(c);
   490	    workload_c3_broad_write(c);
   491	    workload_c4_broad_double_mut(c);
   492	    workload_w2(c);
   493	    workload_w3(c);
   494	    workload_w4(c);
   495	    workload_w5(c);
   496	}
   497	
   498	criterion_group!(phase6, phase6_benches);
   499	criterion_main!(phase6);

===== END FILE: ./benches/phase6.rs =====

   106	fn w2_move(mut query: Query<(&mut Position, &Velocity), (With<Simulated>, Without<Disabled>)>) {
   107	    for (position, velocity) in query.iter() {
   108	        position.x += velocity.x;
   109	        position.y += velocity.y;
   110	    }
   111	}
   112	
   113	fn w2_mutate_health(mut query: Query<&mut Health, With<Simulated>>) {
   114	    for health in query.iter() {
   115	        health.0 = health.0.saturating_sub(1);
   116	    }
   117	}
   118	
   119	fn w2_scan_changed(
   120	    mut query: Query<(Entity, &Health), Changed<Health>>,
   121	    mut stats: ResMut<MixedStats>,
   122	) {
   123	    let mut seen = 0_u64;
   124	    for _ in query.iter() {
   125	        seen = seen.saturating_add(1);
   126	    }
   127	    (*stats).0 = (*stats).0.wrapping_add(seen);
   128	}
   129	
   130	fn w2_scan_added(
   131	    mut query: Query<(Entity, &Health), Added<Health>>,
   132	    mut stats: ResMut<MixedStats>,
   133	) {
   134	    let mut seen = 0_u64;
   135	    for _ in query.iter() {
   136	        seen = seen.saturating_add(1);
   137	    }
   138	    (*stats).0 = (*stats).0.wrapping_add(seen);
   139	}
   140	
   141	fn w3_spawn(mut commands: Commands) {
   142	    for i in 0..128_u32 {
   143	        commands.spawn((
   144	            ChurnTag,
   145	            Position {
   146	                x: i as f32,
   147	                y: i as f32,
   148	            },
   149	            Velocity { x: 0.1, y: -0.1 },
   150	        ));
   151	    }
   152	}
   153	
   154	fn w3_despawn(mut commands: Commands, mut query: Query<(Entity, &ChurnTag)>) {
   155	    for (idx, (entity, _)) in query.iter().enumerate() {
   156	        if idx >= 128 {
   157	            break;
   158	        }
   159	        commands.despawn(entity);
   160	    }
   161	}
   162	
   163	fn w4_write_events(mut writer: EventWriter<BenchEvent>) {
   164	    for i in 0..256_u32 {
   165	        writer.send(BenchEvent(i));
   166	    }
   167	}
   168	
   169	fn w4_read_events(
   170	    reader: EventReader<BenchEvent>,
   171	    mut query: Query<&Position>,
   172	    mut stats: ResMut<EventStats>,
   173	) {
   174	    let events_seen = reader
   175	        .iter()
   176	        .fold(0_u64, |acc, event| acc.wrapping_add(event.0 as u64));
   177	    let entities_seen = query.iter().count() as u64;
   178	    (*stats).0 = (*stats)
   179	        .0
   180	        .wrapping_add(events_seen)
   181	        .wrapping_add(entities_seen);
   182	}
   183

   202	        .0
   203	        .wrapping_add((*r0).0)

   226	        query_matching_matches: after

   229	        query_iter_calls: after
   230	            .query_iter_calls

   232	        query_iter_nanos: after
   233	            .query_iter_nanos
   234	            .saturating_sub(before.query_iter_nanos),
   235	        query_get_calls: after.query_get_calls.saturating_sub(before.query_get_calls),
   236	        query_get_nanos: after.query_get_nanos.saturating_sub(before.query_get_nanos),
   237	        query_single_calls: after
   238	            .query_single_calls
   239	            .saturating_sub(before.query_single_calls),
   240	        query_single_nanos: after
   241	            .query_single_nanos
   242	            .saturating_sub(before.query_single_nanos),
   243	        changed_check_calls: after
   244	            .changed_check_calls
   245	            .saturating_sub(before.changed_check_calls),
   246	        changed_check_nanos: after
   247	            .changed_check_nanos
   248	            .saturating_sub(before.changed_check_nanos),
   249	        added_check_calls: after
   250	            .added_check_calls

   252	        added_check_nanos: after
   253	            .added_check_nanos
   254	            .saturating_sub(before.added_check_nanos),
   255	        runtime_plan_calls: after
   256	            .runtime_plan_calls
   257	            .saturating_sub(before.runtime_plan_calls),
   258	        runtime_plan_nanos: after
   259	            .runtime_plan_nanos

   279	        event_reader_nanos: after
   280	            .event_reader_nanos

   282	        events_read: after.events_read.saturating_sub(before.events_read),
   283	        event_writer_calls: after

   289	        events_written: after.events_written.saturating_sub(before.events_written),

   311	fn print_workload_report(name: &str, elapsed: std::time::Duration, delta: &EcsTelemetrySnapshot) {
   312	    println!("\n=== {} ===", name);
   313	    println!("wall_time_ms: {:.3}", elapsed.as_secs_f64() * 1000.0);
   314	    println!("telemetry: {:#?}", delta);
   315	}

   317	fn main() {
   318	    telemetry::reset();
   319	
   320	    let before_w1 = telemetry::snapshot();
   321	    let start_w1 = Instant::now();
   322	    {
   323	        let mut world = World::new();
   324	        for i in 0..50_000 {
   325	            world.spawn((
   326	                Position {
   327	                    x: i as f32,
   328	                    y: 0.0,
   329	                },
   330	                Velocity { x: 1.0, y: -0.25 },
   331	            ));
   332	        }
   333	        let query = world.query_state::<(&mut Position, &Velocity), ()>();
   334	        for _ in 0..8 {
   335	            for (position, velocity) in query.iter(&mut world) {
   336	                position.x += velocity.x;
   337	                position.y += velocity.y;
   338	            }
   339	        }
   340	    }
   341	    let after_w1 = telemetry::snapshot();
   342	    print_workload_report(
   343	        "W1 broad transform update",
   344	        start_w1.elapsed(),
   345	        &snapshot_delta(&before_w1, &after_w1),
   346	    );
   347	
   348	    let before_w2 = telemetry::snapshot();
   349	    let start_w2 = Instant::now();
   350	    {
   351	        let mut world = World::new();
   352	        world.insert_resource(MixedStats::default());
   353	        for i in 0..20_000 {
   354	            if i % 8 == 0 {
   355	                world.spawn((
   356	                    Position {
   357	                        x: i as f32,
   358	                        y: 0.0,
   359	                    },
   360	                    Velocity { x: 1.0, y: 0.25 },
   361	                    Health(100),
   362	                    Simulated,
   363	                    Disabled,
   364	                ));
   365	            } else {
   366	                world.spawn((
   367	                    Position {
   368	                        x: i as f32,
   369	                        y: 0.0,
   370	                    },
   371	                    Velocity { x: 1.0, y: 0.25 },
   372	                    Health(100),
   373	                    Simulated,
   374	                ));
   375	            }
   376	        }
   377	        let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   378	        runtime.add_systems::<W2, _, _>(
   379	            &mut world,
   380	            (w2_move, w2_mutate_health, w2_scan_changed, w2_scan_added),
   381	        );
   382	        for _ in 0..20 {
   383	            runtime.run_schedule::<W2>(&mut world).expect("w2 run");
   384	        }
   385	    }
   386	    let after_w2 = telemetry::snapshot();
   387	    print_workload_report(
   388	        "W2 gameplay mixed",
   389	        start_w2.elapsed(),
   390	        &snapshot_delta(&before_w2, &after_w2),
   391	    );
   392	
   393	    let before_w3 = telemetry::snapshot();
   394	    let start_w3 = Instant::now();
   395	    {
   396	        let mut world = World::new();
   397	        for i in 0..20_000 {
   398	            world.spawn((
   399	                ChurnTag,
   400	                Position {
   401	                    x: i as f32,
   402	                    y: 0.0,
   403	                },
   404	                Velocity { x: 0.0, y: 0.0 },
   405	            ));
   406	        }
   407	        let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   408	        runtime.add_systems::<W3, _, _>(&mut world, (w3_spawn, w3_despawn));
   409	        for _ in 0..20 {
   410	            runtime.run_schedule::<W3>(&mut world).expect("w3 run");
   411	        }
   412	    }
   413	    let after_w3 = telemetry::snapshot();
   414	    print_workload_report(
   415	        "W3 structural churn",
   416	        start_w3.elapsed(),
   417	        &snapshot_delta(&before_w3, &after_w3),
   418	    );
   419	
   420	    let before_w4 = telemetry::snapshot();
   421	    let start_w4 = Instant::now();
   422	    {
   423	        let mut world = World::new();
   424	        world.insert_resource(EventStats::default());
   425	        for i in 0..10_000 {
   426	            world.spawn((
   427	                Position {
   428	                    x: i as f32,
   429	                    y: i as f32,
   430	                },
   431	                Velocity { x: 0.0, y: 0.0 },
   432	            ));
   433	        }
   434	        let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   435	        runtime.add_systems::<W4, _, _>(&mut world, (w4_write_events, w4_read_events));
   436	        for _ in 0..20 {
   437	            runtime.run_schedule::<W4>(&mut world).expect("w4 run");
   438	            world.clear_events::<BenchEvent>();
   439	        }
   440	    }
   441	    let after_w4 = telemetry::snapshot();
   442	    print_workload_report(
   443	        "W4 event heavy",
   444	        start_w4.elapsed(),
   445	        &snapshot_delta(&before_w4, &after_w4),
   446	    );
   447	
   448	    let before_w5 = telemetry::snapshot();
   449	    let start_w5 = Instant::now();
   450	    {
   451	        let mut world = World::new();
   452	        world.insert_resource(R0::default());
   453	        world.insert_resource(R1::default());
   454	        world.insert_resource(R2::default());
   455	        world.insert_resource(R3::default());
   456	        world.insert_resource(Sink::default());
   457	
   458	        let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   459	        for _ in 0..16 {
   460	            runtime.add_systems::<W5, _, _>(
   461	                &mut world,
   462	                (
   463	                    w5_write_r0.in_set(SetA),
   464	                    w5_write_r1.in_set(SetA),
   465	                    w5_read_mix.after(SetA).in_set(SetB),
   466	                    w5_write_r2.after(SetB).in_set(SetC),
   467	                    w5_read_mix_alt.after(SetC),
   468	                    w5_write_r3.in_set(SetA),
   469	                ),
   470	            );
   471	        }
   472	
   473	        for _ in 0..40 {
   474	            runtime.run_schedule::<W5>(&mut world).expect("w5 run");
   475	        }
   476	    }
   477	    let after_w5 = telemetry::snapshot();
   478	    print_workload_report(
   479	        "W5 scheduler stress",
   480	        start_w5.elapsed(),
   481	        &snapshot_delta(&before_w5, &after_w5),
   482	    );
   483	
   484	    println!("\n=== cumulative snapshot ===");
   485	    println!("{:#?}", telemetry::snapshot());
   486	}

   106	fn w2_move(mut query: Query<(&mut Position, &Velocity), (With<Simulated>, Without<Disabled>)>) {
   107	    for (position, velocity) in query.iter() {
   108	        position.x += velocity.x;
   109	        position.y += velocity.y;
   110	    }
   111	}
   112	
   113	fn w2_mutate_health(mut query: Query<&mut Health, With<Simulated>>) {
   114	    for health in query.iter() {
   115	        health.0 = health.0.saturating_sub(1);
   116	    }
   117	}
   118	
   119	fn w2_scan_changed(
   120	    mut query: Query<(Entity, &Health), Changed<Health>>,
   121	    mut stats: ResMut<MixedStats>,
   122	) {
   123	    let mut seen = 0_u64;
   124	    for _ in query.iter() {
   125	        seen = seen.saturating_add(1);
   126	    }
   127	    (*stats).0 = (*stats).0.wrapping_add(seen);
   128	}
   129	
   130	fn w2_scan_added(
   131	    mut query: Query<(Entity, &Health), Added<Health>>,
   132	    mut stats: ResMut<MixedStats>,
   133	) {
   134	    let mut seen = 0_u64;
   135	    for _ in query.iter() {
   136	        seen = seen.saturating_add(1);
   137	    }
   138	    (*stats).0 = (*stats).0.wrapping_add(seen);
   139	}
   140	
   141	fn w3_spawn(mut commands: Commands) {
   142	    for i in 0..128_u32 {
   143	        commands.spawn((
   144	            ChurnTag,
   145	            Position {
   146	                x: i as f32,
   147	                y: i as f32,
   148	            },
   149	            Velocity { x: 0.1, y: -0.1 },
   150	        ));
   151	    }
   152	}
   153	
   154	fn w3_despawn(mut commands: Commands, mut query: Query<(Entity, &ChurnTag)>) {
   155	    for (idx, (entity, _)) in query.iter().enumerate() {
   156	        if idx >= 128 {
   157	            break;
   158	        }
   159	        commands.despawn(entity);
   160	    }
   161	}
   162	
   163	fn w4_write_events(mut writer: EventWriter<BenchEvent>) {
   164	    for i in 0..256_u32 {
   165	        writer.send(BenchEvent(i));
   166	    }
   167	}
   168	
   169	fn w4_read_events(
   170	    reader: EventReader<BenchEvent>,
   171	    mut query: Query<&Position>,
   172	    mut stats: ResMut<EventStats>,
   173	) {
   174	    let events_seen = reader
   175	        .iter()
   176	        .fold(0_u64, |acc, event| acc.wrapping_add(event.0 as u64));
   177	    let entities_seen = query.iter().count() as u64;
   178	    (*stats).0 = (*stats)
   179	        .0
   180	        .wrapping_add(events_seen)
   181	        .wrapping_add(entities_seen);
   182	}
   183	
   184	fn w5_write_r0(mut r0: ResMut<R0>) {
   185	    (*r0).0 = (*r0).0.wrapping_add(1);
   186	}
   187	
   188	fn w5_write_r1(mut r1: ResMut<R1>) {
   189	    (*r1).0 = (*r1).0.wrapping_add(1);
   190	}
   191	
   192	fn w5_write_r2(mut r2: ResMut<R2>) {
   193	    (*r2).0 = (*r2).0.wrapping_add(1);
   194	}
   195	
   196	fn w5_write_r3(mut r3: ResMut<R3>) {
   197	    (*r3).0 = (*r3).0.wrapping_add(1);
   198	}
   199	
   200	fn w5_read_mix(r0: Res<R0>, r1: Res<R1>, r2: Res<R2>, mut sink: ResMut<Sink>) {
   201	    (*sink).0 = (*sink)
   202	        .0
   203	        .wrapping_add((*r0).0)
   204	        .wrapping_add((*r1).0)
   205	        .wrapping_add((*r2).0);
   206	}
   207	
   208	fn w5_read_mix_alt(r1: Res<R1>, r3: Res<R3>, mut sink: ResMut<Sink>) {
   209	    (*sink).0 = (*sink).0.wrapping_add((*r1).0).wrapping_add((*r3).0);
   210	}

   212	fn snapshot_delta(
   213	    before: &EcsTelemetrySnapshot,
   214	    after: &EcsTelemetrySnapshot,
   215	) -> EcsTelemetrySnapshot {
   216	    EcsTelemetrySnapshot {
   217	        query_matching_calls: after
   218	            .query_matching_calls
   219	            .saturating_sub(before.query_matching_calls),
   220	        query_matching_nanos: after
   221	            .query_matching_nanos
   222	            .saturating_sub(before.query_matching_nanos),
   223	        query_matching_candidates: after
   224	            .query_matching_candidates
   225	            .saturating_sub(before.query_matching_candidates),
   226	        query_matching_matches: after
   227	            .query_matching_matches
   228	            .saturating_sub(before.query_matching_matches),
   229	        query_iter_calls: after
   230	            .query_iter_calls
   231	            .saturating_sub(before.query_iter_calls),
   232	        query_iter_nanos: after
   233	            .query_iter_nanos
   234	            .saturating_sub(before.query_iter_nanos),
   235	        query_get_calls: after.query_get_calls.saturating_sub(before.query_get_calls),
   236	        query_get_nanos: after.query_get_nanos.saturating_sub(before.query_get_nanos),
   237	        query_single_calls: after
   238	            .query_single_calls
   239	            .saturating_sub(before.query_single_calls),
   240	        query_single_nanos: after
   241	            .query_single_nanos
   242	            .saturating_sub(before.query_single_nanos),
   243	        changed_check_calls: after
   244	            .changed_check_calls
   245	            .saturating_sub(before.changed_check_calls),
   246	        changed_check_nanos: after
   247	            .changed_check_nanos

   249	        added_check_calls: after

   252	        added_check_nanos: after
   253	            .added_check_nanos
   254	            .saturating_sub(before.added_check_nanos),
   255	        runtime_plan_calls: after
   256	            .runtime_plan_calls
   257	            .saturating_sub(before.runtime_plan_calls),
   258	        runtime_plan_nanos: after
   259	            .runtime_plan_nanos
   260	            .saturating_sub(before.runtime_plan_nanos),
   261	        runtime_stage_calls: after

   264	        runtime_stage_nanos: after
   265	            .runtime_stage_nanos

   267	        runtime_flush_calls: after

   276	        event_reader_calls: after

   279	        event_reader_nanos: after
   280	            .event_reader_nanos

   282	        events_read: after.events_read.saturating_sub(before.events_read),
   283	        event_writer_calls: after
   284	            .event_writer_calls
   285	            .saturating_sub(before.event_writer_calls),
   286	        event_writer_nanos: after
   287	            .event_writer_nanos
   288	            .saturating_sub(before.event_writer_nanos),
   289	        events_written: after.events_written.saturating_sub(before.events_written),
   290	        scheduler: scheduler::telemetry::SchedulerTelemetrySnapshot {
   291	            plan_build_calls: after
   292	                .scheduler

   311	fn print_workload_report(name: &str, elapsed: std::time::Duration, delta: &EcsTelemetrySnapshot) {
   312	    println!("\n=== {} ===", name);
   313	    println!("wall_time_ms: {:.3}", elapsed.as_secs_f64() * 1000.0);
   314	    println!("telemetry: {:#?}", delta);
   315	}

   317	fn main() {
   318	    telemetry::reset();
   319	
   320	    let before_w1 = telemetry::snapshot();
   321	    let start_w1 = Instant::now();
   322	    {
   323	        let mut world = World::new();
   324	        for i in 0..50_000 {
   325	            world.spawn((
   326	                Position {
   327	                    x: i as f32,
   328	                    y: 0.0,
   329	                },
   330	                Velocity { x: 1.0, y: -0.25 },
   331	            ));
   332	        }
   333	        let query = world.query_state::<(&mut Position, &Velocity), ()>();
   334	        for _ in 0..8 {
   335	            for (position, velocity) in query.iter(&mut world) {
   336	                position.x += velocity.x;
   337	                position.y += velocity.y;
   338	            }
   339	        }
   340	    }
   341	    let after_w1 = telemetry::snapshot();
   342	    print_workload_report(
   343	        "W1 broad transform update",
   344	        start_w1.elapsed(),
   345	        &snapshot_delta(&before_w1, &after_w1),
   346	    );
   347	
   348	    let before_c2 = telemetry::snapshot();
   349	    let start_c2 = Instant::now();
   350	    {
   351	        let mut world = World::new();
   352	        for i in 0..50_000 {
   353	            world.spawn((
   354	                Position {
   355	                    x: i as f32,
   356	                    y: 0.0,
   357	                },
   358	                Velocity { x: 1.0, y: -0.25 },
   359	            ));
   360	        }
   361	        let query = world.query_state::<&Position, ()>();
   362	        let mut checksum = 0.0_f32;
   363	        for _ in 0..8 {
   364	            for position in query.iter(&world) {
   365	                checksum += position.x + position.y;
   366	            }
   367	        }
   368	        std::hint::black_box(checksum);
   369	    }
   370	    let after_c2 = telemetry::snapshot();
   371	    print_workload_report(
   372	        "C2 broad no-filter read query",
   373	        start_c2.elapsed(),
   374	        &snapshot_delta(&before_c2, &after_c2),
   375	    );
   376	
   377	    let before_c3 = telemetry::snapshot();
   378	    let start_c3 = Instant::now();
   379	    {
   380	        let mut world = World::new();
   381	        for i in 0..50_000 {
   382	            world.spawn((
   383	                Position {
   384	                    x: i as f32,
   385	                    y: 0.0,
   386	                },
   387	                Velocity { x: 1.0, y: -0.25 },
   388	            ));
   389	        }
   390	        let query = world.query_state::<&mut Velocity, ()>();
   391	        let mut checksum = 0.0_f32;
   392	        for _ in 0..8 {
   393	            for velocity in query.iter(&mut world) {
   394	                velocity.x += 0.01;
   395	                velocity.y -= 0.01;
   396	                checksum += velocity.x + velocity.y;
   397	            }
   398	        }
   399	        std::hint::black_box(checksum);
   400	    }
   401	    let after_c3 = telemetry::snapshot();
   402	    print_workload_report(
   403	        "C3 broad simple write query",
   404	        start_c3.elapsed(),
   405	        &snapshot_delta(&before_c3, &after_c3),
   406	    );
   407	
   408	    let before_w2 = telemetry::snapshot();
   409	    let start_w2 = Instant::now();
   410	    {
   411	        let mut world = World::new();
   412	        world.insert_resource(MixedStats::default());
   413	        for i in 0..20_000 {
   414	            if i % 8 == 0 {
   415	                world.spawn((
   416	                    Position {
   417	                        x: i as f32,
   418	                        y: 0.0,
   419	                    },
   420	                    Velocity { x: 1.0, y: 0.25 },
   421	                    Health(100),
   422	                    Simulated,
   423	                    Disabled,
   424	                ));
   425	            } else {
   426	                world.spawn((
   427	                    Position {
   428	                        x: i as f32,
   429	                        y: 0.0,
   430	                    },
   431	                    Velocity { x: 1.0, y: 0.25 },
   432	                    Health(100),
   433	                    Simulated,
   434	                ));
   435	            }
   436	        }
   437	        let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   438	        runtime.add_systems::<W2, _, _>(
   439	            &mut world,
   440	            (w2_move, w2_mutate_health, w2_scan_changed, w2_scan_added),
   441	        );
   442	        for _ in 0..20 {
   443	            runtime.run_schedule::<W2>(&mut world).expect("w2 run");
   444	        }
   445	    }
   446	    let after_w2 = telemetry::snapshot();
   447	    print_workload_report(
   448	        "W2 gameplay mixed",
   449	        start_w2.elapsed(),
   450	        &snapshot_delta(&before_w2, &after_w2),
   451	    );
   452	
   453	    let before_w3 = telemetry::snapshot();
   454	    let start_w3 = Instant::now();
   455	    {
   456	        let mut world = World::new();
   457	        for i in 0..20_000 {
   458	            world.spawn((
   459	                ChurnTag,
   460	                Position {
   461	                    x: i as f32,
   462	                    y: 0.0,
   463	                },
   464	                Velocity { x: 0.0, y: 0.0 },
   465	            ));
   466	        }
   467	        let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   468	        runtime.add_systems::<W3, _, _>(&mut world, (w3_spawn, w3_despawn));
   469	        for _ in 0..20 {
   470	            runtime.run_schedule::<W3>(&mut world).expect("w3 run");
   471	        }
   472	    }
   473	    let after_w3 = telemetry::snapshot();
   474	    print_workload_report(
   475	        "W3 structural churn",
   476	        start_w3.elapsed(),
   477	        &snapshot_delta(&before_w3, &after_w3),
   478	    );
   479	
   480	    let before_w4 = telemetry::snapshot();
   481	    let start_w4 = Instant::now();
   482	    {
   483	        let mut world = World::new();
   484	        world.insert_resource(EventStats::default());
   485	        for i in 0..10_000 {
   486	            world.spawn((
   487	                Position {
   488	                    x: i as f32,
   489	                    y: i as f32,
   490	                },
   491	                Velocity { x: 0.0, y: 0.0 },
   492	            ));
   493	        }
   494	        let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   495	        runtime.add_systems::<W4, _, _>(&mut world, (w4_write_events, w4_read_events));
   496	        for _ in 0..20 {
   497	            runtime.run_schedule::<W4>(&mut world).expect("w4 run");
   498	            world.clear_events::<BenchEvent>();
   499	        }
   500	    }
   501	    let after_w4 = telemetry::snapshot();
   502	    print_workload_report(
   503	        "W4 event heavy",
   504	        start_w4.elapsed(),
   505	        &snapshot_delta(&before_w4, &after_w4),
   506	    );
   507	
   508	    let before_w5 = telemetry::snapshot();
   509	    let start_w5 = Instant::now();
   510	    {
   511	        let mut world = World::new();
   512	        world.insert_resource(R0::default());
   513	        world.insert_resource(R1::default());
   514	        world.insert_resource(R2::default());
   515	        world.insert_resource(R3::default());
   516	        world.insert_resource(Sink::default());
   517	
   518	        let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   519	        for _ in 0..16 {
   520	            runtime.add_systems::<W5, _, _>(
   521	                &mut world,
   522	                (
   523	                    w5_write_r0.in_set(SetA),
   524	                    w5_write_r1.in_set(SetA),
   525	                    w5_read_mix.after(SetA).in_set(SetB),
   526	                    w5_write_r2.after(SetB).in_set(SetC),
   527	                    w5_read_mix_alt.after(SetC),
   528	                    w5_write_r3.in_set(SetA),
   529	                ),
   530	            );
   531	        }
   532	
   533	        for _ in 0..40 {
   534	            runtime.run_schedule::<W5>(&mut world).expect("w5 run");
   535	        }
   536	    }
   537	    let after_w5 = telemetry::snapshot();
   538	    print_workload_report(

     1	use ecs::prelude::*;
     2	use ecs::telemetry::{self, EcsTelemetrySnapshot};
     3	use scheduler::{ScheduleLabel, SystemSet};
     4	use std::time::Instant;
     5	
     6	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
     7	struct Position {
     8	    x: f32,
     9	    y: f32,

    52	impl ScheduleLabel for W2 {
    53	    fn name() -> &'static str {
    54	        "W2"
    55	    }
    56	}
