   106	fn w2_move(mut query: Query<(&mut Position, &Velocity), (With<Simulated>, Without<Disabled>)>) {
   107	    for (position, velocity) in query.iter() {
   108	        position.x += velocity.x;
   109	        position.y += velocity.y;
   110	    }
   111	}
   112	
   113	fn w2_mutate_health(mut query: Query<&mut Health, With<Simulated>>) {
   114	    for health in query.iter() {
   115	        health.0 = health.0.saturating_sub(1);
   116	    }
   117	}
   118	
   119	fn w2_scan_changed(
   120	    mut query: Query<(Entity, &Health), Changed<Health>>,
   121	    mut stats: ResMut<MixedStats>,
   122	) {
   123	    let mut seen = 0_u64;
   124	    for _ in query.iter() {
   125	        seen = seen.saturating_add(1);
   126	    }
   127	    (*stats).0 = (*stats).0.wrapping_add(seen);
   128	}
   129	
   130	fn w2_scan_added(
   131	    mut query: Query<(Entity, &Health), Added<Health>>,
   132	    mut stats: ResMut<MixedStats>,
   133	) {
   134	    let mut seen = 0_u64;
   135	    for _ in query.iter() {
   136	        seen = seen.saturating_add(1);
   137	    }
   138	    (*stats).0 = (*stats).0.wrapping_add(seen);
   139	}
   140	
   141	fn w3_spawn(mut commands: Commands) {
   142	    for i in 0..128_u32 {
   143	        commands.spawn((
   144	            ChurnTag,
   145	            Position {
   146	                x: i as f32,
   147	                y: i as f32,
   148	            },
   149	            Velocity { x: 0.1, y: -0.1 },
   150	        ));
   151	    }
   152	}
   153	
   154	fn w3_despawn(mut commands: Commands, mut query: Query<(Entity, &ChurnTag)>) {
   155	    for (idx, (entity, _)) in query.iter().enumerate() {
   156	        if idx >= 128 {
   157	            break;
   158	        }
   159	        commands.despawn(entity);
   160	    }
   161	}
   162	
   163	fn w4_write_events(mut writer: EventWriter<BenchEvent>) {
   164	    for i in 0..256_u32 {
   165	        writer.send(BenchEvent(i));
   166	    }
   167	}
   168	
   169	fn w4_read_events(
   170	    reader: EventReader<BenchEvent>,
   171	    mut query: Query<&Position>,
   172	    mut stats: ResMut<EventStats>,
   173	) {
   174	    let events_seen = reader
   175	        .iter()
   176	        .fold(0_u64, |acc, event| acc.wrapping_add(event.0 as u64));
   177	    let entities_seen = query.iter().count() as u64;
   178	    (*stats).0 = (*stats)
   179	        .0
   180	        .wrapping_add(events_seen)
   181	        .wrapping_add(entities_seen);
   182	}
   183	
   184	fn w5_write_r0(mut r0: ResMut<R0>) {
   185	    (*r0).0 = (*r0).0.wrapping_add(1);
   186	}
   187	
   188	fn w5_write_r1(mut r1: ResMut<R1>) {
   189	    (*r1).0 = (*r1).0.wrapping_add(1);
   190	}
   191	
   192	fn w5_write_r2(mut r2: ResMut<R2>) {
   193	    (*r2).0 = (*r2).0.wrapping_add(1);
   194	}
   195	
   196	fn w5_write_r3(mut r3: ResMut<R3>) {
   197	    (*r3).0 = (*r3).0.wrapping_add(1);
   198	}
   199	
   200	fn w5_read_mix(r0: Res<R0>, r1: Res<R1>, r2: Res<R2>, mut sink: ResMut<Sink>) {
   201	    (*sink).0 = (*sink)
   202	        .0
   203	        .wrapping_add((*r0).0)
   204	        .wrapping_add((*r1).0)
   205	        .wrapping_add((*r2).0);
   206	}
   207	
   208	fn w5_read_mix_alt(r1: Res<R1>, r3: Res<R3>, mut sink: ResMut<Sink>) {
   209	    (*sink).0 = (*sink).0.wrapping_add((*r1).0).wrapping_add((*r3).0);
   210	}
   211	
   212	fn snapshot_delta(
   213	    before: &EcsTelemetrySnapshot,
   214	    after: &EcsTelemetrySnapshot,
   215	) -> EcsTelemetrySnapshot {
   216	    EcsTelemetrySnapshot {
   217	        query_matching_calls: after
   218	            .query_matching_calls
   219	            .saturating_sub(before.query_matching_calls),
   220	        query_matching_nanos: after
   221	            .query_matching_nanos
   222	            .saturating_sub(before.query_matching_nanos),
   223	        query_matching_candidates: after
   224	            .query_matching_candidates
   225	            .saturating_sub(before.query_matching_candidates),
   226	        query_matching_matches: after
   227	            .query_matching_matches
   228	            .saturating_sub(before.query_matching_matches),
   229	        query_iter_calls: after
   230	            .query_iter_calls
   231	            .saturating_sub(before.query_iter_calls),
   232	        query_iter_nanos: after
   233	            .query_iter_nanos
   234	            .saturating_sub(before.query_iter_nanos),
   235	        query_get_calls: after.query_get_calls.saturating_sub(before.query_get_calls),
   236	        query_get_nanos: after.query_get_nanos.saturating_sub(before.query_get_nanos),
   237	        query_single_calls: after
   238	            .query_single_calls
   239	            .saturating_sub(before.query_single_calls),
   240	        query_single_nanos: after
   241	            .query_single_nanos
   242	            .saturating_sub(before.query_single_nanos),
   243	        changed_check_calls: after
   244	            .changed_check_calls
   245	            .saturating_sub(before.changed_check_calls),
   246	        changed_check_nanos: after
   247	            .changed_check_nanos
   248	            .saturating_sub(before.changed_check_nanos),
   249	        added_check_calls: after
   250	            .added_check_calls
   251	            .saturating_sub(before.added_check_calls),
   252	        added_check_nanos: after
   253	            .added_check_nanos
   254	            .saturating_sub(before.added_check_nanos),
   255	        runtime_plan_calls: after
   256	            .runtime_plan_calls
   257	            .saturating_sub(before.runtime_plan_calls),
   258	        runtime_plan_nanos: after
   259	            .runtime_plan_nanos
   260	            .saturating_sub(before.runtime_plan_nanos),
   261	        runtime_stage_calls: after
   262	            .runtime_stage_calls
   263	            .saturating_sub(before.runtime_stage_calls),
   264	        runtime_stage_nanos: after
   265	            .runtime_stage_nanos
   266	            .saturating_sub(before.runtime_stage_nanos),
   267	        runtime_flush_calls: after
   268	            .runtime_flush_calls
   269	            .saturating_sub(before.runtime_flush_calls),
   270	        runtime_flush_nanos: after
   271	            .runtime_flush_nanos
   272	            .saturating_sub(before.runtime_flush_nanos),
   273	        runtime_flush_command_queues: after
   274	            .runtime_flush_command_queues
   275	            .saturating_sub(before.runtime_flush_command_queues),
   276	        event_reader_calls: after
   277	            .event_reader_calls
   278	            .saturating_sub(before.event_reader_calls),
   279	        event_reader_nanos: after
   280	            .event_reader_nanos
   281	            .saturating_sub(before.event_reader_nanos),
   282	        events_read: after.events_read.saturating_sub(before.events_read),
   283	        event_writer_calls: after
   284	            .event_writer_calls
   285	            .saturating_sub(before.event_writer_calls),
   286	        event_writer_nanos: after
   287	            .event_writer_nanos
   288	            .saturating_sub(before.event_writer_nanos),
   289	        events_written: after.events_written.saturating_sub(before.events_written),
   290	        scheduler: scheduler::telemetry::SchedulerTelemetrySnapshot {
   291	            plan_build_calls: after
   292	                .scheduler
   293	                .plan_build_calls
   294	                .saturating_sub(before.scheduler.plan_build_calls),
   295	            plan_build_nanos: after
   296	                .scheduler
   297	                .plan_build_nanos
   298	                .saturating_sub(before.scheduler.plan_build_nanos),
   299	            plan_conflict_checks: after
   300	                .scheduler
   301	                .plan_conflict_checks
   302	                .saturating_sub(before.scheduler.plan_conflict_checks),
   303	            plan_stage_count: after
   304	                .scheduler
   305	                .plan_stage_count
   306	                .saturating_sub(before.scheduler.plan_stage_count),
   307	        },
   308	    }
   309	}
   310	
   311	fn print_workload_report(name: &str, elapsed: std::time::Duration, delta: &EcsTelemetrySnapshot) {
   312	    println!("\n=== {} ===", name);
   313	    println!("wall_time_ms: {:.3}", elapsed.as_secs_f64() * 1000.0);
   314	    println!("telemetry: {:#?}", delta);
   315	}
   316	
   317	fn main() {
   318	    telemetry::reset();
   319	
   320	    let before_w1 = telemetry::snapshot();
   321	    let start_w1 = Instant::now();
   322	    {
   323	        let mut world = World::new();
   324	        for i in 0..50_000 {
   325	            world.spawn((
   326	                Position {
   327	                    x: i as f32,
   328	                    y: 0.0,
   329	                },
   330	                Velocity { x: 1.0, y: -0.25 },
   331	            ));
   332	        }
   333	        let query = world.query_state::<(&mut Position, &Velocity), ()>();
   334	        for _ in 0..8 {
   335	            for (position, velocity) in query.iter(&mut world) {
   336	                position.x += velocity.x;
   337	                position.y += velocity.y;
   338	            }
   339	        }
   340	    }
   341	    let after_w1 = telemetry::snapshot();
   342	    print_workload_report(
   343	        "W1 broad transform update",
   344	        start_w1.elapsed(),
   345	        &snapshot_delta(&before_w1, &after_w1),
   346	    );
   347	
   348	    let before_c2 = telemetry::snapshot();
   349	    let start_c2 = Instant::now();
   350	    {
   351	        let mut world = World::new();
   352	        for i in 0..50_000 {
   353	            world.spawn((
   354	                Position {
   355	                    x: i as f32,
   356	                    y: 0.0,
   357	                },
   358	                Velocity { x: 1.0, y: -0.25 },
   359	            ));
   360	        }
   361	        let query = world.query_state::<&Position, ()>();
   362	        let mut checksum = 0.0_f32;
   363	        for _ in 0..8 {
   364	            for position in query.iter(&world) {
   365	                checksum += position.x + position.y;
   366	            }
   367	        }
   368	        std::hint::black_box(checksum);
   369	    }
   370	    let after_c2 = telemetry::snapshot();
   371	    print_workload_report(
   372	        "C2 broad no-filter read query",
   373	        start_c2.elapsed(),
   374	        &snapshot_delta(&before_c2, &after_c2),
   375	    );
   376	
   377	    let before_c3 = telemetry::snapshot();
   378	    let start_c3 = Instant::now();
   379	    {
   380	        let mut world = World::new();
   381	        for i in 0..50_000 {
   382	            world.spawn((
   383	                Position {
   384	                    x: i as f32,
   385	                    y: 0.0,
   386	                },
   387	                Velocity { x: 1.0, y: -0.25 },
   388	            ));
   389	        }
   390	        let query = world.query_state::<&mut Velocity, ()>();
   391	        let mut checksum = 0.0_f32;
   392	        for _ in 0..8 {
   393	            for velocity in query.iter(&mut world) {
   394	                velocity.x += 0.01;
   395	                velocity.y -= 0.01;
   396	                checksum += velocity.x + velocity.y;
   397	            }
   398	        }
   399	        std::hint::black_box(checksum);
   400	    }
   401	    let after_c3 = telemetry::snapshot();
   402	    print_workload_report(
   403	        "C3 broad simple write query",
   404	        start_c3.elapsed(),
   405	        &snapshot_delta(&before_c3, &after_c3),
   406	    );
   407	
   408	    let before_c4 = telemetry::snapshot();
   409	    let start_c4 = Instant::now();
   410	    {
   411	        let mut world = World::new();
   412	        for i in 0..50_000 {
   413	            world.spawn((
   414	                Position {
   415	                    x: i as f32,
   416	                    y: 0.0,
   417	                },
   418	                Velocity { x: 1.0, y: -0.25 },
   419	            ));
   420	        }
   421	        let query = world.query_state::<(&mut Position, &mut Velocity), ()>();
   422	        let mut checksum = 0.0_f32;
   423	        for _ in 0..8 {
   424	            for (position, velocity) in query.iter(&mut world) {
   425	                velocity.x += 0.01;
   426	                velocity.y -= 0.01;
   427	                position.x += velocity.x;
   428	                position.y += velocity.y;
   429	                checksum += position.x + position.y + velocity.x + velocity.y;
   430	            }
   431	        }
   432	        std::hint::black_box(checksum);
   433	    }
   434	    let after_c4 = telemetry::snapshot();
   435	    print_workload_report(
   436	        "C4 broad double mutable query",
   437	        start_c4.elapsed(),
   438	        &snapshot_delta(&before_c4, &after_c4),
   439	    );
   440	
   441	    let before_w2 = telemetry::snapshot();
   442	    let start_w2 = Instant::now();
   443	    {
   444	        let mut world = World::new();
   445	        world.insert_resource(MixedStats::default());
   446	        for i in 0..20_000 {
   447	            if i % 8 == 0 {
   448	                world.spawn((
   449	                    Position {
   450	                        x: i as f32,
   451	                        y: 0.0,
   452	                    },
   453	                    Velocity { x: 1.0, y: 0.25 },
   454	                    Health(100),
   455	                    Simulated,
   456	                    Disabled,
   457	                ));
   458	            } else {
   459	                world.spawn((
   460	                    Position {
   461	                        x: i as f32,
   462	                        y: 0.0,
   463	                    },
   464	                    Velocity { x: 1.0, y: 0.25 },
   465	                    Health(100),
   466	                    Simulated,
   467	                ));
   468	            }
   469	        }
   470	        let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   471	        runtime.add_systems::<W2, _, _>(
   472	            &mut world,
   473	            (w2_move, w2_mutate_health, w2_scan_changed, w2_scan_added),
   474	        );
   475	        for _ in 0..20 {
   476	            runtime.run_schedule::<W2>(&mut world).expect("w2 run");
   477	        }
   478	    }
   479	    let after_w2 = telemetry::snapshot();
   480	    print_workload_report(
   481	        "W2 gameplay mixed",
   482	        start_w2.elapsed(),
   483	        &snapshot_delta(&before_w2, &after_w2),
   484	    );
   485	
   486	    let before_w3 = telemetry::snapshot();
   487	    let start_w3 = Instant::now();
   488	    {
   489	        let mut world = World::new();
   490	        for i in 0..20_000 {
   491	            world.spawn((
   492	                ChurnTag,
   493	                Position {
   494	                    x: i as f32,
   495	                    y: 0.0,
   496	                },
   497	                Velocity { x: 0.0, y: 0.0 },
   498	            ));
   499	        }
   500	        let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   501	        runtime.add_systems::<W3, _, _>(&mut world, (w3_spawn, w3_despawn));
   502	        for _ in 0..20 {
   503	            runtime.run_schedule::<W3>(&mut world).expect("w3 run");
   504	        }
   505	    }
   506	    let after_w3 = telemetry::snapshot();
   507	    print_workload_report(
   508	        "W3 structural churn",
   509	        start_w3.elapsed(),
   510	        &snapshot_delta(&before_w3, &after_w3),
   511	    );
   512	
   513	    let before_w4 = telemetry::snapshot();
   514	    let start_w4 = Instant::now();
   515	    {
   516	        let mut world = World::new();
   517	        world.insert_resource(EventStats::default());
   518	        for i in 0..10_000 {
   519	            world.spawn((
   520	                Position {
   521	                    x: i as f32,
   522	                    y: i as f32,
   523	                },
   524	                Velocity { x: 0.0, y: 0.0 },
   525	            ));
   526	        }
   527	        let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   528	        runtime.add_systems::<W4, _, _>(&mut world, (w4_write_events, w4_read_events));
   529	        for _ in 0..20 {
   530	            runtime.run_schedule::<W4>(&mut world).expect("w4 run");
   531	            world.clear_events::<BenchEvent>();
   532	        }
   533	    }
   534	    let after_w4 = telemetry::snapshot();
   535	    print_workload_report(
   536	        "W4 event heavy",
   537	        start_w4.elapsed(),
   538	        &snapshot_delta(&before_w4, &after_w4),
   539	    );
   540	
   541	    let before_w5 = telemetry::snapshot();
   542	    let start_w5 = Instant::now();
   543	    {
   544	        let mut world = World::new();
   545	        world.insert_resource(R0::default());
   546	        world.insert_resource(R1::default());
   547	        world.insert_resource(R2::default());
   548	        world.insert_resource(R3::default());
   549	        world.insert_resource(Sink::default());
   550	
   551	        let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   552	        for _ in 0..16 {
   553	            runtime.add_systems::<W5, _, _>(
   554	                &mut world,
   555	                (
   556	                    w5_write_r0.in_set(SetA),
   557	                    w5_write_r1.in_set(SetA),
   558	                    w5_read_mix.after(SetA).in_set(SetB),
   559	                    w5_write_r2.after(SetB).in_set(SetC),
   560	                    w5_read_mix_alt.after(SetC),
   561	                    w5_write_r3.in_set(SetA),
   562	                ),
   563	            );
   564	        }
   565	
   566	        for _ in 0..40 {
   567	            runtime.run_schedule::<W5>(&mut world).expect("w5 run");
   568	        }
   569	    }
   570	    let after_w5 = telemetry::snapshot();
   571	    print_workload_report(
   572	        "W5 scheduler stress",
   573	        start_w5.elapsed(),
   574	        &snapshot_delta(&before_w5, &after_w5),
   575	    );
   576	
   577	    println!("\n=== cumulative snapshot ===");
   578	    println!("{:#?}", telemetry::snapshot());
   579	}

===== FILE: ./examples/phase6_profile.rs =====
     1	use ecs::prelude::*;
     2	use ecs::telemetry::{self, EcsTelemetrySnapshot};
     3	use scheduler::{ScheduleLabel, SystemSet};
     4	use std::time::{Duration, Instant};
     5	
     6	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
     7	struct Position {
     8	    x: f32,
     9	    y: f32,
    10	}
    11	
    12	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
    13	struct Velocity {
    14	    x: f32,
    15	    y: f32,
    16	}
    17	
    18	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
    19	struct Simulated;
    20	
    21	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
    22	struct Disabled;
    23

   106	#[derive(Copy, Clone)]
   107	struct WorkloadMeta {
   108	    entity_count: usize,
   109	    repetition_count: u32,
   110	    schedule_run_count: u32,
   111	}
   112	
   113	fn nanos_to_ms(nanos: u64) -> f64 {
   114	    nanos as f64 / 1_000_000.0
   115	}
   116	
   117	fn print_workload_report(
   118	    name: &str,
   119	    setup_elapsed: Duration,
   120	    run_elapsed: Duration,
   121	    meta: WorkloadMeta,
   122	    delta: &EcsTelemetrySnapshot,
   123	) {
   124	    let query_total_ms = nanos_to_ms(
   125	        delta
   126	            .query_matching_nanos
   127	            .saturating_add(delta.query_iter_nanos)
   128	            .saturating_add(delta.query_get_nanos)
   129	            .saturating_add(delta.query_single_nanos),
   130	    );
   131	    let filter_total_ms = nanos_to_ms(
   132	        delta
   133	            .changed_check_nanos
   134	            .saturating_add(delta.added_check_nanos),
   135	    );
   136	    let runtime_total_ms = nanos_to_ms(
   137	        delta
   138	            .runtime_plan_nanos
   139	            .saturating_add(delta.runtime_stage_nanos)
   140	            .saturating_add(delta.runtime_flush_nanos),
   141	    );
   142	    let event_total_ms = nanos_to_ms(
   143	        delta
   144	            .event_reader_nanos
   145	            .saturating_add(delta.event_writer_nanos),
   146	    );
   147	
   148	    println!("\n=== {} ===", name);
   149	    println!("setup_time_ms: {:.3}", setup_elapsed.as_secs_f64() * 1000.0);
   150	    println!("run_time_ms: {:.3}", run_elapsed.as_secs_f64() * 1000.0);
   151	    println!(
   152	        "metadata: entities={} repetitions={} schedule_runs={}",
   153	        meta.entity_count, meta.repetition_count, meta.schedule_run_count
   154	    );
   155	
   156	    println!(
   157	        "derived_ms: query_total={:.3} filter_total={:.3} runtime_total={:.3} event_total={:.3}",
   158	        query_total_ms, filter_total_ms, runtime_total_ms, event_total_ms
   159	    );
   160	
   161	    println!(
   162	        "query: matching_calls={} iter_calls={} get_calls={} single_calls={}",
   163	        delta.query_matching_calls,
   164	        delta.query_iter_calls,
   165	        delta.query_get_calls,
   166	        delta.query_single_calls
   167	    );
   168	    println!(
   169	        "runtime: plan_calls={} stage_calls={} flush_calls={} flush_queues={}",
   170	        delta.runtime_plan_calls,
   171	        delta.runtime_stage_calls,
   172	        delta.runtime_flush_calls,
   173	        delta.runtime_flush_command_queues
   174	    );
   175	    println!(
   176	        "events: reader_calls={} writer_calls={} read={} written={}",
   177	        delta.event_reader_calls, delta.event_writer_calls, delta.events_read, delta.events_written
   178	    );
   179	
   180	    println!("scheduler_summary:");
   181	    println!(
   182	        "  plan_build_calls={} plan_build_ms={:.3} conflict_checks={} stage_count={}",
   183	        delta.scheduler.plan_build_calls,
   184	        nanos_to_ms(delta.scheduler.plan_build_nanos),
   185	        delta.scheduler.plan_conflict_checks,
   186	        delta.scheduler.plan_stage_count
   187	    );
   188	
   189	    if delta.query_get_calls == 0 {
   190	        println!("note: query_get_nanos is zero because Query::get was not exercised.");
   191	    }
   192	    if delta.query_single_calls == 0 {
   193	        println!("note: query_single_nanos is zero because Query::single was not exercised.");
   194	    }
   195	}
   196	
   197	fn w2_move(mut query: Query<(&mut Position, &Velocity), (With<Simulated>, Without<Disabled>)>) {
   198	    for (position, velocity) in query.iter() {
   199	        position.x += velocity.x;
   200	        position.y += velocity.y;
   201	    }
   202	}
   203	
   204	fn w2_mutate_health(mut query: Query<&mut Health, With<Simulated>>) {
   205	    for health in query.iter() {
   206	        health.0 = health.0.saturating_sub(1);
   207	    }
   208	}
   209	
   210	fn w2_scan_changed(
   211	    mut query: Query<(Entity, &Health), Changed<Health>>,
   212	    mut stats: ResMut<MixedStats>,
   213	) {
   214	    let mut seen = 0_u64;
   215	    for _ in query.iter() {
   216	        seen = seen.saturating_add(1);
   217	    }
   218	    (*stats).0 = (*stats).0.wrapping_add(seen);
   219	}
   220	
   221	fn w2_scan_added(
   222	    mut query: Query<(Entity, &Health), Added<Health>>,
   223	    mut stats: ResMut<MixedStats>,
   224	) {
   225	    let mut seen = 0_u64;
   226	    for _ in query.iter() {
   227	        seen = seen.saturating_add(1);
   228	    }
   229	    (*stats).0 = (*stats).0.wrapping_add(seen);
   230	}
   231	
   232	fn w3_spawn(mut commands: Commands) {
   233	    for i in 0..128_u32 {
   234	        commands.spawn((
   235	            ChurnTag,
   236	            Position {
   237	                x: i as f32,
   238	                y: i as f32,
   239	            },
   240	            Velocity { x: 0.1, y: -0.1 },
   241	        ));
   242	    }
   243	}
   244	
   245	fn w3_despawn(mut commands: Commands, mut query: Query<(Entity, &ChurnTag)>) {
   246	    for (idx, (entity, _)) in query.iter().enumerate() {
   247	        if idx >= 128 {
   248	            break;
   249	        }
   250	        commands.despawn(entity);
   251	    }
   252	}
   253	
   254	fn w4_write_events(mut writer: EventWriter<BenchEvent>) {
   255	    for i in 0..256_u32 {
   256	        writer.send(BenchEvent(i));
   257	    }
   258	}
   259	
   260	fn w4_read_events(
   261	    reader: EventReader<BenchEvent>,
   262	    mut query: Query<&Position>,
   263	    mut stats: ResMut<EventStats>,
   264	) {
   265	    let events_seen = reader
   266	        .iter()
   267	        .fold(0_u64, |acc, event| acc.wrapping_add(event.0 as u64));
   268	    let entities_seen = query.iter().count() as u64;
   269	    (*stats).0 = (*stats)
   270	        .0
   271	        .wrapping_add(events_seen)
   272	        .wrapping_add(entities_seen);
   273	}
   274	
   275	fn w5_write_r0(mut r0: ResMut<R0>) {
   276	    (*r0).0 = (*r0).0.wrapping_add(1);
   277	}
   278	
   279	fn w5_write_r1(mut r1: ResMut<R1>) {
   280	    (*r1).0 = (*r1).0.wrapping_add(1);
   281	}
   282	
   283	fn w5_write_r2(mut r2: ResMut<R2>) {
   284	    (*r2).0 = (*r2).0.wrapping_add(1);
   285	}
   286	
   287	fn w5_write_r3(mut r3: ResMut<R3>) {
   288	    (*r3).0 = (*r3).0.wrapping_add(1);
   289	}
   290	
   291	fn w5_read_mix(r0: Res<R0>, r1: Res<R1>, r2: Res<R2>, mut sink: ResMut<Sink>) {
   292	    (*sink).0 = (*sink)
   293	        .0
   294	        .wrapping_add((*r0).0)
   295	        .wrapping_add((*r1).0)
   296	        .wrapping_add((*r2).0);
   297	}
   298	
   299	fn w5_read_mix_alt(r1: Res<R1>, r3: Res<R3>, mut sink: ResMut<Sink>) {
   300	    (*sink).0 = (*sink).0.wrapping_add((*r1).0).wrapping_add((*r3).0);
   301	}
   302	
   303	fn main() {
   304	    telemetry::reset();
   305	
   306	    {
   307	        let setup_start = Instant::now();
   308	        let mut world = World::new();
   309	        for i in 0..50_000 {
   310	            world.spawn((
   311	                Position {
   312	                    x: i as f32,
   313	                    y: 0.0,
   314	                },
   315	                Velocity { x: 1.0, y: -0.25 },
   316	            ));
   317	        }
   318	        let query = world.query_state::<(&mut Position, &Velocity), ()>();
   319	        let setup_elapsed = setup_start.elapsed();
   320	
   321	        // Warmup iteration (untimed).
   322	        for (position, velocity) in query.iter(&mut world) {
   323	            position.x += velocity.x;
   324	            position.y += velocity.y;
   325	        }
   326	
   327	        let before = telemetry::snapshot();
   328	        let run_start = Instant::now();
   329	        for _ in 0..8 {
   330	            for (position, velocity) in query.iter(&mut world) {
   331	                position.x += velocity.x;
   332	                position.y += velocity.y;
   333	            }
   334	        }
   335	        let run_elapsed = run_start.elapsed();
   336	        let after = telemetry::snapshot();
   337	
   338	        print_workload_report(
   339	            "W1 broad transform update (50k x 8)",
   340	            setup_elapsed,
   341	            run_elapsed,
   342	            WorkloadMeta {
   343	                entity_count: 50_000,
   344	                repetition_count: 8,
   345	                schedule_run_count: 0,
   346	            },
   347	            &telemetry::snapshot_delta(&before, &after),
   348	        );
   349	    }
   350	
   351	    {
   352	        let setup_start = Instant::now();
   353	        let mut world = World::new();
   354	        for i in 0..50_000 {
   355	            world.spawn((
   356	                Position {
   357	                    x: i as f32,
   358	                    y: 0.0,
   359	                },
   360	                Velocity { x: 1.0, y: -0.25 },
   361	            ));
   362	        }
   363	        let query = world.query_state::<&Position, ()>();
   364	        let setup_elapsed = setup_start.elapsed();
   365	
   366	        // Warmup iteration (untimed).
   367	        let mut warmup_checksum = 0.0_f32;
   368	        for position in query.iter(&world) {
   369	            warmup_checksum += position.x + position.y;
   370	        }
   371	        std::hint::black_box(warmup_checksum);
   372	
   373	        let before = telemetry::snapshot();
   374	        let run_start = Instant::now();
   375	        let mut checksum = 0.0_f32;
   376	        for _ in 0..8 {
   377	            for position in query.iter(&world) {
   378	                checksum += position.x + position.y;
   379	            }
   380	        }
   381	        std::hint::black_box(checksum);
   382	        let run_elapsed = run_start.elapsed();
   383	        let after = telemetry::snapshot();
   384	
   385	        print_workload_report(
   386	            "C2 broad no-filter read query (50k x 8)",
   387	            setup_elapsed,
   388	            run_elapsed,
   389	            WorkloadMeta {
   390	                entity_count: 50_000,
   391	                repetition_count: 8,
   392	                schedule_run_count: 0,
   393	            },
   394	            &telemetry::snapshot_delta(&before, &after),
   395	        );
   396	    }
   397	
   398	    {
   399	        let setup_start = Instant::now();
   400	        let mut world = World::new();
   401	        for i in 0..50_000 {
   402	            world.spawn((
   403	                Position {
   404	                    x: i as f32,
   405	                    y: 0.0,
   406	                },
   407	                Velocity { x: 1.0, y: -0.25 },
   408	            ));
   409	        }
   410	        let query = world.query_state::<&mut Velocity, ()>();
   411	        let setup_elapsed = setup_start.elapsed();
   412	
   413	        // Warmup iteration (untimed).
   414	        let mut warmup_checksum = 0.0_f32;
   415	        for velocity in query.iter(&mut world) {
   416	            velocity.x += 0.01;
   417	            velocity.y -= 0.01;
   418	            warmup_checksum += velocity.x + velocity.y;
   419	        }
   420	        std::hint::black_box(warmup_checksum);
   421	
   422	        let before = telemetry::snapshot();
   423	        let run_start = Instant::now();
   424	        let mut checksum = 0.0_f32;
   425	        for _ in 0..8 {
   426	            for velocity in query.iter(&mut world) {
   427	                velocity.x += 0.01;
   428	                velocity.y -= 0.01;
   429	                checksum += velocity.x + velocity.y;
   430	            }
   431	        }
   432	        std::hint::black_box(checksum);
   433	        let run_elapsed = run_start.elapsed();
   434	        let after = telemetry::snapshot();
   435	
   436	        print_workload_report(
   437	            "C3 broad simple write query (50k x 8)",
   438	            setup_elapsed,
   439	            run_elapsed,
   440	            WorkloadMeta {
   441	                entity_count: 50_000,
   442	                repetition_count: 8,
   443	                schedule_run_count: 0,
   444	            },
   445	            &telemetry::snapshot_delta(&before, &after),
   446	        );
   447	    }
   448	
   449	    {
   450	        let setup_start = Instant::now();
   451	        let mut world = World::new();
   452	        for i in 0..50_000 {
   453	            world.spawn((
   454	                Position {
   455	                    x: i as f32,
   456	                    y: 0.0,
   457	                },
   458	                Velocity { x: 1.0, y: -0.25 },
   459	            ));
   460	        }
   461	        let query = world.query_state::<(&mut Position, &mut Velocity), ()>();
   462	        let setup_elapsed = setup_start.elapsed();
   463	
   464	        // Warmup iteration (untimed).
   465	        let mut warmup_checksum = 0.0_f32;
   466	        for (position, velocity) in query.iter(&mut world) {
   467	            velocity.x += 0.01;
   468	            velocity.y -= 0.01;
   469	            position.x += velocity.x;
   470	            position.y += velocity.y;
   471	            warmup_checksum += position.x + position.y + velocity.x + velocity.y;
   472	        }
   473	        std::hint::black_box(warmup_checksum);
   474	
   475	        let before = telemetry::snapshot();
   476	        let run_start = Instant::now();
   477	        let mut checksum = 0.0_f32;
   478	        for _ in 0..8 {
   479	            for (position, velocity) in query.iter(&mut world) {
   480	                velocity.x += 0.01;
   481	                velocity.y -= 0.01;
   482	                position.x += velocity.x;
   483	                position.y += velocity.y;
   484	                checksum += position.x + position.y + velocity.x + velocity.y;
   485	            }
   486	        }
   487	        std::hint::black_box(checksum);
   488	        let run_elapsed = run_start.elapsed();
   489	        let after = telemetry::snapshot();
   490	
   491	        print_workload_report(
   492	            "C4 broad double mutable query (50k x 8)",
   493	            setup_elapsed,
   494	            run_elapsed,
   495	            WorkloadMeta {
   496	                entity_count: 50_000,
   497	                repetition_count: 8,
   498	                schedule_run_count: 0,
   499	            },
   500	            &telemetry::snapshot_delta(&before, &after),
   501	        );
   502	    }
   503	
   504	    {
   505	        let setup_start = Instant::now();
   506	        let mut world = World::new();
   507	        world.insert_resource(MixedStats::default());
   508	        for i in 0..20_000 {
   509	            if i % 8 == 0 {
   510	                world.spawn((
   511	                    Position {
   512	                        x: i as f32,
   513	                        y: 0.0,
   514	                    },
   515	                    Velocity { x: 1.0, y: 0.25 },
   516	                    Health(100),
   517	                    Simulated,
   518	                    Disabled,
   519	                ));
   520	            } else {
   521	                world.spawn((
   522	                    Position {
   523	                        x: i as f32,
   524	                        y: 0.0,
   525	                    },
   526	                    Velocity { x: 1.0, y: 0.25 },
   527	                    Health(100),
   528	                    Simulated,
   529	                ));
   530	            }
   531	        }
   532	        let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   533	        runtime.add_systems::<W2, _, _>(
   534	            &mut world,
   535	            (w2_move, w2_mutate_health, w2_scan_changed, w2_scan_added),
   536	        );
   537	        let _ = runtime.plan_for::<W2>().expect("w2 plan should exist");
   538	        let setup_elapsed = setup_start.elapsed();
   539	
   540	        // Warmup iteration (untimed).
   541	        runtime
   542	            .run_schedule::<W2>(&mut world)
   543	            .expect("w2 warmup run");
   544	
   545	        let before = telemetry::snapshot();
   546	        let run_start = Instant::now();
   547	        for _ in 0..20 {
   548	            runtime.run_schedule::<W2>(&mut world).expect("w2 run");
   549	        }
   550	        let run_elapsed = run_start.elapsed();
   551	        let after = telemetry::snapshot();
   552	
   553	        print_workload_report(
   554	            "W2 mixed/composite gameplay schedule (20k x 20 runs)",
   555	            setup_elapsed,
   556	            run_elapsed,
   557	            WorkloadMeta {
   558	                entity_count: 20_000,
   559	                repetition_count: 20,
   560	                schedule_run_count: 20,
   561	            },
   562	            &telemetry::snapshot_delta(&before, &after),
   563	        );
   564	    }
   565	
   566	    {
   567	        let setup_start = Instant::now();
   568	        let mut world = World::new();
   569	        for i in 0..20_000 {
   570	            world.spawn((
   571	                ChurnTag,
   572	                Position {
   573	                    x: i as f32,
   574	                    y: 0.0,
   575	                },
   576	                Velocity { x: 0.0, y: 0.0 },
   577	            ));
   578	        }
   579	        let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   580	        runtime.add_systems::<W3, _, _>(&mut world, (w3_spawn, w3_despawn));
   581	        let _ = runtime.plan_for::<W3>().expect("w3 plan should exist");
   582	        let setup_elapsed = setup_start.elapsed();
   583	
   584	        // Warmup iteration (untimed).
   585	        runtime
   586	            .run_schedule::<W3>(&mut world)
   587	            .expect("w3 warmup run");
   588	
   589	        let before = telemetry::snapshot();
   590	        let run_start = Instant::now();
   591	        for _ in 0..20 {
   592	            runtime.run_schedule::<W3>(&mut world).expect("w3 run");
   593	        }
   594	        let run_elapsed = run_start.elapsed();
   595	        let after = telemetry::snapshot();
   596	
   597	        print_workload_report(
   598	            "W3 structural churn schedule (20k base, 128 churn x 20 runs)",
   599	            setup_elapsed,
   600	            run_elapsed,
   601	            WorkloadMeta {
   602	                entity_count: 20_000,
   603	                repetition_count: 20,
   604	                schedule_run_count: 20,
   605	            },
   606	            &telemetry::snapshot_delta(&before, &after),
   607	        );
   608	    }
   609	
   610	    {
   611	        let setup_start = Instant::now();
   612	        let mut world = World::new();
   613	        world.insert_resource(EventStats::default());
   614	        for i in 0..10_000 {
   615	            world.spawn((
   616	                Position {
   617	                    x: i as f32,
   618	                    y: i as f32,
   619	                },
   620	                Velocity { x: 0.0, y: 0.0 },
   621	            ));
   622	        }
   623	        let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   624	        runtime.add_systems::<W4, _, _>(&mut world, (w4_write_events, w4_read_events));
   625	        let _ = runtime.plan_for::<W4>().expect("w4 plan should exist");
   626	        let setup_elapsed = setup_start.elapsed();
   627	
   628	        // Warmup iteration (untimed).
   629	        runtime
   630	            .run_schedule::<W4>(&mut world)
   631	            .expect("w4 warmup run");
   632	        // Clearing the event channel between runs is intentional here: this workload models
   633	        // per-frame transient event consumption where backlog carryover would skew read/write cost.
   634	        world.clear_events::<BenchEvent>();
   635	
   636	        let before = telemetry::snapshot();
   637	        let run_start = Instant::now();
   638	        for _ in 0..20 {
   639	            runtime.run_schedule::<W4>(&mut world).expect("w4 run");
   640	            // This workload intentionally uses explicit clear-based event lifecycle cleanup.
   641	            world.clear_events::<BenchEvent>();
   642	        }
   643	        let run_elapsed = run_start.elapsed();
   644	        let after = telemetry::snapshot();
   645	
   646	        print_workload_report(
   647	            "W4 event-heavy schedule (10k entities, 256 events x 20 runs)",
   648	            setup_elapsed,
   649	            run_elapsed,
   650	            WorkloadMeta {
   651	                entity_count: 10_000,
   652	                repetition_count: 20,
   653	                schedule_run_count: 20,
   654	            },
   655	            &telemetry::snapshot_delta(&before, &after),
   656	        );
   657	    }
   658	
   659	    {
   660	        let setup_start = Instant::now();
   661	        let mut world = World::new();
   662	        world.insert_resource(R0::default());
   663	        world.insert_resource(R1::default());
   664	        world.insert_resource(R2::default());
   665	        world.insert_resource(R3::default());
   666	        world.insert_resource(Sink::default());
   667	
   668	        let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   669	        for _ in 0..16 {
   670	            runtime.add_systems::<W5, _, _>(
   671	                &mut world,
   672	                (
   673	                    w5_write_r0.in_set(SetA),
   674	                    w5_write_r1.in_set(SetA),
   675	                    w5_read_mix.after(SetA).in_set(SetB),
   676	                    w5_write_r2.after(SetB).in_set(SetC),
   677	                    w5_read_mix_alt.after(SetC),
   678	                    w5_write_r3.in_set(SetA),
   679	                ),
   680	            );
   681	        }
   682	        // Build the execution plan before timed runs so setup/planning cost is separated.
   683	        let _ = runtime.plan_for::<W5>().expect("w5 plan should exist");
   684	        let setup_elapsed = setup_start.elapsed();
   685	
   686	        // Warmup iteration (untimed).
   687	        runtime
   688	            .run_schedule::<W5>(&mut world)
   689	            .expect("w5 warmup run");
   690	
   691	        let before = telemetry::snapshot();
   692	        let run_start = Instant::now();
   693	        for _ in 0..40 {
   694	            runtime.run_schedule::<W5>(&mut world).expect("w5 run");
   695	        }
   696	        let run_elapsed = run_start.elapsed();
   697	        let after = telemetry::snapshot();
   698	
   699	        print_workload_report(
   700	            "W5 scheduler stress schedule (16 registrations x 40 runs)",
   701	            setup_elapsed,
   702	            run_elapsed,
   703	            WorkloadMeta {
   704	                entity_count: 0,
   705	                repetition_count: 40,
   706	                schedule_run_count: 40,
   707	            },
   708	            &telemetry::snapshot_delta(&before, &after),
   709	        );
   710	    }
   711	
   712	    println!("\n=== cumulative snapshot ===");
   713	    println!("{:#?}", telemetry::snapshot());
   714	}

===== END FILE: ./examples/phase6_profile.rs =====

===== FILE: ./src/bundle.rs =====
     1	use crate::{Component, Entity, EntityError, World};
     2	
     3	/// Group of components that can be inserted or removed together.
     4	pub trait Bundle: Sized + 'static {
     5	    fn register(world: &mut World);
     6	    fn insert(self, world: &mut World, entity: Entity) -> Result<(), EntityError>;
     7	    fn remove(world: &mut World, entity: Entity) -> Result<Self, EntityError>;
     8	}
     9	
    10	impl<T: Component> Bundle for T {
    11	    fn register(world: &mut World) {
    12	        world.__register_component::<T>();
    13	    }
    14	
    15	    fn insert(self, world: &mut World, entity: Entity) -> Result<(), EntityError> {
    16	        world.__insert_component(entity, self)
    17	    }
    18	
    19	    fn remove(world: &mut World, entity: Entity) -> Result<Self, EntityError> {
    20	        world.__remove_component::<T>(entity)
    21	    }
    22	}
    23	
    24	macro_rules! impl_bundle_tuple {
    25	    ($(($ty:ident, $var:ident)),+ $(,)?) => {
    26	        impl<$($ty: Component),+> Bundle for ($($ty,)+) {
    27	            fn register(world: &mut World) {
    28	                $(world.__register_component::<$ty>();)+
    29	            }
    30	
    31	            fn insert(self, world: &mut World, entity: Entity) -> Result<(), EntityError> {
    32	                let ($($var,)+) = self;
    33	                $(world.__insert_component(entity, $var)?;)+
    34	                Ok(())
    35	            }
    36	
    37	            fn remove(world: &mut World, entity: Entity) -> Result<Self, EntityError> {
    38	                Ok((
    39	                    $(world.__remove_component::<$ty>(entity)?,)+
    40	                ))
    41	            }
    42	        }
    43	    };
    44	}
    45	
    46	impl_bundle_tuple!((A, a), (B, b));
    47	impl_bundle_tuple!((A, a), (B, b), (C, c));
    48	impl_bundle_tuple!((A, a), (B, b), (C, c), (D, d));
    49	impl_bundle_tuple!((A, a), (B, b), (C, c), (D, d), (E, e));
    50	impl_bundle_tuple!((A, a), (B, b), (C, c), (D, d), (E, e), (F, f));

===== END FILE: ./src/bundle.rs =====

===== FILE: ./src/commands/batch.rs =====
     1	use super::deferred::{DeferredCommand, DeferredCommandAdapter};
     2	use super::queue::CommandQueue;
     3	use crate::bundle::Bundle;
     4	use crate::entity::Entity;
     5	use crate::errors::CommandError;
     6	use crate::world::World;
     7	
     8	pub struct BatchCommands {
     9	    queue: CommandQueue,
    10	}
    11	
    12	impl BatchCommands {
    13	    pub fn new() -> Self {
    14	        Self { queue: Vec::new() }
    15	    }
    16	
    17	    fn queue_typed<T: 'static, C>(&mut self, command: C)
    18	    where
    19	        C: DeferredCommand<T>,
    20	    {
    21	        self.queue
    22	            .push(Box::new(DeferredCommandAdapter::new(command)));
    23	    }
    24	
    25	    pub fn defer<T: 'static, C>(&mut self, command: C)
    26	    where
    27	        C: DeferredCommand<T>,
    28	    {
    29	        self.queue_typed(command);
    30	    }
    31	
    32	    pub fn queue<F>(&mut self, command: F)
    33	    where
    34	        F: FnOnce(&mut World) -> Result<(), CommandError> + 'static,
    35	    {
    36	        self.queue_typed(command);
    37	    }
    38	
    39	    pub fn spawn<B: Bundle + 'static>(&mut self, bundle: B) {
    40	        self.queue(move |world: &mut World| {
    41	            world.spawn(bundle);
    42	            Ok(())
    43	        });
    44	    }
    45	
    46	    pub fn despawn(&mut self, entity: Entity) {
    47	        self.queue(move |world: &mut World| {
    48	            world.despawn(entity)?;
    49	            Ok(())
    50	        });
    51	    }
    52	
    53	    pub fn insert<B: Bundle + 'static>(&mut self, entity: Entity, bundle: B) {
    54	        self.queue(move |world: &mut World| {
    55	            world.insert(entity, bundle)?;
    56	            Ok(())
    57	        });
    58	    }
    59	
    60	    pub fn remove<B: Bundle + 'static>(&mut self, entity: Entity) {
    61	        self.queue(move |world: &mut World| {
    62	            let _: B = world.remove(entity)?;
    63	            Ok(())
    64	        });
    65	    }
    66	
    67	    pub fn apply(self, world: &mut World) -> Result<(), CommandError> {
    68	        for command in self.queue {
    69	            command.apply_erased(world)?;
    70	        }
    71	        Ok(())
    72	    }
    73	}
    74	
    75	impl Default for BatchCommands {
    76	    fn default() -> Self {
    77	        Self::new()
    78	    }
    79	}
    80	
    81	impl DeferredCommand<()> for BatchCommands {
    82	    fn apply(self: Box<Self>, world: &mut World) -> Result<(), CommandError> {
    83	        (*self).apply(world)
    84	    }
    85	}

===== FILE: ./src/commands/commands.rs =====
     1	use super::batch::BatchCommands;
     2	use super::deferred::{DeferredCommand, DeferredCommandAdapter};
     3	use super::queue::CommandQueue;
     4	use crate::bundle::Bundle;
     5	use crate::entity::Entity;
     6	use crate::errors::CommandError;
     7	use crate::world::World;
     8	use std::cell::{Cell, RefCell};
     9	use std::ptr::NonNull;
    10	use std::rc::Rc;
    11	
    12	pub struct Commands {
    13	    queue: CommandQueueStorage,
    14	}
    15	
    16	enum CommandQueueStorage {
    17	    Owned(CommandQueue),
    18	    ExternalOwner(ExternalCommandQueue),
    19	    ExternalBorrowed(ExternalCommandQueue),
    20	}
    21	
    22	#[derive(Clone)]
    23	struct ExternalCommandQueue {
    24	    queue: Rc<RefCell<CommandQueue>>,
    25	    active: Rc<Cell<bool>>,
    26	}
    27	
    28	impl ExternalCommandQueue {
    29	    fn new() -> Self {
    30	        Self {
    31	            queue: Rc::new(RefCell::new(Vec::new())),
    32	            active: Rc::new(Cell::new(true)),
    33	        }
    34	    }
    35	
    36	    fn assert_active(&self) {
    37	        assert!(
    38	            self.active.get(),
    39	            "commands param escaped its system execution scope"
    40	        );
    41	    }
    42	
    43	    fn drain(&self) -> CommandQueue {
    44	        std::mem::take(&mut *self.queue.borrow_mut())
    45	    }
    46	}
    47	
    48	impl Commands {
    49	    pub fn new() -> Self {
    50	        Self {
    51	            queue: CommandQueueStorage::Owned(Vec::new()),
    52	        }
    53	    }
    54	
    55	    pub(crate) fn new_external_owner() -> Self {
    56	        Self {
    57	            queue: CommandQueueStorage::ExternalOwner(ExternalCommandQueue::new()),
    58	        }
    59	    }
    60	
    61	    pub(crate) fn from_external(owner: *mut Commands) -> Self {
    62	        let owner = NonNull::new(owner).expect("command owner pointer must not be null");
    63	        // Safety: owner pointers are only provided by runtime command owner construction.
    64	        let queue = unsafe {
    65	            owner
    66	                .as_ref()
    67	                .external_queue()
    68	                .expect("command owner must provide an external queue")
    69	        };
    70	        Self {
    71	            queue: CommandQueueStorage::ExternalBorrowed(queue),
    72	        }
    73	    }
    74	
    75	    fn external_queue(&self) -> Option<ExternalCommandQueue> {
    76	        match &self.queue {
    77	            CommandQueueStorage::ExternalOwner(queue)
    78	            | CommandQueueStorage::ExternalBorrowed(queue) => Some(queue.clone()),
    79	            CommandQueueStorage::Owned(_) => None,
    80	        }
    81	    }
    82	
    83	    fn push_erased(&mut self, command: Box<dyn super::deferred::ErasedDeferredCommand>) {
    84	        match &mut self.queue {
    85	            CommandQueueStorage::Owned(queue) => queue.push(command),
    86	            CommandQueueStorage::ExternalOwner(queue) => queue.queue.borrow_mut().push(command),
    87	            CommandQueueStorage::ExternalBorrowed(queue) => {
    88	                queue.assert_active();
    89	                queue.queue.borrow_mut().push(command);
    90	            }
    91	        }
    92	    }
    93	
    94	    fn into_queue(self) -> CommandQueue {
    95	        match self.queue {
    96	            CommandQueueStorage::Owned(queue) => queue,
    97	            CommandQueueStorage::ExternalOwner(queue) => queue.drain(),
    98	            CommandQueueStorage::ExternalBorrowed(queue) => {
    99	                queue.assert_active();
   100	                queue.drain()
   101	            }
   102	        }
   103	    }
   104	
   105	    pub(crate) fn finalize_external_owner(&mut self) -> Commands {
   106	        let CommandQueueStorage::ExternalOwner(queue) = &self.queue else {
   107	            panic!("external command owner finalization requires runtime command owner");
   108	        };
   109	        queue.active.set(false);
   110	        let staged_queue = queue.drain();
   111	        Commands {
   112	            queue: CommandQueueStorage::Owned(staged_queue),
   113	        }
   114	    }
   115	
   116	    fn queue_typed<T: 'static, C>(&mut self, command: C)
   117	    where
   118	        C: DeferredCommand<T>,
   119	    {
   120	        self.push_erased(Box::new(DeferredCommandAdapter::new(command)));
   121	    }
   122	
   123	    pub fn defer<T: 'static, C>(&mut self, command: C)
   124	    where
   125	        C: DeferredCommand<T>,
   126	    {
   127	        self.queue_typed(command);
   128	    }
   129	
   130	    pub fn queue<F>(&mut self, command: F)
   131	    where
   132	        F: FnOnce(&mut World) -> Result<(), CommandError> + 'static,
   133	    {
   134	        self.queue_typed(command);
   135	    }
   136	
   137	    pub fn batch<F>(&mut self, build: F)
   138	    where
   139	        F: FnOnce(&mut BatchCommands),
   140	    {
   141	        let mut batch = BatchCommands::new();
   142	        build(&mut batch);
   143	        self.defer(batch);
   144	    }
   145	
   146	    pub fn spawn<B: Bundle + 'static>(&mut self, bundle: B) {
   147	        self.queue(move |world: &mut World| {
   148	            world.spawn(bundle);
   149	            Ok(())
   150	        });
   151	    }
   152	
   153	    pub fn despawn(&mut self, entity: Entity) {
   154	        self.queue(move |world: &mut World| {
   155	            world.despawn(entity)?;
   156	            Ok(())
   157	        });
   158	    }
   159	
   160	    pub fn insert<B: Bundle + 'static>(&mut self, entity: Entity, bundle: B) {
   161	        self.queue(move |world: &mut World| {
   162	            world.insert(entity, bundle)?;
   163	            Ok(())
   164	        });
   165	    }
   166	
   167	    pub fn remove<B: Bundle + 'static>(&mut self, entity: Entity) {
   168	        self.queue(move |world: &mut World| {
   169	            let _: B = world.remove(entity)?;
   170	            Ok(())
   171	        });
   172	    }
   173	
   174	    pub fn apply(self, world: &mut World) -> Result<(), CommandError> {
   175	        for command in self.into_queue() {
   176	            command.apply_erased(world)?;
   177	        }
   178	        Ok(())
   179	    }
   180	}
   181	
   182	impl Default for Commands {
   183	    fn default() -> Self {
   184	        Self::new()
   185	    }
   186	}

===== END FILE: ./src/commands/commands.rs =====

===== FILE: ./src/commands/deferred.rs =====
     1	use crate::errors::CommandError;
     2	use crate::world::World;
     3	use std::marker::PhantomData;
     4	
     5	pub trait DeferredCommand<T>: 'static {
     6	    fn apply(self: Box<Self>, world: &mut World) -> Result<T, CommandError>;
     7	}
     8	
     9	pub(crate) trait ErasedDeferredCommand {
    10	    fn apply_erased(self: Box<Self>, world: &mut World) -> Result<(), CommandError>;
    11	}
    12	
    13	pub(crate) struct DeferredCommandAdapter<T, C>
    14	where
    15	    C: DeferredCommand<T>,
    16	{
    17	    command: C,
    18	    _marker: PhantomData<fn() -> T>,
    19	}
    20	
    21	impl<T, C> DeferredCommandAdapter<T, C>
    22	where
    23	    C: DeferredCommand<T>,
    24	{
    25	    pub(crate) fn new(command: C) -> Self {
    26	        Self {
    27	            command,
    28	            _marker: PhantomData,
    29	        }
    30	    }
    31	}
    32	
    33	impl<T, C> ErasedDeferredCommand for DeferredCommandAdapter<T, C>
    34	where
    35	    C: DeferredCommand<T>,
    36	{
    37	    fn apply_erased(self: Box<Self>, world: &mut World) -> Result<(), CommandError> {
    38	        let Self { command, .. } = *self;
    39	        let _ = Box::new(command).apply(world)?;
    40	        Ok(())
    41	    }
    42	}
    43	
    44	impl<F> DeferredCommand<()> for F
    45	where
    46	    F: FnOnce(&mut World) -> Result<(), CommandError> + 'static,
    47	{
    48	    fn apply(self: Box<Self>, world: &mut World) -> Result<(), CommandError> {
    49	        (*self)(world)
    50	    }
    51	}

===== END FILE: ./src/commands/deferred.rs =====

===== FILE: ./src/entity.rs =====
     1	#[derive(Copy, Clone, Debug, Default, Eq, PartialEq, Hash, Ord, PartialOrd)]
     2	pub struct Entity {
     3	    pub id: u32,
     4	    pub generation: u32,
     5	}
     6	
     7	#[derive(Default)]
     8	pub struct EntityAllocator {
     9	    next_id: u32,
    10	    free_list: Vec<u32>,
    11	    generations: Vec<u32>,
    12	}
    13	
    14	impl EntityAllocator {
    15	    pub fn new() -> Self {
    16	        Self::default()
    17	    }
    18	
    19	    pub fn allocate(&mut self) -> Entity {
    20	        if let Some(id) = self.free_list.pop() {
    21	            Entity {
    22	                id,
    23	                generation: self.generations[id as usize],
    24	            }
    25	        } else {
    26	            let id = self.next_id;
    27	            self.next_id += 1;
    28	            self.generations.push(0);
    29	            Entity { id, generation: 0 }
    30	        }
    31	    }
    32	
    33	    pub fn free(&mut self, entity: Entity) {
    34	        if let Some(generation) = self.generations.get_mut(entity.id as usize) {
    35	            *generation = generation.saturating_add(1);
    36	            self.free_list.push(entity.id);
    37	        }
    38	    }
    39	}

===== END FILE: ./src/entity.rs =====

===== FILE: ./src/indexing/spatial_hash.rs =====
     1	use super::spatial_index::{SpatialIndex, SpatialIndexStorage};
     2	use crate::Entity;
     3	use crate::errors::SpatialIndexError;
     4	use geometry::Aabb3;
     5	use std::collections::{BTreeSet, HashMap};
     6	
     7	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone)]
     8	pub struct SpatialHashConfig {
     9	    pub cell_size: f32,
    10	}
    11	
    12	impl Default for SpatialHashConfig {
    13	    fn default() -> Self {
    14	        Self { cell_size: 1.0 }
    15	    }
    16	}
    17	
    18	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash, Ord, PartialOrd)]
    19	struct CellCoord {
    20	    x: i32,
    21	    y: i32,
    22	    z: i32,
    23	}
    24	
    25	#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy)]
    26	struct EntitySpatialEntry {
    27	    bounds: Aabb3,
    28	    min_cell: CellCoord,
    29	    max_cell: CellCoord,
    30	}
    31	
    32	pub struct SpatialHashIndex {
    33	    cell_size: f32,
    34	    cells: HashMap<CellCoord, BTreeSet<Entity>>,
    35	    entities: HashMap<Entity, EntitySpatialEntry>,
    36	}
    37	
    38	impl SpatialHashIndex {
    39	    pub fn new(config: SpatialHashConfig) -> Result<Self, SpatialIndexError> {
    40	        if !config.cell_size.is_finite() || config.cell_size <= 0.0 {
    41	            return Err(SpatialIndexError::InvalidCellSize {
    42	                cell_size: config.cell_size,
    43	            });
    44	        }
    45	
    46	        Ok(Self {
    47	            cell_size: config.cell_size,
    48	            cells: HashMap::new(),
    49	            entities: HashMap::new(),
    50	        })
    51	    }
    52	
    53	    fn ensure_valid_bounds(bounds: Aabb3) -> Result<(), SpatialIndexError> {
    54	        if !bounds.is_valid() {
    55	            return Err(SpatialIndexError::InvalidBounds);
    56	        }
    57	        Ok(())
    58	    }
    59	
    60	    fn axis_to_cell(&self, value: f32) -> i32 {
    61	        (value / self.cell_size).floor() as i32
    62	    }
    63	
    64	    fn cell_range_for_bounds(&self, bounds: Aabb3) -> (CellCoord, CellCoord) {
    65	        (
    66	            CellCoord {
    67	                x: self.axis_to_cell(bounds.min.x),
    68	                y: self.axis_to_cell(bounds.min.y),
    69	                z: self.axis_to_cell(bounds.min.z),
    70	            },
    71	            CellCoord {
    72	                x: self.axis_to_cell(bounds.max.x),
    73	                y: self.axis_to_cell(bounds.max.y),
    74	                z: self.axis_to_cell(bounds.max.z),
    75	            },
    76	        )
    77	    }
    78	
    79	    fn remove_entity_from_cells(
    80	        &mut self,
    81	        entity: Entity,
    82	        min_cell: CellCoord,
    83	        max_cell: CellCoord,
    84	    ) {
    85	        for x in min_cell.x..=max_cell.x {
    86	            for y in min_cell.y..=max_cell.y {
    87	                for z in min_cell.z..=max_cell.z {
    88	                    let coord = CellCoord { x, y, z };
    89	                    let mut should_remove_cell = false;
    90	                    if let Some(occupants) = self.cells.get_mut(&coord) {
    91	                        occupants.remove(&entity);
    92	                        should_remove_cell = occupants.is_empty();
    93	                    }
    94	                    if should_remove_cell {
    95	                        self.cells.remove(&coord);
    96	                    }
    97	                }
    98	            }
    99	        }
   100	    }
   101	
   102	    fn insert_entity_into_cells(
   103	        &mut self,
   104	        entity: Entity,
   105	        min_cell: CellCoord,
   106	        max_cell: CellCoord,
   107	    ) {
   108	        for x in min_cell.x..=max_cell.x {
   109	            for y in min_cell.y..=max_cell.y {
   110	                for z in min_cell.z..=max_cell.z {
   111	                    self.cells
   112	                        .entry(CellCoord { x, y, z })
   113	                        .or_default()
   114	                        .insert(entity);
   115	                }
   116	            }
   117	        }
   118	    }
   119	
   120	    fn upsert_entity(&mut self, entity: Entity, bounds: Aabb3) {
   121	        let (min_cell, max_cell) = self.cell_range_for_bounds(bounds);
   122	        if let Some(previous) = self.entities.remove(&entity) {
   123	            self.remove_entity_from_cells(entity, previous.min_cell, previous.max_cell);
   124	        }
   125	        self.insert_entity_into_cells(entity, min_cell, max_cell);
   126	        self.entities.insert(
   127	            entity,
   128	            EntitySpatialEntry {
   129	                bounds,
   130	                min_cell,
   131	                max_cell,
   132	            },
   133	        );
   134	    }
   135	}
   136	
   137	impl SpatialIndex for SpatialHashIndex {
   138	    fn insert(&mut self, entity: Entity, bounds: Aabb3) -> Result<(), SpatialIndexError> {
   139	        Self::ensure_valid_bounds(bounds)?;
   140	        self.upsert_entity(entity, bounds);
   141	        Ok(())
   142	    }
   143	
   144	    fn update(&mut self, entity: Entity, bounds: Aabb3) -> Result<(), SpatialIndexError> {
   145	        Self::ensure_valid_bounds(bounds)?;
   146	        self.upsert_entity(entity, bounds);
   147	        Ok(())
   148	    }
   149	
   150	    fn remove(&mut self, entity: Entity) -> bool {
   151	        let Some(previous) = self.entities.remove(&entity) else {
   152	            return false;
   153	        };
   154	        self.remove_entity_from_cells(entity, previous.min_cell, previous.max_cell);
   155	        true
   156	    }
   157	
   158	    fn query_aabb(&self, bounds: Aabb3) -> Result<Vec<Entity>, SpatialIndexError> {
   159	        Self::ensure_valid_bounds(bounds)?;
   160	        let (min_cell, max_cell) = self.cell_range_for_bounds(bounds);
   161	        let mut candidates = BTreeSet::new();
   162	        for x in min_cell.x..=max_cell.x {
   163	            for y in min_cell.y..=max_cell.y {
   164	                for z in min_cell.z..=max_cell.z {
   165	                    if let Some(occupants) = self.cells.get(&CellCoord { x, y, z }) {
   166	                        candidates.extend(occupants.iter().copied());
   167	                    }
   168	                }
   169	            }
   170	        }
   171	
   172	        let mut results = Vec::new();
   173	        for entity in candidates {
   174	            let Some(entry) = self.entities.get(&entity) else {
   175	                continue;
   176	            };
   177	            if entry.bounds.intersects(&bounds) {
   178	                results.push(entity);
   179	            }
   180	        }
   181	        Ok(results)
   182	    }
   183	}
   184	
   185	impl SpatialIndexStorage for SpatialHashIndex {}

===== END FILE: ./src/indexing/spatial_hash.rs =====

     9	pub struct QueryTypeAccess {
    10	    type_id: TypeId,
    11	    name: &'static str,
    12	}
    13	
    14	impl QueryTypeAccess {
    15	    pub fn of<T: 'static>(name: &'static str) -> Self {
    16	        Self {
    17	            type_id: TypeId::of::<T>(),
    18	            name,
    19	        }
    20	    }
    21	
    22	    pub fn type_id(&self) -> TypeId {
    23	        self.type_id
    24	    }
    25	
    26	    pub fn name(&self) -> &'static str {
    27	        self.name
    28	    }

    31	#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default)]
    32	pub struct QueryAccess {
    33	    component_reads: Vec<QueryTypeAccess>,
    34	    orphaned_component_reads: Vec<QueryTypeAccess>,
    35	    component_writes: Vec<QueryTypeAccess>,
    36	    resource_reads: Vec<QueryTypeAccess>,
    37	    resource_writes: Vec<QueryTypeAccess>,
    38	    deferred_structural_mutation: bool,
    39	}
    40	
    41	impl QueryAccess {
    42	    pub fn structural_mutation() -> Self {
    43	        let mut access = Self::default();
    44	        access.deferred_structural_mutation = true;
    45	        access
    46	    }
    47	
    48	    pub fn component_reads(&self) -> &[QueryTypeAccess] {
    49	        &self.component_reads
    50	    }

    61	        &self.resource_reads
    62	    }
    63

    66	    }

    70	    }

    74	            &mut self.component_reads,
    75	            QueryTypeAccess::of::<T>(T::component_name()),
    76	        );

    91	    }

    97	        );

   117	    }

   119	
   120	pub trait QueryFilter {
   121	    fn configure(required: &mut Vec<TypeId>, excluded: &mut Vec<TypeId>);
   122	
   123	    fn append_access(_access: &mut QueryAccess) {}
   124	
   125	    fn needs_tick_filter() -> bool {
   126	        false
   127	    }
   128	
   129	    fn matches_entity(_world: &World, _entity: Entity, _since_tick: u64) -> bool {
   130	        true
   131	    }
   132	}
   133	
   134	impl QueryFilter for () {
   135	    fn configure(_required: &mut Vec<TypeId>, _excluded: &mut Vec<TypeId>) {}
   136	}
   137	
   138	pub struct With<T: Component>(PhantomData<T>);
   139	pub struct Without<T: Component>(PhantomData<T>);
   140	
   141	impl<T: Component> QueryFilter for With<T> {
   142	    fn configure(required: &mut Vec<TypeId>, _excluded: &mut Vec<TypeId>) {
   143	        push_unique_type(required, TypeId::of::<T>());
   144	    }
   145	}
   146	
   147	impl<T: Component> QueryFilter for Without<T> {
   148	    fn configure(_required: &mut Vec<TypeId>, excluded: &mut Vec<TypeId>) {
   149	        push_unique_type(excluded, TypeId::of::<T>());
   150	    }
   151	}
   152	
   153	pub struct Changed<T: Component>(PhantomData<T>);
   154	pub struct Added<T: Component>(PhantomData<T>);
   155	
   156	impl<T: Component> QueryFilter for Changed<T> {
   157	    fn configure(required: &mut Vec<TypeId>, _excluded: &mut Vec<TypeId>) {
   158	        push_unique_type(required, TypeId::of::<T>());
   159	    }
   160	
   161	    fn append_access(access: &mut QueryAccess) {
   162	        access.add_component_read::<T>();
   163	    }
   164	
   165	    fn needs_tick_filter() -> bool {
   166	        true
   167	    }
   168	
   169	    fn matches_entity(world: &World, entity: Entity, since_tick: u64) -> bool {
   170	        world.component_changed_for_entity_since::<T>(entity, since_tick)
   171	    }
   172	}
   173	
   174	impl<T: Component> QueryFilter for Added<T> {
   175	    fn configure(required: &mut Vec<TypeId>, _excluded: &mut Vec<TypeId>) {
   176	        push_unique_type(required, TypeId::of::<T>());
   177	    }
   178	
   179	    fn append_access(access: &mut QueryAccess) {
   180	        access.add_component_read::<T>();
   181	    }
   182	
   183	    fn needs_tick_filter() -> bool {
   184	        true
   185	    }
   186	
   187	    fn matches_entity(world: &World, entity: Entity, since_tick: u64) -> bool {
   188	        world.component_added_for_entity_since::<T>(entity, since_tick)
   189	    }
   190	}
   191	
   192	impl<A: QueryFilter, B: QueryFilter> QueryFilter for (A, B) {
   193	    fn configure(required: &mut Vec<TypeId>, excluded: &mut Vec<TypeId>) {
   194	        A::configure(required, excluded);
   195	        B::configure(required, excluded);
   196	    }
   197	
   198	    fn append_access(access: &mut QueryAccess) {
   199	        A::append_access(access);
   200	        B::append_access(access);
   201	    }
   202	
   203	    fn needs_tick_filter() -> bool {
   204	        A::needs_tick_filter() || B::needs_tick_filter()
   205	    }
   206	
   207	    fn matches_entity(world: &World, entity: Entity, since_tick: u64) -> bool {
   208	        A::matches_entity(world, entity, since_tick) && B::matches_entity(world, entity, since_tick)
   209	    }
   210	}
   211	
   212	macro_rules! impl_query_filter_tuple {
   213	    ($(($($name:ident),+)),+ $(,)?) => {
   214	        $(
   215	            impl<$($name: QueryFilter,)+> QueryFilter for ($($name,)+) {
   216	                fn configure(required: &mut Vec<TypeId>, excluded: &mut Vec<TypeId>) {
   217	                    $(
   218	                        $name::configure(required, excluded);
   219	                    )+
   220	                }
   221	
   222	                fn append_access(access: &mut QueryAccess) {
   223	                    $(
   224	                        $name::append_access(access);
   225	                    )+
   226	                }
   227	
   228	                fn needs_tick_filter() -> bool {
   229	                    false $(|| $name::needs_tick_filter())+
   230	                }
   231	
   232	                fn matches_entity(world: &World, entity: Entity, since_tick: u64) -> bool {
   233	                    true $(
   234	                        && $name::matches_entity(world, entity, since_tick)
   235	                    )+
   236	                }
   237	            }
   238	        )+
   239	    };
   240	}
   241	
   242	impl_query_filter_tuple!((A, B, C), (A, B, C, D), (A, B, C, D, E), (A, B, C, D, E, F));
   243	
   244	impl<T: Component> With<T> {
   245	    pub fn new() -> Self {
   246	        Self(PhantomData)
   247	    }
   248	}
   249	
   250	impl<T: Component> Without<T> {
   251	    pub fn new() -> Self {
   252	        Self(PhantomData)
   253	    }
   254	}
   255	
   256	impl<T: Component> Changed<T> {
   257	    pub fn new() -> Self {
   258	        Self(PhantomData)
   259	    }
   260	}
   261	
   262	impl<T: Component> Added<T> {
   263	    pub fn new() -> Self {
   264	        Self(PhantomData)
   265	    }
   266	}
   267	
   268	pub(super) fn push_unique_type(target: &mut Vec<TypeId>, type_id: TypeId) {
   269	    if !target.contains(&type_id) {
   270	        target.push(type_id);
   271	    }
   272	}
   273	
   274	fn push_unique_access(target: &mut Vec<QueryTypeAccess>, access: QueryTypeAccess) {
   275	    if !target.iter().any(|entry| entry.type_id == access.type_id) {
   276	        target.push(access);
   277	    }
   278	}

     1	// Owner: Grotto Quest ecs - Removed Component Query
     2	use super::access_and_filters::QueryAccess;
     3	use crate::component::Component;
     4	use crate::entity::Entity;
     5	use crate::world::World;
     6	use std::any::TypeId;
     7	use std::cell::RefCell;
     8	use std::marker::PhantomData;
     9	use std::ptr::NonNull;
    10	
    11	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]
    12	pub struct Orphaned<T: Component> {
    13	    entity: Entity,
    14	    tick: u64,
    15	    _marker: PhantomData<T>,
    16	}
    17	
    18	impl<T: Component> Orphaned<T> {
    19	    pub fn entity(&self) -> Entity {
    20	        self.entity
    21	    }
    22	
    23	    pub fn tick(&self) -> u64 {
    24	        self.tick
    25	    }
    26	}
    27	
    28	pub struct QueryOrphanedState<T: Component> {
    29	    access: QueryAccess,
    30	    scratch: RefCell<Vec<(Entity, u64)>>,
    31	    _marker: PhantomData<T>,
    32	}
    33	
    34	impl<T: Component> QueryOrphanedState<T> {
    35	    pub fn new(_world: &World) -> Self {
    36	        let mut access = QueryAccess::default();
    37	        access.add_orphaned_component_read::<T>();
    38	        Self {
    39	            access,
    40	            scratch: RefCell::new(Vec::new()),
    41	            _marker: PhantomData,
    42	        }
    43	    }
    44	
    45	    pub fn access(&self) -> &QueryAccess {
    46	        &self.access
    47	    }
    48	
    49	    pub fn iter<'w>(&self, world: &'w World) -> impl Iterator<Item = Orphaned<T>> + 'w {
    50	        let mut scratch = self.scratch.borrow_mut();
    51	        world.removed_component_records_current_window(TypeId::of::<T>(), &mut scratch);
    52	        let records = scratch
    53	            .iter()
    54	            .map(|(entity, tick)| Orphaned {
    55	                entity: *entity,
    56	                tick: *tick,
    57	                _marker: PhantomData,
    58	            })
    59	            .collect::<Vec<_>>();
    60	        records.into_iter()
    61	    }
    62	}
    63	
    64	pub struct QueryOrphaned<T: Component> {
    65	    world: NonNull<World>,
    66	    state: NonNull<QueryOrphanedState<T>>,
    67	    _marker: PhantomData<T>,
    68	}
    69	
    70	impl<T: Component> QueryOrphaned<T> {
    71	    pub(crate) fn new(world: *mut World, state: &mut QueryOrphanedState<T>) -> Self {
    72	        Self {
    73	            world: NonNull::new(world).expect("world pointer must not be null"),
    74	            state: NonNull::from(state),
    75	            _marker: PhantomData,
    76	        }
    77	    }
    78	
    79	    pub fn access(&self) -> &QueryAccess {
    80	        unsafe { self.state.as_ref().access() }
    81	    }
    82	
    83	    pub fn iter(&mut self) -> impl Iterator<Item = Orphaned<T>> + '_ {
    84	        let world = unsafe { self.world.as_ref() };
    85	        unsafe { self.state.as_ref().iter(world) }
    86	    }
    87	}

     1	// Owner: Grotto Quest ecs - Query Runtime
     2	use super::access_and_filters::QueryAccess;
     3	use super::traits_and_state::{QueryArchetypeRow, QueryData, QueryFastCache};
     4	use crate::component::Component;
     5	use crate::entity::Entity;
     6	use crate::storage::ArchetypeExecutionBinding;
     7	use crate::world::World;
     8	use std::any::TypeId;
     9	
    10	fn required_types_match(required_present: &[TypeId], expected: &[TypeId]) -> bool {
    11	    required_present.len() == expected.len()
    12	        && expected
    13	            .iter()
    14	            .all(|type_id| required_present.contains(type_id))
    15	}
    16	
    17	fn collect_rows_from_bindings(
    18	    world: &World,
    19	    bindings: &[ArchetypeExecutionBinding],
    20	    rows: &mut Vec<QueryArchetypeRow>,
    21	) {
    22	    rows.clear();
    23	    for binding in bindings {
    24	        for row in 0..binding.row_count {
    25	            if let Some(entity) = world.archetype_entity_at(binding.archetype_index, row) {
    26	                rows.push(QueryArchetypeRow {
    27	                    entity,
    28	                    archetype_index: binding.archetype_index,
    29	                    row,
    30	                });
    31	            }
    32	        }
    33	    }
    34	    rows.sort_unstable();
    35	}
    36	
    37	impl<T: Component> QueryData for &T {
    38	    type Item<'w> = &'w T;
    39	    type WorldRef<'w> = &'w World;
    40	
    41	    fn query_types() -> Vec<TypeId> {
    42	        vec![TypeId::of::<T>()]
    43	    }
    44	
    45	    fn append_access(access: &mut QueryAccess) {
    46	        access.add_component_read::<T>();
    47	    }
    48	
    49	    fn supports_fast_path() -> bool {
    50	        true
    51	    }
    52	
    53	    fn prepare_fast_cache(world: *mut World, cache: &mut QueryFastCache) -> bool {
    54	        let world_ptr = world as *const World;
    55	        if cache.world_ptr != world_ptr {
    56	            cache.world_ptr = world_ptr;
    57	            cache.archetype_bindings.clear();
    58	        }
    59	        true
    60	    }
    61	
    62	    unsafe fn fetch<'w>(world: *mut World, entity: Entity) -> Option<Self::Item<'w>> {
    63	        unsafe { (&*world).archetype_component::<T>(entity) }
    64	    }
    65	
    66	    unsafe fn fetch_fast<'w>(
    67	        world: *mut World,
    68	        entity: Entity,
    69	        cache: &mut QueryFastCache,
    70	    ) -> Option<Self::Item<'w>> {
    71	        let _ = cache;
    72	        unsafe { Self::fetch(world, entity) }
    73	    }
    74	
    75	    unsafe fn world_ref<'w>(world: *mut World) -> Self::WorldRef<'w> {
    76	        unsafe { &*world }
    77	    }
    78	}

    80	impl<T: Component> QueryData for &mut T {
    81	    type Item<'w> = &'w mut T;
    82	    type WorldRef<'w> = &'w mut World;
    83	
    84	    fn query_types() -> Vec<TypeId> {
    85	        vec![TypeId::of::<T>()]
    86	    }
    87	
    88	    fn append_access(access: &mut QueryAccess) {
    89	        access.add_component_write::<T>();
    90	    }
    91	
    92	    fn supports_fast_path() -> bool {
    93	        true
    94	    }
    95	
    96	    fn prepare_fast_cache(world: *mut World, cache: &mut QueryFastCache) -> bool {
    97	        let world_ptr = world as *const World;
    98	        if cache.world_ptr != world_ptr {
    99	            cache.world_ptr = world_ptr;
   100	            cache.archetype_bindings.clear();
   101	        }
   102	        true
   103	    }
   104	
   105	    fn supports_archetype_execution() -> bool {
   106	        true
   107	    }
   108	
   109	    fn collect_archetype_rows(
   110	        world: *mut World,
   111	        required_present: &[TypeId],
   112	        excluded: &[TypeId],
   113	        rows: &mut Vec<QueryArchetypeRow>,
   114	        cache: &mut QueryFastCache,
   115	    ) -> bool {
   116	        if !required_types_match(required_present, &[TypeId::of::<T>()]) || !excluded.is_empty() {
   117	            return false;
   118	        }
   119	
   120	        let world_ref = unsafe { &*world };
   121	        if !world_ref.matching_archetype_bindings_into(
   122	            required_present,
   123	            excluded,
   124	            &mut cache.archetype_bindings,
   125	        ) {
   126	            return false;
   127	        }
   128	
   129	        collect_rows_from_bindings(world_ref, &cache.archetype_bindings, rows);
   130	        true
   131	    }
   132	
   133	    fn mark_changed(world: *mut World, entity: Entity) {
   134	        // Safety: query execution ensures exclusive mutable world access for this query form.
   135	        let _ = unsafe { (&mut *world).get_mut::<T>(entity) };
   136	    }
   137	
   138	    fn mark_changed_fast(world: *mut World, entity: Entity, _cache: &mut QueryFastCache) {
   139	        let world_mut = unsafe { &mut *world };
   140	        world_mut.mark_component_modified_by_id(entity, TypeId::of::<T>(), T::component_name());
   141	    }
   142	
   143	    unsafe fn fetch<'w>(world: *mut World, entity: Entity) -> Option<Self::Item<'w>> {
   144	        unsafe { (&mut *world).archetype_component_mut_untracked::<T>(entity) }
   145	    }
   146	
   147	    unsafe fn fetch_fast<'w>(
   148	        world: *mut World,
   149	        entity: Entity,
   150	        cache: &mut QueryFastCache,
   151	    ) -> Option<Self::Item<'w>> {
   152	        let _ = cache;
   153	        unsafe { Self::fetch(world, entity) }
   154	    }
   155	
   156	    unsafe fn world_ref<'w>(world: *mut World) -> Self::WorldRef<'w> {
   157	        unsafe { &mut *world }
   158	    }
   159	}
