   209	impl<A: Component, B: Component> QueryData for (&A, &B) {
   210	    type Item<'w> = (&'w A, &'w B);
   211	    type WorldRef<'w> = &'w World;
   212	
   213	    fn query_types() -> Vec<TypeId> {
   214	        vec![TypeId::of::<A>(), TypeId::of::<B>()]
   215	    }
   216	
   217	    fn append_access(access: &mut QueryAccess) {
   218	        access.add_component_read::<A>();
   219	        access.add_component_read::<B>();
   220	    }
   221	
   222	    unsafe fn fetch<'w>(world: *mut World, entity: Entity) -> Option<Self::Item<'w>> {
   223	        let a = unsafe { (&*world).archetype_component::<A>(entity) }?;
   224	        let b = unsafe { (&*world).archetype_component::<B>(entity) }?;
   225	        Some((a, b))
   226	    }
   227	
   228	    unsafe fn world_ref<'w>(world: *mut World) -> Self::WorldRef<'w> {
   229	        unsafe { &*world }
   230	    }
   231	}

   233	impl<A: Component, B: Component> QueryData for (&mut A, &B) {
   234	    type Item<'w> = (&'w mut A, &'w B);
   235	    type WorldRef<'w> = &'w mut World;
   236	
   237	    fn query_types() -> Vec<TypeId> {
   238	        vec![TypeId::of::<A>(), TypeId::of::<B>()]
   239	    }
   240	
   241	    fn append_access(access: &mut QueryAccess) {
   242	        access.add_component_write::<A>();
   243	        access.add_component_read::<B>();
   244	    }
   245	
   246	    fn supports_fast_path() -> bool {
   247	        true
   248	    }
   249	
   250	    fn prepare_fast_cache(world: *mut World, cache: &mut QueryFastCache) -> bool {
   251	        if TypeId::of::<A>() == TypeId::of::<B>() {
   252	            cache.archetype_bindings.clear();
   253	            return false;
   254	        }
   255	
   256	        let world_ptr = world as *const World;
   257	        if cache.world_ptr != world_ptr {
   258	            cache.world_ptr = world_ptr;
   259	            cache.archetype_bindings.clear();
   260	        }
   261	
   262	        true
   263	    }
   264	
   265	    fn supports_archetype_execution() -> bool {
   266	        true
   267	    }
   268	
   269	    fn collect_archetype_rows(
   270	        world: *mut World,
   271	        required_present: &[TypeId],
   272	        excluded: &[TypeId],
   273	        rows: &mut Vec<QueryArchetypeRow>,
   274	        cache: &mut QueryFastCache,
   275	    ) -> bool {
   276	        if TypeId::of::<A>() == TypeId::of::<B>()
   277	            || !required_types_match(required_present, &[TypeId::of::<A>(), TypeId::of::<B>()])
   278	            || !excluded.is_empty()
   279	        {
   280	            return false;
   281	        }
   282	
   283	        let world_ref = unsafe { &*world };
   284	        if !world_ref.matching_archetype_bindings_into(
   285	            required_present,
   286	            excluded,
   287	            &mut cache.archetype_bindings,
   288	        ) {
   289	            return false;
   290	        }
   291	
   292	        collect_rows_from_bindings(world_ref, &cache.archetype_bindings, rows);
   293	        true
   294	    }
   295	
   296	    fn mark_changed(world: *mut World, entity: Entity) {
   297	        // Safety: query execution ensures exclusive mutable world access for this query form.
   298	        let _ = unsafe { (&mut *world).get_mut::<A>(entity) };
   299	    }
   300	
   301	    fn mark_changed_fast(world: *mut World, entity: Entity, _cache: &mut QueryFastCache) {
   302	        let world_mut = unsafe { &mut *world };
   303	        world_mut.mark_component_modified_by_id(entity, TypeId::of::<A>(), A::component_name());
   304	    }
   305	
   306	    unsafe fn fetch<'w>(world: *mut World, entity: Entity) -> Option<Self::Item<'w>> {
   307	        assert_ne!(
   308	            TypeId::of::<A>(),
   309	            TypeId::of::<B>(),
   310	            "mutable/read query requires distinct component types",
   311	        );
   312	
   313	        let world_mut = unsafe { &mut *world };
   314	        let b = world_mut.archetype_component::<B>(entity)? as *const B;
   315	        let a = world_mut.archetype_component_mut_untracked::<A>(entity)? as *mut A;
   316	
   317	        // Safety: mutable/read query access requires distinct component types.
   318	        Some(unsafe { (&mut *a, &*b) })
   319	    }
   320	
   321	    unsafe fn fetch_fast<'w>(
   322	        world: *mut World,
   323	        entity: Entity,
   324	        cache: &mut QueryFastCache,
   325	    ) -> Option<Self::Item<'w>> {
   326	        let _ = cache;
   327	        unsafe { Self::fetch(world, entity) }
   328	    }
   329	
   330	    unsafe fn world_ref<'w>(world: *mut World) -> Self::WorldRef<'w> {
   331	        unsafe { &mut *world }
   332	    }
   333	}

   338	
   339	    fn query_types() -> Vec<TypeId> {

   341	    }

   344	        access.add_component_read::<A>();
   345	        access.add_component_write::<B>();
   346	    }
   347	
   348	    fn mark_changed(world: *mut World, entity: Entity) {
   349	        // Safety: query execution ensures exclusive mutable world access for this query form.
   350	        let _ = unsafe { (&mut *world).get_mut::<B>(entity) };
   351	    }

   354	        assert_ne!(
   355	            TypeId::of::<A>(),

   358	        );

   360	        let world_mut = unsafe { &mut *world };

   362	        let b = world_mut.archetype_component_mut_untracked::<B>(entity)? as *mut B;
   363

   440	        let _ = world_mut.get_mut::<B>(entity);

   499	impl<T: Component> QueryData for Option<&mut T> {
   500	    type Item<'w> = Option<&'w mut T>;
   501	    type WorldRef<'w> = &'w mut World;
   502	
   503	    fn query_types() -> Vec<TypeId> {
   504	        Vec::new()
   505	    }
   506	
   507	    fn append_access(access: &mut QueryAccess) {
   508	        access.add_component_write::<T>();
   509	    }
   510	
   511	    fn mark_changed(world: *mut World, entity: Entity) {
   512	        let should_mark = unsafe { (&*world).archetype_component::<T>(entity) };
   513	        if should_mark.is_some() {
   514	            // Safety: query execution ensures exclusive mutable world access for this query form.
   515	            let _ = unsafe { (&mut *world).get_mut::<T>(entity) };
   516	        }
   517	    }
   518	
   519	    unsafe fn fetch<'w>(world: *mut World, entity: Entity) -> Option<Self::Item<'w>> {
   520	        let value = unsafe { (&mut *world).archetype_component_mut_untracked::<T>(entity) };
   521	        Some(value)
   522	    }
   523	
   524	    unsafe fn world_ref<'w>(world: *mut World) -> Self::WorldRef<'w> {
   525	        unsafe { &mut *world }
   526	    }
   527	}

   529	impl<A: Component, B: Component> QueryData for (&mut A, Option<&B>) {
   530	    type Item<'w> = (&'w mut A, Option<&'w B>);
   531	    type WorldRef<'w> = &'w mut World;
   532	
   533	    fn query_types() -> Vec<TypeId> {
   534	        vec![TypeId::of::<A>()]
   535	    }
   536	
   537	    fn append_access(access: &mut QueryAccess) {
   538	        access.add_component_write::<A>();
   539	        access.add_component_read::<B>();
   540	    }
   541	
   542	    fn mark_changed(world: *mut World, entity: Entity) {
   543	        // Safety: query execution ensures exclusive mutable world access for this query form.
   544	        let _ = unsafe { (&mut *world).get_mut::<A>(entity) };
   545	    }
   546	
   547	    unsafe fn fetch<'w>(world: *mut World, entity: Entity) -> Option<Self::Item<'w>> {
   548	        assert_ne!(
   549	            TypeId::of::<A>(),
   550	            TypeId::of::<B>(),
   551	            "mutable/optional query requires distinct component types",
   552	        );
   553	
   554	        let world_mut = unsafe { &mut *world };
   555	        let b = world_mut
   556	            .archetype_component::<B>(entity)
   557	            .map(|value| value as *const B);
   558	        let a = world_mut.archetype_component_mut_untracked::<A>(entity)? as *mut A;
   559	
   560	        // Safety: mutable/optional query access requires distinct component types.
   561	        Some(unsafe { (&mut *a, b.map(|ptr| &*ptr)) })
   562	    }
   563	
   564	    unsafe fn world_ref<'w>(world: *mut World) -> Self::WorldRef<'w> {
   565	        unsafe { &mut *world }
   566	    }
   567	}

   579	        access.add_component_read::<B>();

   582	    unsafe fn fetch<'w>(world: *mut World, entity: Entity) -> Option<Self::Item<'w>> {
   583	        let world_ref = unsafe { &*world };
   584	        let a = world_ref.archetype_component::<A>(entity)?;
   585	        let b = world_ref.archetype_component::<B>(entity);
   586	        Some((a, b))

   594	impl<A: Component, B: Component> QueryData for (&A, Option<&mut B>) {
   595	    type Item<'w> = (&'w A, Option<&'w mut B>);
   596	    type WorldRef<'w> = &'w mut World;
   597	
   598	    fn query_types() -> Vec<TypeId> {
   599	        vec![TypeId::of::<A>()]
   600	    }
   601	
   602	    fn append_access(access: &mut QueryAccess) {
   603	        access.add_component_read::<A>();
   604	        access.add_component_write::<B>();
   605	    }
   606	
   607	    fn mark_changed(world: *mut World, entity: Entity) {
   608	        let should_mark = unsafe { (&*world).archetype_component::<B>(entity) };
   609	        if should_mark.is_some() {
   610	            // Safety: query execution ensures exclusive mutable world access for this query form.
   611	            let _ = unsafe { (&mut *world).get_mut::<B>(entity) };
   612	        }
   613	    }
   614	
   615	    unsafe fn fetch<'w>(world: *mut World, entity: Entity) -> Option<Self::Item<'w>> {
   616	        assert_ne!(
   617	            TypeId::of::<A>(),
   618	            TypeId::of::<B>(),
   619	            "read/optional mutable query requires distinct component types",
   620	        );
   621	
   622	        let world_mut = unsafe { &mut *world };
   623	        let a = world_mut.archetype_component::<A>(entity)? as *const A;
   624	        let b = world_mut
   625	            .archetype_component_mut_untracked::<B>(entity)
   626	            .map(|value| value as *mut B);
   627	
   628	        // Safety: read/optional mutable query access requires distinct component types.
   629	        Some(unsafe { (&*a, b.map(|ptr| &mut *ptr)) })
   630	    }
   631	
   632	    unsafe fn world_ref<'w>(world: *mut World) -> Self::WorldRef<'w> {
   633	        unsafe { &mut *world }
   634	    }
   635	}
   636	
   637	impl<A: Component, B: Component> QueryData for (&mut A, Option<&mut B>) {
   638	    type Item<'w> = (&'w mut A, Option<&'w mut B>);
   639	    type WorldRef<'w> = &'w mut World;
   640	
   641	    fn query_types() -> Vec<TypeId> {
   642	        vec![TypeId::of::<A>()]
   643	    }
   644	
   645	    fn append_access(access: &mut QueryAccess) {
   646	        access.add_component_write::<A>();
   647	        access.add_component_write::<B>();
   648	    }
   649	
   650	    fn mark_changed(world: *mut World, entity: Entity) {
   651	        // Safety: query execution ensures exclusive mutable world access for this query form.
   652	        let world_mut = unsafe { &mut *world };
   653	        let _ = world_mut.get_mut::<A>(entity);
   654	        if world_mut.get::<B>(entity).is_some() {
   655	            let _ = world_mut.get_mut::<B>(entity);
   656	        }
   657	    }
   658	
   659	    unsafe fn fetch<'w>(world: *mut World, entity: Entity) -> Option<Self::Item<'w>> {
   660	        assert_ne!(
   661	            TypeId::of::<A>(),
   662	            TypeId::of::<B>(),
   663	            "mutable/optional mutable query requires distinct component types",
   664	        );
   665	
   666	        let world_mut = unsafe { &mut *world };
   667	        let b = world_mut
   668	            .archetype_component_mut_untracked::<B>(entity)
   669	            .map(|value| value as *mut B);
   670	        let a = world_mut.archetype_component_mut_untracked::<A>(entity)? as *mut A;
   671	
   672	        // Safety: mutable/optional mutable query access requires distinct component types.
   673	        Some(unsafe { (&mut *a, b.map(|ptr| &mut *ptr)) })
   674	    }
   675	
   676	    unsafe fn world_ref<'w>(world: *mut World) -> Self::WorldRef<'w> {
   677	        unsafe { &mut *world }
   678	    }
   679	}
   680	
   681	impl<T: Component> QueryData for (Entity, Option<&T>) {
   682	    type Item<'w> = (Entity, Option<&'w T>);
   683	    type WorldRef<'w> = &'w World;
   684	
   685	    fn query_types() -> Vec<TypeId> {
   686	        Vec::new()
   687	    }
   688	
   689	    fn append_access(access: &mut QueryAccess) {
   690	        access.add_component_read::<T>();
   691	    }
   692	
   693	    unsafe fn fetch<'w>(world: *mut World, entity: Entity) -> Option<Self::Item<'w>> {
   694	        let value = unsafe { (&*world).archetype_component::<T>(entity) };
   695	        Some((entity, value))
   696	    }
   697	
   698	    unsafe fn world_ref<'w>(world: *mut World) -> Self::WorldRef<'w> {
   699	        unsafe { &*world }
   700	    }
   701	}

   703	impl<A: Component, B: Component, C: Component> QueryData for (&A, &B, &C) {
   704	    type Item<'w> = (&'w A, &'w B, &'w C);
   705	    type WorldRef<'w> = &'w World;
   706	
   707	    fn query_types() -> Vec<TypeId> {
   708	        vec![TypeId::of::<A>(), TypeId::of::<B>(), TypeId::of::<C>()]
   709	    }
   710	
   711	    fn append_access(access: &mut QueryAccess) {
   712	        access.add_component_read::<A>();
   713	        access.add_component_read::<B>();
   714	        access.add_component_read::<C>();
   715	    }
   716	
   717	    unsafe fn fetch<'w>(world: *mut World, entity: Entity) -> Option<Self::Item<'w>> {
   718	        let a = unsafe { (&*world).archetype_component::<A>(entity) }?;
   719	        let b = unsafe { (&*world).archetype_component::<B>(entity) }?;
   720	        let c = unsafe { (&*world).archetype_component::<C>(entity) }?;
   721	        Some((a, b, c))
   722	    }
   723	
   724	    unsafe fn world_ref<'w>(world: *mut World) -> Self::WorldRef<'w> {
   725	        unsafe { &*world }
   726	    }
   727	}

   729	impl<A: Component, B: Component, C: Component> QueryData for (&mut A, &B, &C) {
   730	    type Item<'w> = (&'w mut A, &'w B, &'w C);
   731	    type WorldRef<'w> = &'w mut World;
   732	
   733	    fn query_types() -> Vec<TypeId> {
   734	        vec![TypeId::of::<A>(), TypeId::of::<B>(), TypeId::of::<C>()]
   735	    }
   736	
   737	    fn append_access(access: &mut QueryAccess) {
   738	        access.add_component_write::<A>();
   739	        access.add_component_read::<B>();
   740	        access.add_component_read::<C>();
   741	    }
   742	
   743	    fn mark_changed(world: *mut World, entity: Entity) {
   744	        // Safety: query execution ensures exclusive mutable world access for this query form.
   745	        let _ = unsafe { (&mut *world).get_mut::<A>(entity) };
   746	    }
   747	
   748	    unsafe fn fetch<'w>(world: *mut World, entity: Entity) -> Option<Self::Item<'w>> {
   749	        assert_ne!(
   750	            TypeId::of::<A>(),
   751	            TypeId::of::<B>(),
   752	            "mutable/read tuple query requires distinct component types",
   753	        );
   754	        assert_ne!(
   755	            TypeId::of::<A>(),
   756	            TypeId::of::<C>(),
   757	            "mutable/read tuple query requires distinct component types",
   758	        );
   759	
   760	        let world_mut = unsafe { &mut *world };
   761	        let b = world_mut.archetype_component::<B>(entity)? as *const B;
   762	        let c = world_mut.archetype_component::<C>(entity)? as *const C;
   763	        let a = world_mut.archetype_component_mut_untracked::<A>(entity)? as *mut A;
   764	
   765	        // Safety: mutable/read tuple query access requires distinct component types.
   766	        Some(unsafe { (&mut *a, &*b, &*c) })
   767	    }
   768	
   769	    unsafe fn world_ref<'w>(world: *mut World) -> Self::WorldRef<'w> {
   770	        unsafe { &mut *world }
   771	    }
   772	}

   774	impl<A: Component, B: Component, C: Component> QueryData for (&mut A, &mut B, &C) {
   775	    type Item<'w> = (&'w mut A, &'w mut B, &'w C);
   776	    type WorldRef<'w> = &'w mut World;
   777	
   778	    fn query_types() -> Vec<TypeId> {
   779	        vec![TypeId::of::<A>(), TypeId::of::<B>(), TypeId::of::<C>()]
   780	    }

   783	        access.add_component_write::<A>();
   784	        access.add_component_write::<B>();
   785	        access.add_component_read::<C>();
   786	    }
   787	
   788	    fn mark_changed(world: *mut World, entity: Entity) {
   789	        // Safety: query execution ensures exclusive mutable world access for this query form.
   790	        let world_mut = unsafe { &mut *world };
   791	        let _ = world_mut.get_mut::<A>(entity);
   792	        let _ = world_mut.get_mut::<B>(entity);
   793	    }

   796	        assert_ne!(

   800	        );

   804	            "mutable/read tuple query requires distinct component types",
   805	        );
   806	        assert_ne!(

   808	            TypeId::of::<C>(),
   809	            "mutable/read tuple query requires distinct component types",
   810	        );

   814	        let a = world_mut.archetype_component_mut_untracked::<A>(entity)? as *mut A;
   815	        let b = world_mut.archetype_component_mut_untracked::<B>(entity)? as *mut B;

   818	        Some(unsafe { (&mut *a, &mut *b, &*c) })
   819	    }

   822	        unsafe { &mut *world }
   823	    }

    16	pub trait QueryData {
    17	    type Item<'w>;
    18	    type WorldRef<'w>: QueryWorldRef<'w>;
    19	
    20	    fn query_types() -> Vec<TypeId>;
    21	    fn append_access(access: &mut QueryAccess);
    22	
    23	    fn mark_changed(_world: *mut World, _entity: Entity) {}
    24	
    25	    /// Enables cached mark/fetch hooks that avoid per-entity setup work inside the iterator loop.
    26	    fn supports_fast_path() -> bool {
    27	        false
    28	    }
    29	
    30	    fn prepare_fast_cache(_world: *mut World, _cache: &mut QueryFastCache) -> bool {
    31	        false
    32	    }
    33	
    34	    fn mark_changed_fast(world: *mut World, entity: Entity, _cache: &mut QueryFastCache) {
    35	        Self::mark_changed(world, entity);
    36	    }
    37	
    38	    /// Enables archetype-row execution instead of the entity-list fallback path.
    39	    fn supports_archetype_execution() -> bool {
    40	        false
    41	    }
    42	
    43	    fn collect_archetype_rows(
    44	        _world: *mut World,
    45	        _required_present: &[TypeId],
    46	        _excluded: &[TypeId],
    47	        _rows: &mut Vec<QueryArchetypeRow>,
    48	        _cache: &mut QueryFastCache,
    49	    ) -> bool {
    50	        false
    51	    }
    52	
    53	    /// Safety: the caller must uphold the access guarantees described by `Self::append_access`.
    54	    unsafe fn fetch<'w>(world: *mut World, entity: Entity) -> Option<Self::Item<'w>>;
    55	
    56	    /// Safety: the caller must uphold the access guarantees described by `Self::append_access`.
    57	    unsafe fn fetch_fast<'w>(
    58	        world: *mut World,
    59	        entity: Entity,
    60	        _cache: &mut QueryFastCache,
    61	    ) -> Option<Self::Item<'w>> {
    62	        unsafe { Self::fetch(world, entity) }
    63	    }
    64	
    65	    /// Safety: `world` must point to a valid world for the returned borrow lifetime.
    66	    unsafe fn world_ref<'w>(world: *mut World) -> Self::WorldRef<'w>;
    67	}

    72	    type WorldRef<'w>: QueryWorldRef<'w>;

    79	
    80	    #[doc(hidden)]

    82

    85	
    86	    #[doc(hidden)]
    87	    fn prepare_fast_cache(world: *mut World, cache: &mut QueryFastCache) -> bool;
    88	
    89	    #[doc(hidden)]

    91	
    92	    #[doc(hidden)]

    97	        world: *mut World,
    98	        required_present: &[TypeId],
    99	        excluded: &[TypeId],
   100	        rows: &mut Vec<QueryArchetypeRow>,
   101	        cache: &mut QueryFastCache,
   102	    ) -> bool;
   103	
   104	    /// # Safety
   105	    /// The caller must uphold the access guarantees described by `Self::append_access`.
   106	    #[doc(hidden)]

   108

   193	        self as *const World as *mut World
   194	    }
   195	}

   210	#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default)]
   211	pub struct QueryFastCache {
   212	    // Tracks cache ownership across reused `QueryState` runs and cross-world rebinding.
   213	    pub(crate) world_ptr: *const World,
   214	    // Reused archetype bindings for archetype-row execution forms.
   215	    pub(crate) archetype_bindings: Vec<ArchetypeExecutionBinding>,
   216	}
   217	
   218	pub struct QueryState<Q, F = ()> {
   219	    required_present: Vec<TypeId>,
   220	    excluded: Vec<TypeId>,
   221	    access: QueryAccess,
   222	    last_run_tick: Cell<u64>,
   223	    scratch_pool: Rc<RefCell<Vec<Vec<Entity>>>>,
   224	    archetype_row_scratch_pool: Rc<RefCell<Vec<Vec<QueryArchetypeRow>>>>,
   225	    fast_fetch_enabled: bool,
   226	    archetype_execution_enabled: bool,
   227	    fast_cache: RefCell<QueryFastCache>,
   228	    _marker: PhantomData<(Q, F)>,
   229	}
   230	
   231	impl<Q: QuerySpec, F: QueryFilter> QueryState<Q, F> {
   232	    pub fn new(_world: &World) -> Self {
   233	        Self::detached()
   234	    }
   235	
   236	    pub fn access(&self) -> &QueryAccess {
   237	        &self.access
   238	    }
   239	
   240	    pub fn with<T: Component>(mut self) -> Self {
   241	        push_unique_type(&mut self.required_present, TypeId::of::<T>());
   242	        self
   243	    }
   244	
   245	    pub fn without<T: Component>(mut self) -> Self {
   246	        push_unique_type(&mut self.excluded, TypeId::of::<T>());
   247	        self
   248	    }
   249	
   250	    pub fn iter<'w>(&self, world: Q::WorldRef<'w>) -> impl Iterator<Item = Q::Item<'w>> + 'w
   251	    where
   252	        Q: 'w,
   253	    {
   254	        let start = Instant::now();
   255	        let world_ptr = world.into_world_ptr();
   256	        let world_ref = unsafe { &*world_ptr };
   257	        let since_tick = self.last_run_tick.get();
   258	        let (use_fast_fetch, mut fast_cache) = self.prepare_fast_fetch(world_ptr);
   259	
   260	        if self.archetype_execution_enabled {
   261	            let mut rows = self.acquire_archetype_row_vec();
   262	            if Q::collect_archetype_rows(
   263	                world_ptr,
   264	                &self.required_present,
   265	                &self.excluded,
   266	                &mut rows,
   267	                &mut fast_cache,
   268	            ) {
   269	                if F::needs_tick_filter() {
   270	                    rows.retain(|row| F::matches_entity(world_ref, row.entity, since_tick));
   271	                }
   272	                self.last_run_tick.set(world_ref.current_change_tick());
   273	                telemetry::record_query_iter(start.elapsed().as_nanos() as u64);
   274	                return QueryIter::<Q> {
   275	                    world: world_ptr,
   276	                    entities: None,
   277	                    archetype_rows: Some(rows),
   278	                    scratch_pool: Rc::clone(&self.scratch_pool),
   279	                    archetype_row_scratch_pool: Rc::clone(&self.archetype_row_scratch_pool),
   280	                    use_fast_fetch,
   281	                    fast_cache,
   282	                    index: 0,
   283	                    _marker: PhantomData,
   284	                };
   285	            }
   286	            self.release_archetype_row_vec(rows);
   287	        }
   288	
   289	        let mut entities = self.acquire_scratch_vec();
   290	        // Fallback path for query forms that do not support archetype-row execution.
   291	        self.matching_entities_into(world_ref, &mut entities);
   292	        self.last_run_tick.set(world_ref.current_change_tick());
   293	        telemetry::record_query_iter(start.elapsed().as_nanos() as u64);
   294	        QueryIter::<Q> {
   295	            world: world_ptr,
   296	            entities: Some(entities),
   297	            archetype_rows: None,
   298	            scratch_pool: Rc::clone(&self.scratch_pool),
   299	            archetype_row_scratch_pool: Rc::clone(&self.archetype_row_scratch_pool),
   300	            use_fast_fetch,
   301	            fast_cache,
   302	            index: 0,
   303	            _marker: PhantomData,
   304	        }
   305	    }
   306	
   307	    pub fn get<'w>(&self, world: Q::WorldRef<'w>, entity: Entity) -> Option<Q::Item<'w>> {
   308	        let start = Instant::now();
   309	        let world_ptr = world.into_world_ptr();
   310	        let world_ref = unsafe { &*world_ptr };
   311	        let matches = self.matches_entity(world_ref, entity);
   312	        self.last_run_tick.set(world_ref.current_change_tick());
   313	        if !matches {
   314	            telemetry::record_query_get(start.elapsed().as_nanos() as u64);
   315	            return None;
   316	        }
   317	        Q::mark_changed(world_ptr, entity);
   318	        // Safety: access conflicts are guarded by the query type and runtime.
   319	        let item = unsafe { Q::fetch(world_ptr, entity) };
   320	        telemetry::record_query_get(start.elapsed().as_nanos() as u64);
   321	        item
   322	    }
   323	
   324	    pub fn single<'w>(&self, world: Q::WorldRef<'w>) -> Result<Q::Item<'w>, QueryError> {
   325	        let start = Instant::now();
   326	        let world_ptr = world.into_world_ptr();
   327	        let world_ref = unsafe { &*world_ptr };
   328	        let mut entities = self.acquire_scratch_vec();
   329	        self.matching_entities_into(world_ref, &mut entities);
   330	        self.last_run_tick.set(world_ref.current_change_tick());
   331	        if entities.is_empty() {
   332	            self.release_scratch_vec(entities);
   333	            telemetry::record_query_single(start.elapsed().as_nanos() as u64);
   334	            return Err(QueryError::NoResults);
   335	        }
   336	        if entities.len() > 1 {
   337	            let count = entities.len();
   338	            self.release_scratch_vec(entities);
   339	            telemetry::record_query_single(start.elapsed().as_nanos() as u64);
   340	            return Err(QueryError::MultipleResults { count });
   341	        }
   342	        Q::mark_changed(world_ptr, entities[0]);
   343	        // Safety: exactly one matching entity exists and query access rules are upheld.
   344	        let result = unsafe { Q::fetch(world_ptr, entities[0]) }.ok_or(QueryError::NoResults);
   345	        self.release_scratch_vec(entities);
   346	        telemetry::record_query_single(start.elapsed().as_nanos() as u64);
   347	        result
   348	    }
   349	
   350	    pub(crate) fn detached() -> Self {
   351	        let query_types = Q::query_types();
   352	        let mut required = Vec::new();
   353	        let mut excluded = Vec::new();
   354	        F::configure(&mut required, &mut excluded);
   355	        let mut required_present = query_types.clone();
   356	        for type_id in &required {
   357	            push_unique_type(&mut required_present, *type_id);
   358	        }
   359	
   360	        let mut access = QueryAccess::default();
   361	        Q::append_access(&mut access);
   362	        F::append_access(&mut access);
   363	
   364	        Self {
   365	            required_present,
   366	            excluded,
   367	            access,
   368	            last_run_tick: Cell::new(0),
   369	            scratch_pool: Rc::new(RefCell::new(Vec::new())),
   370	            archetype_row_scratch_pool: Rc::new(RefCell::new(Vec::new())),
   371	            fast_fetch_enabled: Q::supports_fast_path(),
   372	            archetype_execution_enabled: Q::supports_archetype_execution(),
   373	            fast_cache: RefCell::new(QueryFastCache::default()),
   374	            _marker: PhantomData,
   375	        }
   376	    }
   377	
   378	    fn prepare_fast_fetch(&self, world_ptr: *mut World) -> (bool, QueryFastCache) {
   379	        if !self.fast_fetch_enabled {
   380	            return (false, QueryFastCache::default());
   381	        }
   382	
   383	        let mut cache = self.fast_cache.borrow_mut();
   384	        let prepared = Q::prepare_fast_cache(world_ptr, &mut cache);
   385	        (prepared, cache.clone())
   386	    }
   387	
   388	    fn matching_entities_into(&self, world: &World, out: &mut Vec<Entity>) {
   389	        let since_tick = self.last_run_tick.get();
   390	        world.matching_entities_into(&self.required_present, &self.excluded, out);
   391	        if F::needs_tick_filter() {
   392	            out.retain(|entity| F::matches_entity(world, *entity, since_tick));
   393	        }
   394	    }
   395	
   396	    fn matches_entity(&self, world: &World, entity: Entity) -> bool {
   397	        let since_tick = self.last_run_tick.get();
   398	        world.entity_matches_component_constraints(entity, &self.required_present, &self.excluded)
   399	            && (!F::needs_tick_filter() || F::matches_entity(world, entity, since_tick))
   400	    }
   401	
   402	    fn acquire_scratch_vec(&self) -> Vec<Entity> {
   403	        self.scratch_pool.borrow_mut().pop().unwrap_or_default()
   404	    }
   405	
   406	    fn release_scratch_vec(&self, mut entities: Vec<Entity>) {
   407	        entities.clear();
   408	        let mut pool = self.scratch_pool.borrow_mut();
   409	        if pool.len() < 4 {
   410	            pool.push(entities);
   411	        }
   412	    }
   413	
   414	    fn acquire_archetype_row_vec(&self) -> Vec<QueryArchetypeRow> {
   415	        self.archetype_row_scratch_pool
   416	            .borrow_mut()
   417	            .pop()
   418	            .unwrap_or_default()
   419	    }
   420	
   421	    fn release_archetype_row_vec(&self, mut rows: Vec<QueryArchetypeRow>) {
   422	        rows.clear();
   423	        let mut pool = self.archetype_row_scratch_pool.borrow_mut();
   424	        if pool.len() < 4 {
   425	            pool.push(rows);
   426	        }
   427	    }
   428	}
   429	
   430	pub struct Query<Q, F = ()> {
   431	    world: NonNull<World>,
   432	    state: NonNull<QueryState<Q, F>>,
   433	    _marker: PhantomData<(Q, F)>,
   434	}
   435	
   436	impl<Q, F> Query<Q, F> {
   437	    pub(crate) fn new(world: *mut World, state: &mut QueryState<Q, F>) -> Self {
   438	        Self {
   439	            world: NonNull::new(world).expect("world pointer must not be null"),
   440	            state: NonNull::from(state),
   441	            _marker: PhantomData,
   442	        }
   443	    }
   444	}
   445	
   446	impl<Q: QuerySpec, F: QueryFilter> Query<Q, F> {
   447	    pub fn access(&self) -> &QueryAccess {
   448	        unsafe { self.state.as_ref().access() }
   449	    }
   450	
   451	    pub fn iter(&mut self) -> impl Iterator<Item = Q::Item<'_>> + '_ {
   452	        // Safety: system execution guarantees the world pointer remains valid for this call.
   453	        unsafe { self.state.as_ref().iter(Q::world_ref(self.world.as_ptr())) }
   454	    }
   455	
   456	    pub fn get(&mut self, entity: Entity) -> Option<Q::Item<'_>> {
   457	        // Safety: system execution guarantees the world pointer remains valid for this call.
   458	        unsafe {
   459	            self.state
   460	                .as_ref()
   461	                .get(Q::world_ref(self.world.as_ptr()), entity)
   462	        }
   463	    }
   464	
   465	    pub fn single(&mut self) -> Result<Q::Item<'_>, QueryError> {
   466	        // Safety: system execution guarantees the world pointer remains valid for this call.
   467	        unsafe {
   468	            self.state
   469	                .as_ref()
   470	                .single(Q::world_ref(self.world.as_ptr()))
   471	        }
   472	    }
   473	}
   474	
   475	struct QueryIter<'w, Q: QuerySpec> {
   476	    world: *mut World,
   477	    entities: Option<Vec<Entity>>,
   478	    archetype_rows: Option<Vec<QueryArchetypeRow>>,
   479	    scratch_pool: Rc<RefCell<Vec<Vec<Entity>>>>,
   480	    archetype_row_scratch_pool: Rc<RefCell<Vec<Vec<QueryArchetypeRow>>>>,
   481	    use_fast_fetch: bool,
   482	    fast_cache: QueryFastCache,
   483	    index: usize,
   484	    _marker: PhantomData<Q::WorldRef<'w>>,
   485	}
   486	
   487	impl<'w, Q: QuerySpec> QueryIter<'w, Q> {
   488	    fn mark_and_fetch(&mut self, entity: Entity) -> Option<Q::Item<'w>> {
   489	        if self.use_fast_fetch {
   490	            Q::mark_changed_fast(self.world, entity, &mut self.fast_cache);
   491	            // Safety: `QueryIter` holds the world borrow contract through `Q::WorldRef<'w>`.
   492	            return unsafe { Q::fetch_fast(self.world, entity, &mut self.fast_cache) };
   493	        }
   494	
   495	        Q::mark_changed(self.world, entity);
   496	        // Safety: `QueryIter` holds the world borrow contract through `Q::WorldRef<'w>`.
   497	        unsafe { Q::fetch(self.world, entity) }
   498	    }
   499	}
   500	
   501	impl<'w, Q: QuerySpec> Iterator for QueryIter<'w, Q> {
   502	    type Item = Q::Item<'w>;
   503	
   504	    fn next(&mut self) -> Option<Self::Item> {
   505	        if let Some(rows) = self.archetype_rows.as_ref() {
   506	            let rows_ptr = rows.as_ptr();
   507	            let rows_len = rows.len();
   508	
   509	            while self.index < rows_len {
   510	                // Safety: `self.index < rows_len` and `rows_ptr` points to `rows`.
   511	                let row = unsafe { *rows_ptr.add(self.index) };
   512	                self.index += 1;
   513	                if let Some(item) = self.mark_and_fetch(row.entity) {
   514	                    return Some(item);
   515	                }
   516	            }
   517	            return None;
   518	        }
   519	
   520	        let Some(entities) = self.entities.as_ref() else {
   521	            return None;
   522	        };
   523	        let entities_ptr = entities.as_ptr();
   524	        let entities_len = entities.len();
   525	
   526	        while self.index < entities_len {
   527	            // Safety: `self.index < entities_len` and `entities_ptr` points to `entities`.
   528	            let entity = unsafe { *entities_ptr.add(self.index) };
   529	            self.index += 1;
   530	            if let Some(item) = self.mark_and_fetch(entity) {
   531	                return Some(item);
   532	            }
   533	        }
   534	        None
   535	    }
   536	}
   537	
   538	impl<'w, Q: QuerySpec> Drop for QueryIter<'w, Q> {
   539	    fn drop(&mut self) {
   540	        if let Some(mut entities) = self.entities.take() {
   541	            entities.clear();
   542	            let mut pool = self.scratch_pool.borrow_mut();
   543	            if pool.len() < 4 {
   544	                pool.push(entities);
   545	            }
   546	        }
   547	
   548	        if let Some(mut rows) = self.archetype_rows.take() {
   549	            rows.clear();
   550	            let mut pool = self.archetype_row_scratch_pool.borrow_mut();
   551	            if pool.len() < 4 {
   552	                pool.push(rows);
   553	            }
   554	        }
   555	    }
   556	}

     1	// Owner: ecs Storage - Entity to Archetype Location Map
     2	use super::ArchetypeId;
     3	use crate::entity::Entity;
     4	use std::collections::HashMap;
     5	
     6	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]
     7	pub(crate) struct EntityLocation {
     8	    pub(crate) archetype_id: ArchetypeId,
     9	    pub(crate) row: usize,
    10	}
    11	
    12	#[derive(Debug, Default)]
    13	pub(crate) struct EntityLocationMap {
    14	    entries: HashMap<Entity, EntityLocation>,
    15	}
    16	
    17	impl EntityLocationMap {
    18	    pub(crate) fn get(&self, entity: Entity) -> Option<EntityLocation> {
    19	        self.entries.get(&entity).copied()
    20	    }
    21	
    22	    pub(crate) fn insert(&mut self, entity: Entity, location: EntityLocation) {
    23	        self.entries.insert(entity, location);
    24	    }
    25	
    26	    pub(crate) fn remove(&mut self, entity: Entity) -> Option<EntityLocation> {
    27	        self.entries.remove(&entity)
    28	    }
    29	}
    30	
    31	#[cfg(test)]
    32	mod tests {
    33	    use super::*;
    34	
    35	    #[test]
    36	    fn location_map_insert_lookup_and_remove() {
    37	        let mut map = EntityLocationMap::default();
    38	        let entity = Entity {
    39	            id: 10,
    40	            generation: 0,
    41	        };
    42	        let location = EntityLocation {
    43	            archetype_id: ArchetypeId::new(2),
    44	            row: 4,
    45	        };
    46	
    47	        assert!(map.get(entity).is_none());
    48	        map.insert(entity, location);
    49	        assert_eq!(map.get(entity), Some(location));
    50	        assert_eq!(map.remove(entity), Some(location));
    51	        assert!(map.get(entity).is_none());
    52	    }
    53	}

     1	// Owner: ecs Storage - Archetype Registry, Matching, and Typed Column Storage
     2	use super::{EntityLocation, EntityLocationMap};
     3	use crate::component::Component;
     4	use crate::entity::Entity;
     5	use crate::storage::dense::{DenseColumn, DenseEntityColumn, DenseRowMetadata};

     9	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]
    10	pub(crate) struct ArchetypeExecutionBinding {
    11	    pub(crate) archetype_index: usize,
    12	    pub(crate) row_count: usize,
    13	}
    14	
    15	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]
    16	pub(crate) struct ArchetypeId(usize);
    17	
    18	impl ArchetypeId {
    19	    pub(crate) const fn new(index: usize) -> Self {
    20	        Self(index)
    21	    }
    22	
    23	    pub(crate) const fn index(self) -> usize {
    24	        self.0
    25	    }
    26	}
    27	
    28	#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]
    29	struct ArchetypeKey {
    30	    component_types: Vec<TypeId>,
    31	}
    32	
    33	impl ArchetypeKey {
    34	    fn new(component_types: &[TypeId]) -> Self {
    35	        let mut canonical = component_types.to_vec();
    36	        canonical.sort_unstable();
    37	        canonical.dedup();
    38	        Self {
    39	            component_types: canonical,
    40	        }
    41	    }
    42	
    43	    fn component_types(&self) -> &[TypeId] {
    44	        &self.component_types
    45	    }
    46	
    47	    fn contains(&self, type_id: TypeId) -> bool {
    48	        self.component_types.binary_search(&type_id).is_ok()
    49	    }
    50	}
    51	
    52	struct ErasedDenseRow {
    53	    value: Box<dyn Any>,
    54	    metadata: DenseRowMetadata,
    55	}
    56	
    57	impl ErasedDenseRow {
    58	    fn new_added<T: Component>(value: T, tick: u64, state_generation: u64) -> Self {
    59	        Self {
    60	            value: Box::new(Box::new(value)),
    61	            metadata: DenseRowMetadata::new(tick, tick, state_generation, 0),
    62	        }
    63	    }
    64	
    65	    fn into_typed_value<T: Component>(self) -> T {
    66	        let boxed = self
    67	            .value
    68	            .downcast::<Box<T>>()
    69	            .expect("archetype row value type mismatch");
    70	        **boxed
    71	    }
    72	}
    73	
    74	trait ArchetypeComponentColumn {
    75	    fn len(&self) -> usize;
    76	    fn get_ptr(&self, row: usize) -> Option<*const ()>;
    77	    fn get_mut_ptr(&mut self, row: usize) -> Option<*mut ()>;
    78	    fn metadata(&self, row: usize) -> Option<DenseRowMetadata>;
    79	    fn mark_changed(&mut self, row: usize, tick: u64) -> bool;
    80	    fn mark_stateful_changed(&mut self, row: usize, tick: u64) -> bool;
    81	    fn push_erased(&mut self, row: ErasedDenseRow);
    82	    fn swap_remove_erased(&mut self, row: usize) -> Option<ErasedDenseRow>;
    83	}
    84	
    85	struct TypedArchetypeColumn<T: Component> {
    86	    dense: DenseColumn<T>,
    87	}
    88	
    89	impl<T: Component> Default for TypedArchetypeColumn<T> {
    90	    fn default() -> Self {
    91	        Self {
    92	            dense: DenseColumn::default(),
    93	        }
    94	    }
    95	}
    96	
    97	impl<T: Component> ArchetypeComponentColumn for TypedArchetypeColumn<T> {
    98	    fn len(&self) -> usize {
    99	        self.dense.len()
   100	    }
   101	
   102	    fn get_ptr(&self, row: usize) -> Option<*const ()> {
   103	        self.dense.get_ptr(row).map(|ptr| ptr.cast::<()>())
   104	    }
   105	
   106	    fn get_mut_ptr(&mut self, row: usize) -> Option<*mut ()> {
   107	        self.dense.get_mut_ptr(row).map(|ptr| ptr.cast::<()>())
   108	    }
   109	
   110	    fn metadata(&self, row: usize) -> Option<DenseRowMetadata> {
   111	        self.dense.metadata(row)
   112	    }
   113	
   114	    fn mark_changed(&mut self, row: usize, tick: u64) -> bool {
   115	        self.dense.mark_changed(row, tick)
   116	    }
   117	
   118	    fn mark_stateful_changed(&mut self, row: usize, tick: u64) -> bool {
   119	        self.dense.mark_stateful_changed(row, tick)
   120	    }
   121	
   122	    fn push_erased(&mut self, row: ErasedDenseRow) {
   123	        let value = row
   124	            .value
   125	            .downcast::<Box<T>>()
   126	            .expect("archetype row value type mismatch");
   127	        let _ = self.dense.push_boxed(*value, row.metadata);
   128	    }
   129	
   130	    fn swap_remove_erased(&mut self, row: usize) -> Option<ErasedDenseRow> {
   131	        let removed = self.dense.swap_remove_boxed(row)?;
   132	        Some(ErasedDenseRow {
   133	            value: Box::new(removed.removed_value),
   134	            metadata: removed.removed_metadata,
   135	        })
   136	    }
   137	}
   138	
   139	type ColumnFactory = fn() -> Box<dyn ArchetypeComponentColumn>;
   140	
   141	fn typed_column_factory<T: Component>() -> Box<dyn ArchetypeComponentColumn> {
   142	    Box::new(TypedArchetypeColumn::<T>::default())
   143	}
   144	
   145	struct ArchetypeRecord {
   146	    key: ArchetypeKey,
   147	    entities: DenseEntityColumn,
   148	    columns: HashMap<TypeId, Box<dyn ArchetypeComponentColumn>>,
   149	}
   150	
   151	impl ArchetypeRecord {
   152	    fn new(key: ArchetypeKey) -> Self {
   153	        Self {
   154	            key,
   155	            entities: DenseEntityColumn::default(),
   156	            columns: HashMap::new(),
   157	        }
   158	    }
   159	
   160	    fn matches_constraints(&self, required: &[TypeId], excluded: &[TypeId]) -> bool {
   161	        required.iter().all(|type_id| self.key.contains(*type_id))
   162	            && excluded.iter().all(|type_id| !self.key.contains(*type_id))
   163	    }
   164	}
   165	
   166	#[derive(Default)]
   167	pub(crate) struct ArchetypeRegistry {
   168	    archetypes: Vec<ArchetypeRecord>,
   169	    key_to_id: HashMap<ArchetypeKey, ArchetypeId>,
   170	    column_factories: HashMap<TypeId, ColumnFactory>,
   171	    component_state_generations: HashMap<(Entity, TypeId), u64>,
   172	}
   173	
   174	impl ArchetypeRegistry {
   175	    pub(crate) fn new() -> Self {
   176	        let mut registry = Self::default();
   177	        let empty = ArchetypeKey::new(&[]);
   178	        let empty_id = ArchetypeId::new(0);
   179	        registry.key_to_id.insert(empty.clone(), empty_id);
   180	        registry.archetypes.push(ArchetypeRecord::new(empty));
   181	        registry
   182	    }
   183	
   184	    pub(crate) fn register_component_type<T: Component>(&mut self) {
   185	        self.column_factories
   186	            .entry(TypeId::of::<T>())
   187	            .or_insert(typed_column_factory::<T>);
   188	    }
   189	
   190	    pub(crate) fn component_types(&self, archetype_id: ArchetypeId) -> Option<&[TypeId]> {
   191	        self.archetypes
   192	            .get(archetype_id.index())
   193	            .map(|archetype| archetype.key.component_types())
   194	    }
   195	
   196	    pub(crate) fn component_count(&self, archetype_id: ArchetypeId) -> Option<usize> {
   197	        self.component_types(archetype_id).map(|types| types.len())
   198	    }
   199	
   200	    pub(crate) fn entity_at(&self, archetype_index: usize, row: usize) -> Option<Entity> {
   201	        self.archetypes.get(archetype_index)?.entities.get(row)
   202	    }
   203	
   204	    pub(crate) fn component_ptr<T: Component>(
   205	        &self,
   206	        entity: Entity,
   207	        locations: &EntityLocationMap,
   208	    ) -> Option<*const T> {
   209	        let location = locations.get(entity)?;
   210	        let type_id = TypeId::of::<T>();
   211	        let archetype = self.archetypes.get(location.archetype_id.index())?;
   212	        if !archetype.key.contains(type_id) {
   213	            return None;
   214	        }
   215	        let ptr = archetype.columns.get(&type_id)?.get_ptr(location.row)?;
   216	        Some(ptr.cast::<T>())
   217	    }
   218	
   219	    pub(crate) fn component_mut_ptr<T: Component>(
   220	        &mut self,
   221	        entity: Entity,
   222	        locations: &EntityLocationMap,
   223	    ) -> Option<*mut T> {
   224	        let location = locations.get(entity)?;
   225	        let type_id = TypeId::of::<T>();
   226	        let archetype = self.archetypes.get_mut(location.archetype_id.index())?;
   227	        if !archetype.key.contains(type_id) {
   228	            return None;
   229	        }
   230	        let ptr = archetype
   231	            .columns
   232	            .get_mut(&type_id)?
   233	            .get_mut_ptr(location.row)?;
   234	        Some(ptr.cast::<T>())
   235	    }
   236	
   237	    pub(crate) fn component_metadata<T: Component>(
   238	        &self,
   239	        entity: Entity,
   240	        locations: &EntityLocationMap,
   241	    ) -> Option<DenseRowMetadata> {
   242	        let location = locations.get(entity)?;
   243	        let type_id = TypeId::of::<T>();
   244	        let archetype = self.archetypes.get(location.archetype_id.index())?;
   245	        if !archetype.key.contains(type_id) {
   246	            return None;
   247	        }
   248	        archetype.columns.get(&type_id)?.metadata(location.row)
   249	    }
   250	
   251	    pub(crate) fn mark_component_changed_by_id(
   252	        &mut self,
   253	        entity: Entity,
   254	        component_type: TypeId,
   255	        tick: u64,
   256	        locations: &EntityLocationMap,
   257	    ) -> bool {
   258	        let Some(location) = locations.get(entity) else {
   259	            return false;
   260	        };
   261	        let Some(archetype) = self.archetypes.get_mut(location.archetype_id.index()) else {
   262	            return false;
   263	        };
   264	        if !archetype.key.contains(component_type) {
   265	            return false;
   266	        }
   267	        archetype
   268	            .columns
   269	            .get_mut(&component_type)
   270	            .is_some_and(|column| column.mark_changed(location.row, tick))
   271	    }
   272	
   273	    pub(crate) fn mark_component_stateful_changed_by_id(
   274	        &mut self,
   275	        entity: Entity,
   276	        component_type: TypeId,
   277	        tick: u64,
   278	        locations: &EntityLocationMap,
   279	    ) -> bool {
   280	        let Some(location) = locations.get(entity) else {
   281	            return false;
   282	        };
   283	        let Some(archetype) = self.archetypes.get_mut(location.archetype_id.index()) else {
   284	            return false;
   285	        };
   286	        if !archetype.key.contains(component_type) {
   287	            return false;
   288	        }
   289	        archetype
   290	            .columns
   291	            .get_mut(&component_type)
   292	            .is_some_and(|column| column.mark_stateful_changed(location.row, tick))
   293	    }
   294	
   295	    pub(crate) fn add_component<T: Component>(
   296	        &mut self,
   297	        entity: Entity,
   298	        value: T,
   299	        tick: u64,
   300	        locations: &mut EntityLocationMap,
   301	    ) -> bool {
   302	        let Some(current) = locations.get(entity) else {
   303	            return false;
   304	        };
   305	        let type_id = TypeId::of::<T>();
   306	        let source_types = self
   307	            .component_types(current.archetype_id)
   308	            .map(ToOwned::to_owned)
   309	            .unwrap_or_default();
   310	        if source_types.binary_search(&type_id).is_ok() {
   311	            return self.update_component::<T>(entity, value, tick, locations);
   312	        }
   313	
   314	        let mut target_types = source_types.clone();
   315	        insert_sorted_type(&mut target_types, type_id);
   316	        let target_id = self.find_or_create(&target_types);
   317	        let mut moved_rows = self.extract_rows(current, &source_types, locations);
   318	        let state_generation = self.bump_component_state_generation(entity, type_id);
   319	        moved_rows.insert(
   320	            type_id,
   321	            ErasedDenseRow::new_added(value, tick, state_generation),
   322	        );
   323	        self.append_entity_row(entity, target_id, &target_types, moved_rows, locations);
   324	        true
   325	    }
   326	
   327	    pub(crate) fn update_component<T: Component>(
   328	        &mut self,
   329	        entity: Entity,
   330	        value: T,
   331	        tick: u64,
   332	        locations: &EntityLocationMap,
   333	    ) -> bool {
   334	        let Some(location) = locations.get(entity) else {
   335	            return false;
   336	        };
   337	        let type_id = TypeId::of::<T>();
   338	        let Some(archetype) = self.archetypes.get_mut(location.archetype_id.index()) else {
   339	            return false;
   340	        };
   341	        if !archetype.key.contains(type_id) {
   342	            return false;
   343	        }
   344	        let Some(ptr) = archetype
   345	            .columns
   346	            .get_mut(&type_id)
   347	            .and_then(|column| column.get_mut_ptr(location.row))
   348	        else {
   349	            return false;
   350	        };
   351	        // Safety: type id ensures `ptr` points to `T` in the requested column row.
   352	        unsafe { *(ptr.cast::<T>()) = value };
   353	        archetype
   354	            .columns
   355	            .get_mut(&type_id)
   356	            .is_some_and(|column| column.mark_changed(location.row, tick))
   357	    }
   358	
   359	    pub(crate) fn remove_component<T: Component>(
   360	        &mut self,
   361	        entity: Entity,
   362	        locations: &mut EntityLocationMap,
   363	    ) -> Option<T> {
   364	        let current = locations.get(entity)?;
   365	        let type_id = TypeId::of::<T>();
   366	        let source_types = self
   367	            .component_types(current.archetype_id)
   368	            .map(ToOwned::to_owned)
   369	            .unwrap_or_default();
   370	        if source_types.binary_search(&type_id).is_err() {
   371	            return None;
   372	        }
   373	
   374	        let mut target_types = source_types.clone();
   375	        target_types.retain(|existing| *existing != type_id);
   376	        let target_id = self.find_or_create(&target_types);
   377	        let mut moved_rows = self.extract_rows(current, &source_types, locations);
   378	        let removed = moved_rows.remove(&type_id)?;
   379	        self.append_entity_row(entity, target_id, &target_types, moved_rows, locations);
   380	        Some(removed.into_typed_value::<T>())
   381	    }
   382	
   383	    pub(crate) fn collect_matching_bindings(
   384	        &self,
   385	        required_present: &[TypeId],
   386	        excluded: &[TypeId],
   387	        out: &mut Vec<ArchetypeExecutionBinding>,
   388	    ) -> bool {
   389	        out.clear();
   390	        for (index, archetype) in self.archetypes.iter().enumerate() {
   391	            if !archetype.matches_constraints(required_present, excluded) {
   392	                continue;
   393	            }
   394	            let row_count = archetype.entities.len();
   395	            if row_count == 0 {
   396	                continue;
   397	            }
   398	            out.push(ArchetypeExecutionBinding {
   399	                archetype_index: index,
   400	                row_count,
   401	            });
   402	        }
   403	        true
   404	    }
   405	
   406	    pub(crate) fn set_entity_components(
   407	        &mut self,
   408	        entity: Entity,
   409	        component_types: &[TypeId],
   410	        locations: &mut EntityLocationMap,
   411	    ) -> EntityLocation {
   412	        let target_id = self.find_or_create(component_types);
   413	        if let Some(current) = locations.get(entity) {
   414	            if current.archetype_id == target_id {
   415	                return current;
   416	            }
   417	            self.remove_row(current, locations);
   418	        }
   419	
   420	        let target = self
   421	            .archetypes
   422	            .get_mut(target_id.index())
   423	            .expect("target archetype must exist");
   424	        let row = target.entities.push(entity);
   425	        let location = EntityLocation {
   426	            archetype_id: target_id,
   427	            row,
   428	        };
   429	        locations.insert(entity, location);
   430	        location
   431	    }
   432	
   433	    pub(crate) fn remove_entity(
   434	        &mut self,
   435	        entity: Entity,
   436	        locations: &mut EntityLocationMap,
   437	    ) -> bool {
   438	        let Some(current) = locations.get(entity) else {
   439	            return false;
   440	        };
   441	        let source_types = self
   442	            .component_types(current.archetype_id)
   443	            .map(ToOwned::to_owned)
   444	            .unwrap_or_default();
   445	        let _ = self.extract_rows(current, &source_types, locations);
   446	        let _ = locations.remove(entity);
   447	        self.component_state_generations
   448	            .retain(|(tracked_entity, _), _| *tracked_entity != entity);
   449	        true
   450	    }
   451	
   452	    pub(crate) fn component_state_by_id(
   453	        &self,
   454	        entity: Entity,
   455	        component_type: TypeId,
   456	        locations: &EntityLocationMap,
   457	    ) -> Option<(u64, u64)> {
   458	        let location = locations.get(entity)?;
   459	        let archetype = self.archetypes.get(location.archetype_id.index())?;
   460	        if !archetype.key.contains(component_type) {
   461	            return None;
   462	        }
   463	        let metadata = archetype
   464	            .columns
   465	            .get(&component_type)?
   466	            .metadata(location.row)?;
   467	        Some((metadata.state_generation, metadata.state_version))
   468	    }
   469	
   470	    pub(crate) fn collect_matching_entities(
   471	        &self,
   472	        required_present: &[TypeId],
   473	        excluded: &[TypeId],
   474	        out: &mut Vec<Entity>,
   475	    ) -> bool {
   476	        let mut bindings = Vec::new();
   477	        let _ = self.collect_matching_bindings(required_present, excluded, &mut bindings);
   478	
   479	        out.clear();
   480	        for binding in &bindings {
   481	            for row in 0..binding.row_count {
   482	                if let Some(entity) = self.entity_at(binding.archetype_index, row) {
   483	                    out.push(entity);
   484	                }
   485	            }
   486	        }
   487	        out.sort_unstable();
   488	        true
   489	    }
   490	
   491	    fn find_or_create(&mut self, component_types: &[TypeId]) -> ArchetypeId {
   492	        let key = ArchetypeKey::new(component_types);
   493	        if let Some(existing) = self.key_to_id.get(&key).copied() {
   494	            return existing;
   495	        }
   496	
   497	        let id = ArchetypeId::new(self.archetypes.len());
   498	        self.key_to_id.insert(key.clone(), id);
   499	        self.archetypes.push(ArchetypeRecord::new(key));
   500	        id
   501	    }
   502	
   503	    fn ensure_column_for_type(&mut self, archetype_id: ArchetypeId, type_id: TypeId) {
   504	        let Some(archetype) = self.archetypes.get_mut(archetype_id.index()) else {
   505	            return;
   506	        };
   507	        if archetype.columns.contains_key(&type_id) {
   508	            return;
   509	        }
   510	        assert!(
   511	            archetype.entities.is_empty(),
   512	            "cannot create missing archetype column with existing rows"
   513	        );
   514	        let factory = self
   515	            .column_factories
   516	            .get(&type_id)
   517	            .expect("component type must be registered before archetype value storage");
   518	        archetype.columns.insert(type_id, factory());
   519	    }
   520	
   521	    fn extract_rows(
   522	        &mut self,
   523	        location: EntityLocation,
   524	        source_types: &[TypeId],
   525	        locations: &mut EntityLocationMap,
   526	    ) -> HashMap<TypeId, ErasedDenseRow> {
   527	        let Some(archetype) = self.archetypes.get_mut(location.archetype_id.index()) else {
   528	            return HashMap::new();
   529	        };
   530	        let Some(swap_remove) = archetype.entities.swap_remove(location.row) else {
   531	            return HashMap::new();
   532	        };
   533	        if let Some(moved_entity) = swap_remove.moved_entity {
   534	            locations.insert(
   535	                moved_entity,
   536	                EntityLocation {
   537	                    archetype_id: location.archetype_id,
   538	                    row: location.row,
   539	                },
   540	            );
   541	        }
   542	
   543	        let mut rows = HashMap::new();
   544	        for type_id in source_types {
   545	            if let Some(column) = archetype.columns.get_mut(type_id) {
   546	                let removed = column
   547	                    .swap_remove_erased(location.row)
   548	                    .expect("source archetype column row must exist");
   549	                rows.insert(*type_id, removed);
   550	            }
   551	        }
   552	        rows
   553	    }
   554	
   555	    fn append_entity_row(
   556	        &mut self,
   557	        entity: Entity,
   558	        archetype_id: ArchetypeId,
   559	        target_types: &[TypeId],
   560	        mut moved_rows: HashMap<TypeId, ErasedDenseRow>,
   561	        locations: &mut EntityLocationMap,
   562	    ) -> EntityLocation {
   563	        for type_id in target_types {
   564	            self.ensure_column_for_type(archetype_id, *type_id);
   565	        }
   566	
   567	        let target = self
   568	            .archetypes
   569	            .get_mut(archetype_id.index())
   570	            .expect("target archetype must exist");
   571	        let row = target.entities.push(entity);
   572	        for type_id in target_types {
   573	            let entry = moved_rows
   574	                .remove(type_id)
   575	                .expect("target archetype row value must exist");
   576	            let column = target
   577	                .columns
   578	                .get_mut(type_id)
   579	                .expect("target archetype column must exist");
   580	            assert_eq!(
   581	                column.len(),
   582	                row,
   583	                "target column row alignment must match entity row"
   584	            );
   585	            column.push_erased(entry);
   586	        }
   587	
   588	        let location = EntityLocation { archetype_id, row };
   589	        locations.insert(entity, location);
   590	        location
   591	    }
   592	
   593	    fn remove_row(&mut self, location: EntityLocation, locations: &mut EntityLocationMap) {
   594	        let source_types = self
   595	            .component_types(location.archetype_id)
   596	            .map(ToOwned::to_owned)
   597	            .unwrap_or_default();
   598	        let _ = self.extract_rows(location, &source_types, locations);
   599	    }
   600	
   601	    fn bump_component_state_generation(&mut self, entity: Entity, component_type: TypeId) -> u64 {
   602	        let generation = self
   603	            .component_state_generations
   604	            .get(&(entity, component_type))
   605	            .copied()
   606	            .unwrap_or(0)
   607	            .saturating_add(1);
   608	        self.component_state_generations
   609	            .insert((entity, component_type), generation);
   610	        generation
   611	    }
   612	}
   613	
   614	fn insert_sorted_type(component_types: &mut Vec<TypeId>, type_id: TypeId) {
   615	    match component_types.binary_search(&type_id) {
   616	        Ok(_) => {}
   617	        Err(index) => component_types.insert(index, type_id),
   618	    }
   619	}

   621	#[cfg(test)]
   622	mod tests {
   623	    use super::*;
   624	
   625	    #[test]
   626	    fn set_entity_components_moves_entity_between_archetypes_and_updates_swapped_location() {
   627	        let mut registry = ArchetypeRegistry::new();
   628	        let mut locations = EntityLocationMap::default();
   629	
   630	        let t1 = TypeId::of::<u32>();
   631	        let t2 = TypeId::of::<u64>();
   632	
   633	        let first = Entity {
   634	            id: 1,
   635	            generation: 0,
   636	        };
   637	        let second = Entity {
   638	            id: 2,
   639	            generation: 0,
   640	        };
   641	
   642	        registry.set_entity_components(first, &[t1], &mut locations);
   643	        registry.set_entity_components(second, &[t1], &mut locations);
   644	        let second_location = locations.get(second).expect("entity must have location");
   645	        assert_eq!(second_location.row, 1);
   646	
   647	        registry.set_entity_components(first, &[t1, t2], &mut locations);
   648	        let moved_second = locations
   649	            .get(second)
   650	            .expect("swapped entity should remain mapped");
   651	        assert_eq!(moved_second.row, 0);
   652	    }
   653	
   654	    #[test]
   655	    fn remove_entity_updates_swapped_row_location() {
   656	        let mut registry = ArchetypeRegistry::new();
   657	        let mut locations = EntityLocationMap::default();
   658	        let t1 = TypeId::of::<u32>();
   659	
   660	        let first = Entity {
   661	            id: 5,
   662	            generation: 0,
   663	        };
   664	        let second = Entity {
   665	            id: 6,
   666	            generation: 0,
   667	        };
   668	
   669	        registry.set_entity_components(first, &[t1], &mut locations);
   670	        registry.set_entity_components(second, &[t1], &mut locations);
   671	        assert!(registry.remove_entity(first, &mut locations));
   672	        assert!(locations.get(first).is_none());
   673	        assert_eq!(
   674	            locations.get(second),
   675	            Some(EntityLocation {
   676	                archetype_id: ArchetypeId::new(1),
   677	                row: 0,
   678	            }),
   679	        );
   680	    }
   681	
   682	    #[test]
   683	    fn remove_entity_clears_all_state_generation_entries_for_entity() {
   684	        #[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]
   685	        struct StatefulTag;
   686	        impl Component for StatefulTag {}
   687	
   688	        let mut registry = ArchetypeRegistry::new();
   689	        registry.register_component_type::<StatefulTag>();
   690	        let mut locations = EntityLocationMap::default();
   691	        let entity = Entity {
   692	            id: 42,
   693	            generation: 1,
   694	        };
   695	
   696	        registry.set_entity_components(entity, &[], &mut locations);
   697	        assert!(registry.add_component(entity, StatefulTag, 1, &mut locations));
   698	        let _: StatefulTag = registry
   699	            .remove_component(entity, &mut locations)
   700	            .expect("component should be removable");
   701	
   702	        assert!(
   703	            registry
   704	                .component_state_generations
   705	                .contains_key(&(entity, TypeId::of::<StatefulTag>()))
   706	        );
   707	        assert!(registry.remove_entity(entity, &mut locations));
   708	        assert!(
   709	            !registry
   710	                .component_state_generations
   711	                .keys()
   712	                .any(|(tracked_entity, _)| *tracked_entity == entity)
   713	        );
   714	    }
   715	}

     6	pub(crate) struct DenseRowMetadata {
     7	    pub(crate) added_tick: u64,
     8	    pub(crate) changed_tick: u64,
     9	    pub(crate) state_generation: u64,
    10	    pub(crate) state_version: u64,
    11	}

    16	        added_tick: u64,
    17	        changed_tick: u64,
    18	        state_generation: u64,
    19	        state_version: u64,

    24	            state_generation,

    26	        }

    34	    pub(crate) moved_from_row: Option<usize>,

    40	    pub(crate) removed_value: T,
    41	    pub(crate) removed_metadata: DenseRowMetadata,
    42	    pub(crate) swap: DenseSwapRemove,
    43	}

    50	    pub(crate) swap: DenseSwapRemove,

    53	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]
    54	pub(crate) struct DenseEntitySwapRemove {
    55	    pub(crate) removed_entity: Entity,
    56	    pub(crate) removed_row: usize,
    57	    pub(crate) moved_entity: Option<Entity>,
    58	    pub(crate) moved_from_row: Option<usize>,
    59	}
    60	
    61	#[allow(dead_code)]
    62	#[derive(Debug, Default)]
    63	pub(crate) struct DenseEntityColumn {
    64	    entities: Vec<Entity>,
    65	}
    66	
    67	#[allow(dead_code)]
    68	impl DenseEntityColumn {
    69	    pub(crate) fn len(&self) -> usize {
    70	        self.entities.len()
    71	    }
    72	
    73	    pub(crate) fn is_empty(&self) -> bool {
    74	        self.entities.is_empty()
    75	    }
    76	
    77	    pub(crate) fn get(&self, row: usize) -> Option<Entity> {
    78	        self.entities.get(row).copied()
    79	    }
    80	
    81	    pub(crate) fn push(&mut self, entity: Entity) -> usize {
    82	        let row = self.entities.len();
    83	        self.entities.push(entity);
    84	        row
    85	    }
    86	
    87	    pub(crate) fn iter(&self) -> impl Iterator<Item = Entity> + '_ {
    88	        self.entities.iter().copied()
    89	    }
    90	
    91	    pub(crate) fn swap_remove(&mut self, row: usize) -> Option<DenseEntitySwapRemove> {
    92	        if row >= self.entities.len() {
    93	            return None;
    94	        }
    95	
    96	        let last_row = self.entities.len().saturating_sub(1);
    97	        let removed_entity = self.entities.swap_remove(row);
    98	        let moved_entity = (row != last_row).then(|| self.entities[row]);
    99	        Some(DenseEntitySwapRemove {
   100	            removed_entity,
   101	            removed_row: row,
   102	            moved_entity,
   103	            moved_from_row: (row != last_row).then_some(last_row),
   104	        })
   105	    }
   106	}
   107	
   108	#[allow(dead_code)]
   109	#[derive(Debug)]
   110	pub(crate) struct DenseColumn<T> {
   111	    values: Vec<Box<T>>,
   112	    metadata: Vec<DenseRowMetadata>,
   113	}
   114	
   115	impl<T> Default for DenseColumn<T> {
   116	    fn default() -> Self {
   117	        Self {
   118	            values: Vec::new(),
   119	            metadata: Vec::new(),
   120	        }
   121	    }
   122	}
   123	
   124	#[allow(dead_code)]
   125	impl<T> DenseColumn<T> {
   126	    pub(crate) fn len(&self) -> usize {
   127	        self.values.len()
   128	    }
   129	
   130	    pub(crate) fn is_empty(&self) -> bool {
   131	        self.values.is_empty()
   132	    }
   133	
   134	    pub(crate) fn get(&self, row: usize) -> Option<&T> {
   135	        self.values.get(row).map(Box::as_ref)
   136	    }
   137	
   138	    pub(crate) fn get_mut(&mut self, row: usize) -> Option<&mut T> {
   139	        self.values.get_mut(row).map(Box::as_mut)
   140	    }
   141	
   142	    pub(crate) fn get_ptr(&self, row: usize) -> Option<*const T> {
   143	        self.values.get(row).map(|value| value.as_ref() as *const T)
   144	    }
   145	
   146	    pub(crate) fn get_mut_ptr(&mut self, row: usize) -> Option<*mut T> {
   147	        self.values
   148	            .get_mut(row)
   149	            .map(|value| value.as_mut() as *mut T)
   150	    }
   151	
   152	    pub(crate) fn metadata(&self, row: usize) -> Option<DenseRowMetadata> {
   153	        self.metadata.get(row).copied()
   154	    }
   155	
   156	    pub(crate) fn push(&mut self, value: T, metadata: DenseRowMetadata) -> usize {
   157	        self.push_boxed(Box::new(value), metadata)
   158	    }
   159	
   160	    pub(crate) fn push_boxed(&mut self, value: Box<T>, metadata: DenseRowMetadata) -> usize {
   161	        let row = self.values.len();
   162	        self.values.push(value);
   163	        self.metadata.push(metadata);
   164	        row
   165	    }
   166	
   167	    pub(crate) fn mark_changed(&mut self, row: usize, tick: u64) -> bool {
   168	        let Some(metadata) = self.metadata.get_mut(row) else {
   169	            return false;
   170	        };
   171	        metadata.changed_tick = tick;
   172	        true
   173	    }
   174	
   175	    pub(crate) fn mark_stateful_changed(&mut self, row: usize, tick: u64) -> bool {
   176	        let Some(metadata) = self.metadata.get_mut(row) else {
   177	            return false;
   178	        };
   179	        metadata.changed_tick = tick;
   180	        metadata.state_version = metadata.state_version.saturating_add(1);
   181	        true
   182	    }
   183	
   184	    pub(crate) fn swap_remove_boxed(
   185	        &mut self,
   186	        row: usize,
   187	    ) -> Option<DenseColumnSwapRemoveBoxed<T>> {
   188	        if row >= self.values.len() || row >= self.metadata.len() {
   189	            return None;
   190	        }
   191	
   192	        let last_row = self.values.len().saturating_sub(1);
   193	        let removed_value = self.values.swap_remove(row);
   194	        let removed_metadata = self.metadata.swap_remove(row);
   195	        Some(DenseColumnSwapRemoveBoxed {
   196	            removed_value,
   197	            removed_metadata,
   198	            swap: DenseSwapRemove {
   199	                removed_row: row,
   200	                moved_from_row: (row != last_row).then_some(last_row),
   201	            },
   202	        })
   203	    }
   204	
   205	    pub(crate) fn swap_remove(&mut self, row: usize) -> Option<DenseColumnSwapRemove<T>> {
   206	        let removed = self.swap_remove_boxed(row)?;
   207	        Some(DenseColumnSwapRemove {
   208	            removed_value: *removed.removed_value,
   209	            removed_metadata: removed.removed_metadata,
   210	            swap: removed.swap,
   211	        })
   212	    }
   213	}
   214	
   215	#[cfg(test)]
   216	mod tests {
   217	    use super::*;
   218	
   219	    #[test]
   220	    fn dense_column_swap_remove_reports_moved_row_and_preserves_alignment() {
   221	        let mut column = DenseColumn::default();
   222	        column.push(10_i32, DenseRowMetadata::new(1, 1, 1, 0));
   223	        column.push(20_i32, DenseRowMetadata::new(2, 2, 2, 0));
   224	        column.push(30_i32, DenseRowMetadata::new(3, 3, 3, 0));
   225	
   226	        let removed = column.swap_remove(1).expect("row must exist");
   227	        assert_eq!(removed.removed_value, 20);
   228	        assert_eq!(removed.removed_metadata, DenseRowMetadata::new(2, 2, 2, 0));
   229	        assert_eq!(
   230	            removed.swap,
   231	            DenseSwapRemove {
   232	                removed_row: 1,
   233	                moved_from_row: Some(2),
   234	            }
   235	        );
   236	        assert_eq!(column.len(), 2);
   237	        assert_eq!(column.get(1), Some(&30));
   238	        assert_eq!(column.metadata(1), Some(DenseRowMetadata::new(3, 3, 3, 0)));
   239	    }
   240	
   241	    #[test]
   242	    fn dense_entity_column_swap_remove_returns_moved_entity_when_needed() {
   243	        let mut column = DenseEntityColumn::default();
   244	        let first = Entity {
   245	            id: 1,
   246	            generation: 0,
   247	        };
   248	        let second = Entity {
   249	            id: 2,
   250	            generation: 0,
   251	        };
   252	        let third = Entity {
   253	            id: 3,
   254	            generation: 0,
   255	        };
   256	        column.push(first);
   257	        column.push(second);
   258	        column.push(third);
   259	
   260	        let removed = column.swap_remove(0).expect("row must exist");
   261	        assert_eq!(removed.removed_entity, first);
   262	        assert_eq!(removed.moved_entity, Some(third));
   263	        assert_eq!(removed.moved_from_row, Some(2));
   264	        assert_eq!(column.get(0), Some(third));
   265	        assert_eq!(column.len(), 2);
   266	    }
   267	}

     1	use crate::query::QueryAccess;
     2	use crate::{Commands, ResourceError, World};
     3	use thiserror::Error;
     4	
     5	#[derive(Debug, Error)]
     6	pub enum SystemParamError {
     7	    #[error(transparent)]
     8	    Resource(#[from] ResourceError),
     9	    #[error("invalid system param extraction for {param}: {reason}")]
    10	    InvalidExtraction {
    11	        param: &'static str,
    12	        reason: &'static str,
    13	    },
    14	    #[error("runtime context error: {0}")]
    15	    RuntimeContext(&'static str),
    16	}
    17	
    18	pub trait SystemParam<'w>: Sized {
    19	    type State: 'static;
    20	
    21	    fn init_state(world: &mut World) -> Result<Self::State, SystemParamError>;
    22	    fn access(state: &Self::State) -> QueryAccess;
    23	
    24	    /// `State` must be lifetime-independent for all `'w` implementations of the same
    25	    /// parameter type. Runtime state caching relies on this invariant.
    26	    ///
    27	    /// Safety: `world` and `commands` must point to live values for `'w`.
    28	    unsafe fn extract(
    29	        state: &'w mut Self::State,
    30	        world: *mut World,
    31	        commands: *mut Commands,
    32	    ) -> Result<Self, SystemParamError>;
    33	}

    90	impl<T: 'static> EventReader<T> {
    91	    pub(crate) fn new(world: *mut World) -> Self {
    92	        Self {
    93	            world: NonNull::new(world).expect("world pointer must not be null"),
    94	            _marker: PhantomData,
    95	        }
    96	    }
    97	
    98	    pub fn iter(&self) -> std::slice::Iter<'_, T> {
    99	        let start = Instant::now();
   100	        // Safety: extraction guarantees a live world pointer during system execution.
   101	        let events = unsafe { self.world.as_ref().read_events::<T>() };
   102	        telemetry::record_event_reader(start.elapsed().as_nanos() as u64, events.len() as u64);
   103	        events.iter()
   104	    }
   105	}

   107	#[derive(Debug, Default)]
   108	pub struct EventChannelState {
   109	    next_sequence: u64,
   110	}

   112	pub struct EventChannel<T: 'static> {
   113	    world: NonNull<World>,
   114	    state: NonNull<EventChannelState>,
   115	    _marker: PhantomData<T>,
   116	}
   117	
   118	impl<T: 'static> EventChannel<T> {
   119	    pub(crate) fn new(world: *mut World, state: *mut EventChannelState) -> Self {
   120	        Self {
   121	            world: NonNull::new(world).expect("world pointer must not be null"),
   122	            state: NonNull::new(state).expect("event channel state pointer must not be null"),
   123	            _marker: PhantomData,
   124	        }
   125	    }
   126	
   127	    pub fn iter_all(&self) -> std::slice::Iter<'_, T> {
   128	        let start = Instant::now();
   129	        // Safety: extraction guarantees a live world pointer during system execution.
   130	        let events = unsafe { self.world.as_ref().read_events::<T>() };
   131	        telemetry::record_event_reader(start.elapsed().as_nanos() as u64, events.len() as u64);
   132	        events.iter()
   133	    }
   134	
   135	    pub fn iter_new(&mut self) -> std::slice::Iter<'_, T> {
   136	        let start = Instant::now();
   137	        // Safety: extraction guarantees a live world pointer and param state pointer.
   138	        let state = unsafe { self.state.as_mut() };
   139	        // Safety: extraction guarantees a live world pointer during system execution.
   140	        let (events, next_sequence) = unsafe {
   141	            self.world
   142	                .as_ref()
   143	                .read_events_since::<T>(state.next_sequence)
   144	        };
   145	        state.next_sequence = next_sequence;
   146	        telemetry::record_event_reader(start.elapsed().as_nanos() as u64, events.len() as u64);
   147	        events.iter()
   148	    }
   149	
   150	    pub fn send(&mut self, event: T) {
   151	        let start = Instant::now();
   152	        // Safety: extraction guarantees a live world pointer during system execution.
   153	        unsafe { self.world.as_mut().emit_event(event) };
   154	        telemetry::record_event_writer(start.elapsed().as_nanos() as u64, 1);
   155	    }
   156	}
