    45	pub trait IntoSystemSetKey {
    46	    fn system_set_key(&self) -> SystemSetKey;
    47	}
    48	
    49	impl<S> IntoSystemSetKey for S
    50	where
    51	    S: SystemSet,
    52	{
    53	    fn system_set_key(&self) -> SystemSetKey {
    54	        S::key()
    55	    }
    56	}
    57	
    58	#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default)]
    59	struct SystemConfigMetadata {
    60	    sets: Vec<SystemSetKey>,
    61	    before_sets: Vec<SystemSetKey>,
    62	    after_sets: Vec<SystemSetKey>,
    63	}
    64	
    65	impl SystemConfigMetadata {
    66	    fn with_set(&mut self, key: SystemSetKey) {
    67	        if !self.sets.contains(&key) {
    68	            self.sets.push(key);
    69	        }
    70	    }
    71	
    72	    fn before_set(&mut self, key: SystemSetKey) {
    73	        if !self.before_sets.contains(&key) {
    74	            self.before_sets.push(key);
    75	        }
    76	    }
    77	
    78	    fn after_set(&mut self, key: SystemSetKey) {
    79	        if !self.after_sets.contains(&key) {
    80	            self.after_sets.push(key);
    81	        }
    82	    }
    83	
    84	    fn apply(&self, system: &mut RegisteredSystem<World>) {
    85	        for key in &self.sets {
    86	            system.with_set_key(*key);
    87	        }
    88	        for key in &self.before_sets {
    89	            system.before_set_key(*key);
    90	        }
    91	        for key in &self.after_sets {
    92	            system.after_set_key(*key);
    93	        }
    94	    }
    95	}
    96	
    97	pub struct ConfiguredSystem<S, Marker> {
    98	    system: S,
    99	    config: SystemConfigMetadata,
   100	    _marker: PhantomData<fn() -> Marker>,
   101	}
   102	
   103	impl<S, Marker> ConfiguredSystem<S, Marker> {
   104	    fn new(system: S) -> Self {
   105	        Self {
   106	            system,
   107	            config: SystemConfigMetadata::default(),
   108	            _marker: PhantomData,
   109	        }
   110	    }
   111	
   112	    pub fn in_set<Set>(mut self, set: Set) -> Self
   113	    where
   114	        Set: IntoSystemSetKey,
   115	    {
   116	        self.config.with_set(set.system_set_key());
   117	        self
   118	    }
   119	
   120	    pub fn before<Set>(mut self, set: Set) -> Self
   121	    where
   122	        Set: IntoSystemSetKey,
   123	    {
   124	        self.config.before_set(set.system_set_key());
   125	        self
   126	    }
   127	
   128	    pub fn after<Set>(mut self, set: Set) -> Self
   129	    where
   130	        Set: IntoSystemSetKey,
   131	    {
   132	        self.config.after_set(set.system_set_key());
   133	        self
   134	    }
   135	}

   137	pub trait SystemConfigExt<Marker>: IntoSystem<Marker> + Sized {
   138	    fn in_set<Set>(self, set: Set) -> ConfiguredSystem<Self, Marker>
   139	    where
   140	        Set: IntoSystemSetKey,
   141	    {
   142	        ConfiguredSystem::new(self).in_set(set)
   143	    }
   144	
   145	    fn before<Set>(self, set: Set) -> ConfiguredSystem<Self, Marker>
   146	    where
   147	        Set: IntoSystemSetKey,
   148	    {
   149	        ConfiguredSystem::new(self).before(set)
   150	    }
   151	
   152	    fn after<Set>(self, set: Set) -> ConfiguredSystem<Self, Marker>
   153	    where
   154	        Set: IntoSystemSetKey,
   155	    {
   156	        ConfiguredSystem::new(self).after(set)
   157	    }
   158	}

   160	impl<S, Marker> SystemConfigExt<Marker> for S where S: IntoSystem<Marker> + Sized {}
   161	
   162	pub trait IntoSystemConfigs<Marker> {
   163	    fn register<L: ScheduleLabel>(
   164	        self,
   165	        world: &mut World,
   166	        scheduler: &mut ExecutionScheduler<World>,
   167	        deferred_commands: DeferredCommands,
   168	        build_errors: &mut Vec<anyhow::Error>,
   169	    );
   170	}
   171	
   172	impl<S, Marker> IntoSystemConfigs<Marker> for S
   173	where
   174	    S: IntoSystem<Marker>,
   175	{
   176	    fn register<L: ScheduleLabel>(
   177	        self,
   178	        world: &mut World,
   179	        scheduler: &mut ExecutionScheduler<World>,
   180	        deferred_commands: DeferredCommands,
   181	        build_errors: &mut Vec<anyhow::Error>,
   182	    ) {
   183	        match self.into_registered_system::<L>(world, deferred_commands) {
   184	            Ok(registered) => {
   185	                scheduler.add_system(registered);
   186	            }
   187	            Err(err) => build_errors.push(err),
   188	        }
   189	    }
   190	}
   191	
   192	impl<S, Marker> IntoSystem<Marker> for ConfiguredSystem<S, Marker>
   193	where
   194	    S: IntoSystem<Marker>,
   195	    Marker: 'static,
   196	{
   197	    fn into_registered_system<L: ScheduleLabel>(
   198	        self,
   199	        world: &mut World,
   200	        deferred_commands: DeferredCommands,
   201	    ) -> Result<RegisteredSystem<World>> {
   202	        let mut registered = self
   203	            .system
   204	            .into_registered_system::<L>(world, deferred_commands)?;
   205	        self.config.apply(&mut registered);
   206	        Ok(registered)
   207	    }
   208	}
   209	
   210	macro_rules! impl_into_system_configs_tuple {
   211	    ($(($name:ident, $marker:ident, $index:tt)),+ $(,)?) => {
   212	        impl<$($name, $marker,)+> IntoSystemConfigs<($($marker,)+)> for ($($name,)+)
   213	        where
   214	            $($name: IntoSystemConfigs<$marker>,)+
   215	        {
   216	            fn register<L: ScheduleLabel>(
   217	                self,
   218	                world: &mut World,
   219	                scheduler: &mut ExecutionScheduler<World>,
   220	                deferred_commands: DeferredCommands,
   221	                build_errors: &mut Vec<anyhow::Error>,
   222	            ) {
   223	                $(
   224	                    self.$index.register::<L>(
   225	                        world,
   226	                        scheduler,
   227	                        deferred_commands.clone(),
   228	                        build_errors,
   229	                    );
   230	                )+
   231	            }
   232	        }
   233	    };
   234	}

   279	trait SystemParamState: Sized {
   280	    type State: 'static;
   281	
   282	    fn init_state(world: &mut World) -> std::result::Result<Self::State, SystemParamError>;
   283	    fn access(state: &Self::State) -> QueryAccess;
   284	
   285	    unsafe fn extract<'w>(
   286	        state: &'w mut Self::State,
   287	        world: *mut World,
   288	        commands: *mut Commands,
   289	    ) -> std::result::Result<Self, SystemParamError>;
   290	}
   291	
   292	impl<T> SystemParamState for T
   293	where
   294	    T: for<'w> SystemParam<'w>,
   295	{
   296	    type State = <T as SystemParam<'static>>::State;
   297	
   298	    fn init_state(world: &mut World) -> std::result::Result<Self::State, SystemParamError> {
   299	        <T as SystemParam<'static>>::init_state(world)
   300	    }
   301	
   302	    fn access(state: &Self::State) -> QueryAccess {
   303	        <T as SystemParam<'static>>::access(state)
   304	    }
   305	
   306	    unsafe fn extract<'w>(
   307	        state: &'w mut Self::State,
   308	        world: *mut World,
   309	        commands: *mut Commands,
   310	    ) -> std::result::Result<Self, SystemParamError> {
   311	        // Safety: `SystemParam` implementors are required to keep `State` lifetime-independent.
   312	        // This cast converts the cached `'static` state type view into the extraction lifetime view.
   313	        let state_ptr = state as *mut Self::State as *mut <T as SystemParam<'w>>::State;
   314	        unsafe { <T as SystemParam<'w>>::extract(&mut *state_ptr, world, commands) }
   315	    }
   316	}
   317	
   318	fn merge_access(system_name: &str, access_parts: &[SystemAccess]) -> Result<SystemAccess> {
   319	    let mut merged = SystemAccess::new();
   320	    for access in access_parts {
   321	        let conflicts = merged.conflicts_with(access);
   322	        if let Some(conflict) = conflicts.first() {
   323	            return Err(anyhow!(
   324	                "system '{}' has conflicting param access to '{}' ({:?})",
   325	                system_name,
   326	                conflict.key.name(),
   327	                conflict.kind
   328	            ));
   329	        }
   330	        for read in access.reads() {
   331	            merged.add_read(*read);
   332	        }
   333	        for write in access.writes() {
   334	            merged.add_write(*write);
   335	        }
   336	    }
   337	    Ok(merged)
   338	}
   339	
   340	macro_rules! impl_into_system {
   341	    ($(($index:tt, $param:ident)),* $(,)?) => {
   342	        #[allow(unused_mut, unused_variables, non_snake_case)]
   343	        impl<Func, R, $($param),*> IntoSystem<fn($($param),*) -> R> for Func
   344	        where
   345	            Func: FnMut($($param),*) -> R + 'static,
   346	            R: SystemOutput,
   347	            $($param: SystemParamState,)*
   348	        {
   349	            fn into_registered_system<L: ScheduleLabel>(
   350	                self,
   351	                world: &mut World,
   352	                deferred_commands: DeferredCommands,
   353	            ) -> Result<RegisteredSystem<World>> {
   354	                let system_name = std::any::type_name::<Func>().to_string();
   355	                let mut states = (
   356	                    $(
   357	                        <$param as SystemParamState>::init_state(world)?,
   358	                    )*
   359	                );
   360	                let access_parts = vec![
   361	                    $(
   362	                        query_access_to_system_access(<$param as SystemParamState>::access(&states.$index)),
   363	                    )*
   364	                ];
   365	                let access = merge_access(&system_name, &access_parts)?;
   366	                let mut func = self;
   367	                let deferred_commands_ref = deferred_commands.clone();
   368	
   369	                RegisteredSystem::new::<L>(system_name, access, move |world| {
   370	                    let mut commands = Commands::new_external_owner();
   371	                    $(
   372	                        let $param = unsafe {
   373	                            <$param as SystemParamState>::extract(
   374	                                &mut states.$index,
   375	                                world as *mut World,
   376	                                &mut commands as *mut Commands,
   377	                            )?
   378	                        };
   379	                    )*
   380	                    let result = func($($param),*).into_result();
   381	                    let staged_commands = commands.finalize_external_owner();
   382	                    if result.is_ok() {
   383	                        deferred_commands_ref.borrow_mut().push(staged_commands);
   384	                    }
   385	                    result
   386	                })
   387	            }
   388	        }
   389	    };
   390	}
   391	
   392	impl_into_system!();
   393	impl_into_system!((0, A));
   394	impl_into_system!((0, A), (1, B));
   395	impl_into_system!((0, A), (1, B), (2, C));
   396	impl_into_system!((0, A), (1, B), (2, C), (3, D));
   397	impl_into_system!((0, A), (1, B), (2, C), (3, D), (4, E));
   398	impl_into_system!((0, A), (1, B), (2, C), (3, D), (4, E), (5, F));
   399	impl_into_system!((0, A), (1, B), (2, C), (3, D), (4, E), (5, F), (6, G));
   400	impl_into_system!(
   401	    (0, A),
   402	    (1, B),
   403	    (2, C),
   404	    (3, D),
   405	    (4, E),
   406	    (5, F),
   407	    (6, G),
   408	    (7, H)
   409	);
   410	
   411	pub struct Runtime {
   412	    scheduler: ExecutionScheduler<World>,
   413	    deferred_commands: DeferredCommands,
   414	    build_errors: Vec<anyhow::Error>,
   415	}
   416	
   417	impl Default for Runtime {
   418	    fn default() -> Self {
   419	        Self::new()
   420	    }
   421	}
   422	
   423	impl Runtime {
   424	    pub fn new() -> Self {
   425	        Self {
   426	            scheduler: ExecutionScheduler::new(),
   427	            deferred_commands: Rc::new(RefCell::new(Vec::new())),
   428	            build_errors: Vec::new(),
   429	        }
   430	    }
   431	
   432	    pub fn add_systems<L, S, Marker>(&mut self, world: &mut World, systems: S) -> &mut Self
   433	    where
   434	        L: ScheduleLabel,
   435	        S: IntoSystemConfigs<Marker>,
   436	    {
   437	        systems.register::<L>(
   438	            world,
   439	            &mut self.scheduler,
   440	            self.deferred_commands.clone(),
   441	            &mut self.build_errors,
   442	        );
   443	        self
   444	    }
   445	
   446	    pub fn plan_for<L: ScheduleLabel>(&mut self) -> Option<&ExecutionPlan> {
   447	        self.scheduler.plan_for::<L>()
   448	    }
   449	
   450	    pub fn scheduler(&mut self) -> &mut ExecutionScheduler<World> {
   451	        &mut self.scheduler
   452	    }
   453	
   454	    pub fn run_schedule<L: ScheduleLabel>(&mut self, world: &mut World) -> Result<()> {
   455	        if let Err(err) = self.ensure_build_ready() {
   456	            self.discard_deferred_commands();
   457	            return Err(err);
   458	        }
   459	        let plan_start = Instant::now();
   460	        let Some(plan) = self.scheduler.plan_for::<L>().cloned() else {
   461	            telemetry::record_runtime_plan(plan_start.elapsed().as_nanos() as u64);
   462	            return Ok(());
   463	        };
   464	        telemetry::record_runtime_plan(plan_start.elapsed().as_nanos() as u64);
   465	
   466	        for stage in plan.stages {
   467	            let stage_start = Instant::now();
   468	            for system_index in stage.system_indices {
   469	                let Some(system) = self.scheduler.systems_mut().get_mut(system_index) else {
   470	                    self.discard_deferred_commands();
   471	                    return Err(anyhow!("execution plan referenced missing system"));
   472	                };
   473	                if let Err(err) = system.run(world) {
   474	                    self.discard_deferred_commands();
   475	                    return Err(err);
   476	                }
   477	            }
   478	            telemetry::record_runtime_stage(stage_start.elapsed().as_nanos() as u64);
   479	            // Deferred commands are a stage boundary contract: structural effects become visible
   480	            // only after all systems in the current stage have completed.
   481	            if let Err(err) = self.flush_stage_commands(world) {
   482	                self.discard_deferred_commands();
   483	                return Err(err);
   484	            }
   485	        }
   486	
   487	        Ok(())
   488	    }
   489	
   490	    fn ensure_build_ready(&self) -> Result<()> {
   491	        if self.build_errors.is_empty() {
   492	            return Ok(());
   493	        }
   494	        let messages: Vec<_> = self.build_errors.iter().map(ToString::to_string).collect();
   495	        Err(anyhow!("runtime setup failed:\n{}", messages.join("\n")))
   496	    }
   497	
   498	    fn flush_stage_commands(&self, world: &mut World) -> Result<()> {
   499	        let start = Instant::now();
   500	        world.begin_stage_command_flush();
   501	        let stage_commands = std::mem::take(&mut *self.deferred_commands.borrow_mut());
   502	        let command_queue_count = stage_commands.len() as u64;
   503	        for commands in stage_commands {
   504	            commands.apply(world)?;
   505	        }
   506	        telemetry::record_runtime_flush(start.elapsed().as_nanos() as u64, command_queue_count);
   507	        Ok(())
   508	    }
   509	
   510	    fn discard_deferred_commands(&self) {
   511	        self.deferred_commands.borrow_mut().clear();
   512	    }
   513	}
   514	
   515	fn query_access_to_system_access(access: QueryAccess) -> SystemAccess {
   516	    let mut system_access = SystemAccess::new();
   517	    for read in access.component_reads() {
   518	        system_access.add_read(AccessKey::component_by_id(read.type_id(), read.name()));
   519	    }
   520	    for read in access.orphaned_component_reads() {
   521	        system_access.add_read(AccessKey::orphaned_component_by_id(
   522	            read.type_id(),
   523	            read.name(),
   524	        ));
   525	    }
   526	    for write in access.component_writes() {
   527	        system_access.add_write(AccessKey::component_by_id(write.type_id(), write.name()));
   528	    }
   529	    for read in access.resource_reads() {
   530	        system_access.add_read(AccessKey::resource_by_id(read.type_id(), read.name()));
   531	    }
   532	    for write in access.resource_writes() {
   533	        system_access.add_write(AccessKey::resource_by_id(write.type_id(), write.name()));
   534	    }
   535	    if access.deferred_structural_mutation() {
   536	        system_access.add_write(AccessKey::structural("world_structure"));
   537	    }
   538	    system_access
   539	}

    94	        EVENT_WRITER_CALLS.store(0, Ordering::Relaxed);
    95	        EVENT_WRITER_NANOS.store(0, Ordering::Relaxed);
    96	        EVENTS_WRITTEN.store(0, Ordering::Relaxed);
    97	        telemetry::reset();
    98	    }
    99	
   100	    pub fn snapshot() -> EcsTelemetrySnapshot {
   101	        EcsTelemetrySnapshot {
   102	            query_matching_calls: QUERY_MATCHING_CALLS.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   103	            query_matching_nanos: QUERY_MATCHING_NANOS.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   104	            query_matching_candidates: QUERY_MATCHING_CANDIDATES.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   105	            query_matching_matches: QUERY_MATCHING_MATCHES.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   106	            query_iter_calls: QUERY_ITER_CALLS.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   107	            query_iter_nanos: QUERY_ITER_NANOS.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   108	            query_get_calls: QUERY_GET_CALLS.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   109	            query_get_nanos: QUERY_GET_NANOS.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   110	            query_single_calls: QUERY_SINGLE_CALLS.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   111	            query_single_nanos: QUERY_SINGLE_NANOS.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   112	            changed_check_calls: CHANGED_CHECK_CALLS.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   113	            changed_check_nanos: CHANGED_CHECK_NANOS.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   114	            added_check_calls: ADDED_CHECK_CALLS.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   115	            added_check_nanos: ADDED_CHECK_NANOS.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   116	            runtime_plan_calls: RUNTIME_PLAN_CALLS.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   117	            runtime_plan_nanos: RUNTIME_PLAN_NANOS.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   118	            runtime_stage_calls: RUNTIME_STAGE_CALLS.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   119	            runtime_stage_nanos: RUNTIME_STAGE_NANOS.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   120	            runtime_flush_calls: RUNTIME_FLUSH_CALLS.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   121	            runtime_flush_nanos: RUNTIME_FLUSH_NANOS.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   122	            runtime_flush_command_queues: RUNTIME_FLUSH_COMMAND_QUEUES.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   123	            event_reader_calls: EVENT_READER_CALLS.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   124	            event_reader_nanos: EVENT_READER_NANOS.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   125	            events_read: EVENTS_READ.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   126	            event_writer_calls: EVENT_WRITER_CALLS.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   127	            event_writer_nanos: EVENT_WRITER_NANOS.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   128	            events_written: EVENTS_WRITTEN.load(Ordering::Relaxed),
   129	            scheduler: telemetry::snapshot(),
   130	        }
   131	    }

   136	        QUERY_MATCHING_CANDIDATES.fetch_add(candidates, Ordering::Relaxed);

   225	pub fn snapshot_delta(
   226	    before: &EcsTelemetrySnapshot,
   227	    after: &EcsTelemetrySnapshot,
   228	) -> EcsTelemetrySnapshot {
   229	    EcsTelemetrySnapshot {
   230	        query_matching_calls: after
   231	            .query_matching_calls
   232	            .saturating_sub(before.query_matching_calls),
   233	        query_matching_nanos: after
   234	            .query_matching_nanos
   235	            .saturating_sub(before.query_matching_nanos),
   236	        query_matching_candidates: after
   237	            .query_matching_candidates
   238	            .saturating_sub(before.query_matching_candidates),
   239	        query_matching_matches: after
   240	            .query_matching_matches
   241	            .saturating_sub(before.query_matching_matches),
   242	        query_iter_calls: after
   243	            .query_iter_calls
   244	            .saturating_sub(before.query_iter_calls),
   245	        query_iter_nanos: after
   246	            .query_iter_nanos
   247	            .saturating_sub(before.query_iter_nanos),
   248	        query_get_calls: after.query_get_calls.saturating_sub(before.query_get_calls),
   249	        query_get_nanos: after.query_get_nanos.saturating_sub(before.query_get_nanos),
   250	        query_single_calls: after
   251	            .query_single_calls
   252	            .saturating_sub(before.query_single_calls),
   253	        query_single_nanos: after
   254	            .query_single_nanos
   255	            .saturating_sub(before.query_single_nanos),
   256	        changed_check_calls: after
   257	            .changed_check_calls
   258	            .saturating_sub(before.changed_check_calls),
   259	        changed_check_nanos: after
   260	            .changed_check_nanos
   261	            .saturating_sub(before.changed_check_nanos),
   262	        added_check_calls: after
   263	            .added_check_calls
   264	            .saturating_sub(before.added_check_calls),
   265	        added_check_nanos: after
   266	            .added_check_nanos
   267	            .saturating_sub(before.added_check_nanos),
   268	        runtime_plan_calls: after
   269	            .runtime_plan_calls
   270	            .saturating_sub(before.runtime_plan_calls),
   271	        runtime_plan_nanos: after
   272	            .runtime_plan_nanos
   273	            .saturating_sub(before.runtime_plan_nanos),
   274	        runtime_stage_calls: after
   275	            .runtime_stage_calls
   276	            .saturating_sub(before.runtime_stage_calls),
   277	        runtime_stage_nanos: after
   278	            .runtime_stage_nanos
   279	            .saturating_sub(before.runtime_stage_nanos),
   280	        runtime_flush_calls: after
   281	            .runtime_flush_calls
   282	            .saturating_sub(before.runtime_flush_calls),
   283	        runtime_flush_nanos: after
   284	            .runtime_flush_nanos
   285	            .saturating_sub(before.runtime_flush_nanos),
   286	        runtime_flush_command_queues: after
   287	            .runtime_flush_command_queues
   288	            .saturating_sub(before.runtime_flush_command_queues),
   289	        event_reader_calls: after
   290	            .event_reader_calls
   291	            .saturating_sub(before.event_reader_calls),
   292	        event_reader_nanos: after
   293	            .event_reader_nanos
   294	            .saturating_sub(before.event_reader_nanos),
   295	        events_read: after.events_read.saturating_sub(before.events_read),
   296	        event_writer_calls: after
   297	            .event_writer_calls
   298	            .saturating_sub(before.event_writer_calls),
   299	        event_writer_nanos: after
   300	            .event_writer_nanos
   301	            .saturating_sub(before.event_writer_nanos),
   302	        events_written: after.events_written.saturating_sub(before.events_written),
   303	        scheduler: scheduler::telemetry::SchedulerTelemetrySnapshot {
   304	            plan_build_calls: after
   305	                .scheduler
   306	                .plan_build_calls
   307	                .saturating_sub(before.scheduler.plan_build_calls),
   308	            plan_build_nanos: after
   309	                .scheduler
   310	                .plan_build_nanos
   311	                .saturating_sub(before.scheduler.plan_build_nanos),
   312	            plan_conflict_checks: after

===== FILE: ./src/world/component_indexes.rs =====
     1	// Owner: ecs World - Component Secondary Index Types
     2	use super::world_struct::World;
     3	use crate::component::Component;
     4	use crate::entity::Entity;
     5	use std::any::{Any, TypeId};
     6	use std::collections::BTreeMap;
     7	
     8	pub(super) const DEFAULT_COMPONENT_INDEX_NAME: &str = "__default";
     9	
    10	#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]
    11	pub(super) struct ComponentIndexKey {
    12	    pub(super) component_type: TypeId,
    13	    key_type: TypeId,
    14	    name: String,
    15	}
    16	
    17	impl ComponentIndexKey {
    18	    pub(super) fn new(component_type: TypeId, key_type: TypeId, name: impl Into<String>) -> Self {
    19	        let mut name = name.into();
    20	        name = name.trim().to_string();
    21	        if name.is_empty() {
    22	            name = DEFAULT_COMPONENT_INDEX_NAME.to_string();
    23	        }
    24	        Self {
    25	            component_type,
    26	            key_type,
    27	            name,
    28	        }
    29	    }
    30	}
    31	
    32	pub(super) trait ComponentIndexStorage {
    33	    fn mark_dirty(&mut self);
    34	    fn rebuild(&mut self, world: &World);
    35	    fn as_any(&self) -> &dyn Any;
    36	}
    37	
    38	pub(super) struct ComponentSecondaryIndex<T: Component, K: Ord + Clone + 'static> {
    39	    entries: BTreeMap<K, Vec<Entity>>,
    40	    extractor: fn(&T) -> K,
    41	    dirty: bool,
    42	}
    43	
    44	impl<T: Component, K: Ord + Clone + 'static> ComponentSecondaryIndex<T, K> {
    45	    pub(super) fn new(extractor: fn(&T) -> K) -> Self {
    46	        Self {
    47	            entries: BTreeMap::new(),
    48	            extractor,
    49	            dirty: true,
    50	        }
    51	    }
    52	
    53	    pub(super) fn entities_for(&self, key: &K) -> Vec<Entity> {
    54	        self.entries.get(key).cloned().unwrap_or_default()
    55	    }
    56	
    57	    pub(super) fn first_entity_for(&self, key: &K) -> Option<Entity> {
    58	        self.entries
    59	            .get(key)
    60	            .and_then(|entities| entities.first())
    61	            .copied()
    62	    }
    63	}
    64	
    65	impl<T: Component, K: Ord + Clone + 'static> ComponentIndexStorage
    66	    for ComponentSecondaryIndex<T, K>
    67	{
    68	    fn mark_dirty(&mut self) {
    69	        self.dirty = true;
    70	    }
    71	
    72	    fn rebuild(&mut self, world: &World) {
    73	        if !self.dirty {
    74	            return;
    75	        }
    76	
    77	        self.entries.clear();
    78	        let mut entities = Vec::new();
    79	        world.matching_entities_into(&[TypeId::of::<T>()], &[], &mut entities);
    80	        for entity in entities {
    81	            let Some(component) = world.get::<T>(entity) else {
    82	                continue;
    83	            };
    84	            let key = (self.extractor)(component);
    85	            self.entries.entry(key).or_default().push(entity);
    86	        }
    87	        self.dirty = false;
    88	    }
    89	
    90	    fn as_any(&self) -> &dyn Any {
    91	        self
    92	    }
    93	}

===== END FILE: ./src/world/component_indexes.rs =====

     1	// Owner: ecs World - Borrow Wrappers and Entity Views
     2	use super::world_struct::World;
     3	use crate::bundle::Bundle;
     4	use crate::component::Component;
     5	use crate::entity::Entity;
     6	use crate::errors::EntityError;
     7	use std::ops::{Deref, DerefMut};
     8	
     9	pub struct Mut<'a, T> {
    10	    pub(super) value: &'a mut T,
    11	}
    12	
    13	impl<'a, T> Deref for Mut<'a, T> {
    14	    type Target = T;
    15	
    16	    fn deref(&self) -> &Self::Target {
    17	        self.value
    18	    }
    19	}
    20	
    21	impl<'a, T> DerefMut for Mut<'a, T> {
    22	    fn deref_mut(&mut self) -> &mut Self::Target {
    23	        self.value
    24	    }
    25	}
    26	
    27	pub struct EntityRef<'w> {
    28	    pub(super) world: &'w World,
    29	    pub(super) entity: Entity,
    30	}
    31	
    32	impl<'w> EntityRef<'w> {
    33	    pub fn entity(&self) -> Entity {
    34	        self.entity
    35	    }
    36	
    37	    pub fn contains<T: Component>(&self) -> bool {
    38	        self.world.contains_component::<T>(self.entity)
    39	    }
    40	
    41	    pub fn get<T: Component>(&self) -> Option<&T> {
    42	        self.world.get::<T>(self.entity)
    43	    }
    44	
    45	    pub fn require<T: Component>(&self) -> Result<&T, EntityError> {
    46	        self.world.require::<T>(self.entity)
    47	    }
    48	}
    49	
    50	pub struct EntityMut<'w> {
    51	    pub(super) world: &'w mut World,
    52	    pub(super) entity: Entity,
    53	}
    54	
    55	impl<'w> EntityMut<'w> {
    56	    pub fn entity(&self) -> Entity {
    57	        self.entity
    58	    }
    59	
    60	    pub fn contains<T: Component>(&self) -> bool {
    61	        self.world.contains_component::<T>(self.entity)
    62	    }
    63	
    64	    pub fn get<T: Component>(&self) -> Option<&T> {
    65	        self.world.get::<T>(self.entity)
    66	    }
    67	
    68	    pub fn get_mut<T: Component>(&mut self) -> Option<Mut<'_, T>> {
    69	        self.world.get_mut::<T>(self.entity)
    70	    }
    71	
    72	    pub fn require<T: Component>(&self) -> Result<&T, EntityError> {
    73	        self.world.require::<T>(self.entity)
    74	    }
    75	
    76	    pub fn require_mut<T: Component>(&mut self) -> Result<Mut<'_, T>, EntityError> {
    77	        self.world.require_mut::<T>(self.entity)
    78	    }
    79	
    80	    pub fn insert<B: Bundle>(&mut self, bundle: B) -> Result<(), EntityError> {
    81	        self.world.insert(self.entity, bundle)
    82	    }
    83	
    84	    pub fn remove<B: Bundle>(&mut self) -> Result<B, EntityError> {
    85	        self.world.remove::<B>(self.entity)
    86	    }
    87	
    88	    pub fn despawn(self) -> Result<(), EntityError> {
    89	        self.world.despawn(self.entity)
    90	    }
    91	}

    20	pub enum EventTracingPolicy {
    21	    Disabled,
    22	    OnOverflow,
    23	}
    24	
    25	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]
    26	pub struct EventChannelConfig {
    27	    pub capacity: Option<usize>,
    28	    pub overflow: OverflowPolicy,
    29	    pub lifetime: EventLifetime,
    30	    pub tracing: EventTracingPolicy,
    31	}
    32	
    33	impl Default for EventChannelConfig {
    34	    fn default() -> Self {
    35	        Self {
    36	            capacity: None,
    37	            overflow: OverflowPolicy::DropOldest,
    38	            lifetime: EventLifetime::Manual,
    39	            tracing: EventTracingPolicy::Disabled,
    40	        }
    41	    }
    42	}
    43	
    44	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]
    45	pub struct EventChannelStats {
    46	    pub emitted: u64,
    47	    pub drained: u64,
    48	    pub dropped: u64,
    49	    pub pending: usize,
    50	}
    51	
    52	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]
    53	pub struct EntitySpawnedEvent {
    54	    pub entity: Entity,
    55	}
    56	
    57	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]
    58	pub struct EntityDespawnedEvent {
    59	    pub entity: Entity,
    60	}
    61	
    62	#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]
    63	pub enum ObserverTrigger {
    64	    OnEmit,
    65	    OnDrain,
    66	    EndOfFrame,
    67	}
    68	
    69	#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]
    70	pub struct EventObserverNotification {
    71	    pub observer_id: String,
    72	    pub trigger: ObserverTrigger,
    73	    pub event_type: &'static str,
    74	    pub event_count: usize,
    75	}
    76	
    77	#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]
    78	pub(super) struct EventObserver {
    79	    pub(super) observer_id: String,
    80	    pub(super) event_type: TypeId,
    81	    pub(super) trigger: ObserverTrigger,
    82	    pub(super) invocations: u64,
    83	}
    84	
    85	pub(super) struct EventChannelStorage {
    86	    pub(super) event_type_name: &'static str,
    87	    events: Box<dyn Any>,
    88	    len_fn: fn(&Box<dyn Any>) -> usize,
    89	    clear_fn: fn(&mut Box<dyn Any>) -> usize,
    90	    pub(super) start_sequence: u64,
    91	    pub(super) next_sequence: u64,
    92	    pub(super) config: EventChannelConfig,
    93	    pub(super) emitted: u64,
    94	    pub(super) drained: u64,
    95	    pub(super) dropped: u64,
    96	}
    97	
    98	impl EventChannelStorage {
    99	    pub(super) fn new<T: 'static>() -> Self {
   100	        fn len_for<T: 'static>(events: &Box<dyn Any>) -> usize {
   101	            events
   102	                .downcast_ref::<Vec<T>>()
   103	                .unwrap_or_else(|| panic!("event channel len type mismatch: {}", type_name::<T>()))
   104	                .len()
   105	        }
   106	
   107	        fn clear_for<T: 'static>(events: &mut Box<dyn Any>) -> usize {
   108	            let buffer = events.downcast_mut::<Vec<T>>().unwrap_or_else(|| {
   109	                panic!("event channel clear type mismatch: {}", type_name::<T>())
   110	            });
   111	            let removed = buffer.len();
   112	            buffer.clear();
   113	            removed
   114	        }
   115	
   116	        Self {
   117	            event_type_name: type_name::<T>(),
   118	            events: Box::new(Vec::<T>::new()),
   119	            len_fn: len_for::<T>,
   120	            clear_fn: clear_for::<T>,
   121	            start_sequence: 0,
   122	            next_sequence: 0,
   123	            config: EventChannelConfig::default(),
   124	            emitted: 0,
   125	            drained: 0,
   126	            dropped: 0,
   127	        }
   128	    }
   129	
   130	    pub(super) fn events_ref<T: 'static>(&self) -> &[T] {
   131	        self.events
   132	            .downcast_ref::<Vec<T>>()
   133	            .map(Vec::as_slice)
   134	            .unwrap_or_else(|| {
   135	                panic!(
   136	                    "event channel type mismatch: stored={} requested={}",
   137	                    self.event_type_name,
   138	                    type_name::<T>()
   139	                )
   140	            })
   141	    }
   142	
   143	    pub(super) fn events_mut<T: 'static>(&mut self) -> &mut Vec<T> {
   144	        self.events.downcast_mut::<Vec<T>>().unwrap_or_else(|| {
   145	            panic!(
   146	                "event channel type mismatch: stored={} requested={}",
   147	                self.event_type_name,
   148	                type_name::<T>()
   149	            )
   150	        })
   151	    }
   152	
   153	    pub(super) fn events_len_any(&self) -> usize {
   154	        (self.len_fn)(&self.events)
   155	    }
   156	
   157	    pub(super) fn clear_any(&mut self) -> usize {
   158	        let removed = (self.clear_fn)(&mut self.events);
   159	        self.advance_sequence_for_removed(removed);
   160	        removed
   161	    }
   162	
   163	    pub(super) fn events_ref_since<T: 'static>(&self, sequence: u64) -> &[T] {
   164	        let events = self.events_ref::<T>();
   165	        let clamped_sequence = sequence.max(self.start_sequence).min(self.next_sequence);
   166	        let offset = (clamped_sequence.saturating_sub(self.start_sequence)) as usize;
   167	        &events[offset..]
   168	    }
   169	
   170	    pub(super) fn advance_sequence_for_removed(&mut self, removed: usize) {
   171	        let removed = removed as u64;
   172	        self.start_sequence = self
   173	            .start_sequence
   174	            .saturating_add(removed)
   175	            .min(self.next_sequence);
   176	    }
   177	}

     1	// Owner: ecs World - Secondary Index APIs
     2	use super::component_indexes::{
     3	    ComponentIndexKey, ComponentSecondaryIndex, DEFAULT_COMPONENT_INDEX_NAME,
     4	};
     5	use super::world_struct::World;
     6	use crate::component::Component;
     7	use crate::entity::Entity;
     8	use std::any::TypeId;
     9	
    10	impl World {
    11	    pub fn ensure_component_index_named<T: Component, K: Ord + Clone + 'static>(
    12	        &mut self,
    13	        name: impl Into<String>,
    14	        extractor: fn(&T) -> K,
    15	    ) -> bool {
    16	        self.__register_component::<T>();
    17	        let key = ComponentIndexKey::new(TypeId::of::<T>(), TypeId::of::<K>(), name);
    18	        let mut indexes = self.component_indexes.borrow_mut();
    19	        if indexes.contains_key(&key) {
    20	            return false;
    21	        }
    22	        indexes.insert(
    23	            key,
    24	            Box::new(ComponentSecondaryIndex::<T, K>::new(extractor)),
    25	        );
    26	        drop(indexes);
    27	        self.mark_component_indexes_dirty(TypeId::of::<T>());
    28	        true
    29	    }
    30	
    31	    pub fn find_entity_by_index<T: Component, K: Ord + Clone + 'static>(
    32	        &self,
    33	        key: &K,
    34	    ) -> Option<Entity> {
    35	        self.find_entity_by_index_named::<T, K>(DEFAULT_COMPONENT_INDEX_NAME, key)
    36	    }
    37	
    38	    pub fn find_entity_by_index_named<T: Component, K: Ord + Clone + 'static>(
    39	        &self,
    40	        name: impl Into<String>,
    41	        key: &K,
    42	    ) -> Option<Entity> {
    43	        let index_key = ComponentIndexKey::new(TypeId::of::<T>(), TypeId::of::<K>(), name);
    44	        let mut indexes = self.component_indexes.borrow_mut();
    45	        let Some(index) = indexes.get_mut(&index_key) else {
    46	            return None;
    47	        };
    48	        index.rebuild(self);
    49	        index
    50	            .as_any()
    51	            .downcast_ref::<ComponentSecondaryIndex<T, K>>()
    52	            .and_then(|index| index.first_entity_for(key))
    53	    }
    54	
    55	    pub fn find_entities_by_index<T: Component, K: Ord + Clone + 'static>(
    56	        &self,
    57	        key: &K,
    58	    ) -> Vec<Entity> {
    59	        self.find_entities_by_index_named::<T, K>(DEFAULT_COMPONENT_INDEX_NAME, key)
    60	    }
    61	
    62	    pub fn find_entities_by_index_named<T: Component, K: Ord + Clone + 'static>(
    63	        &self,
    64	        name: impl Into<String>,
    65	        key: &K,
    66	    ) -> Vec<Entity> {
    67	        let index_key = ComponentIndexKey::new(TypeId::of::<T>(), TypeId::of::<K>(), name);
    68	        let mut indexes = self.component_indexes.borrow_mut();
    69	        let Some(index) = indexes.get_mut(&index_key) else {
    70	            return Vec::new();
    71	        };
    72	        index.rebuild(self);
    73	        index
    74	            .as_any()
    75	            .downcast_ref::<ComponentSecondaryIndex<T, K>>()
    76	            .map(|index| index.entities_for(key))
    77	            .unwrap_or_default()
    78	    }
    79	
    80	    pub fn find_component_by_index<T: Component, K: Ord + Clone + 'static>(
    81	        &self,
    82	        key: &K,
    83	    ) -> Option<&T> {
    84	        self.find_component_by_index_named::<T, K>(DEFAULT_COMPONENT_INDEX_NAME, key)
    85	    }
    86	
    87	    pub fn find_component_by_index_named<T: Component, K: Ord + Clone + 'static>(
    88	        &self,
    89	        name: impl Into<String>,
    90	        key: &K,
    91	    ) -> Option<&T> {
    92	        let entity = self.find_entity_by_index_named::<T, K>(name, key)?;
    93	        self.get::<T>(entity)
    94	    }
    95	}

     1	// Owner: ecs World - Core Entity/Resource Lifecycle
     2	use super::change_tracking::{
     3	    ComponentChangeKind, ComponentChangeRecord, ResourceChangeKind, ResourceChangeRecord,
     4	};
     5	use super::component_indexes::DEFAULT_COMPONENT_INDEX_NAME;
     6	use super::entity_handles::{EntityMut, EntityRef, Mut};
     7	use super::event_channels::{EntityDespawnedEvent, EntitySpawnedEvent};
     8	use super::world_struct::World;
     9	use crate::bundle::Bundle;
    10	use crate::commands::Commands;
    11	use crate::component::{Component, ComponentState, Resource, StatefulComponent};
    12	use crate::entity::{Entity, EntityAllocator};
    13	use crate::errors::{EntityError, ResourceError};
    14	use crate::query::{QueryFilter, QueryOrphanedState, QuerySpec, QueryState};
    15	use crate::storage::ArchetypeRegistry;

    20	impl World {
    21	    pub fn new() -> Self {
    22	        Self {
    23	            allocator: EntityAllocator::new(),
    24	            alive_entities: BTreeSet::new(),
    25	            component_registry: HashMap::new(),
    26	            next_component_id: 0,
    27	            resources: HashMap::new(),
    28	            event_channels: HashMap::new(),
    29	            event_observers: HashMap::new(),
    30	            event_observer_notifications: Vec::new(),
    31	            component_indexes: RefCell::new(HashMap::new()),
    32	            spatial_indexes: HashMap::new(),
    33	            archetype_registry: ArchetypeRegistry::new(),
    34	            entity_locations: Default::default(),
    35	            change_tick: 0,
    36	            component_change_ticks: HashMap::new(),
    37	            resource_change_ticks: HashMap::new(),
    38	            component_change_log: Vec::new(),
    39	            removed_component_records: HashMap::new(),
    40	            resource_change_log: Vec::new(),
    41	        }
    42	    }
    43	
    44	    pub fn commands(&self) -> Commands {
    45	        Commands::new()
    46	    }
    47	
    48	    pub fn contains(&self, entity: Entity) -> bool {
    49	        self.alive_entities.contains(&entity)
    50	    }
    51	
    52	    pub fn spawn<B: Bundle>(&mut self, bundle: B) -> Entity {
    53	        B::register(self);
    54	        let entity = self.allocator.allocate();
    55	        self.alive_entities.insert(entity);
    56	        self.place_entity_in_empty_archetype(entity);
    57	        bundle
    58	            .insert(self, entity)
    59	            .expect("bundle insert should succeed for new entity");
    60	        self.emit_event(EntitySpawnedEvent { entity });
    61	        entity
    62	    }
    63	
    64	    pub fn despawn(&mut self, entity: Entity) -> Result<(), EntityError> {
    65	        self.ensure_entity_exists(entity)?;
    66	        self.remove_entity_from_spatial_indexes(entity);
    67	        let removed_types = self
    68	            .entity_locations
    69	            .get(entity)
    70	            .and_then(|location| {
    71	                self.archetype_registry
    72	                    .component_types(location.archetype_id)
    73	                    .map(|types| types.to_vec())
    74	            })
    75	            .unwrap_or_default();
    76	        self.remove_entity_from_archetype_tracking(entity);
    77	        self.alive_entities.remove(&entity);
    78	        self.allocator.free(entity);
    79	        for type_id in removed_types {
    80	            let component_name = self
    81	                .component_registry
    82	                .get(&type_id)
    83	                .map(|meta| meta.name)
    84	                .unwrap_or("unknown_component");
    85	            self.record_component_change(
    86	                entity,
    87	                type_id,
    88	                component_name,
    89	                ComponentChangeKind::Removed,
    90	            );
    91	        }
    92	        self.emit_event(EntityDespawnedEvent { entity });
    93	        Ok(())
    94	    }
    95	
    96	    pub fn insert<B: Bundle>(&mut self, entity: Entity, bundle: B) -> Result<(), EntityError> {
    97	        self.ensure_entity_exists(entity)?;
    98	        B::register(self);
    99	        bundle.insert(self, entity)
   100	    }
   101	
   102	    pub fn remove<B: Bundle>(&mut self, entity: Entity) -> Result<B, EntityError> {
   103	        self.ensure_entity_exists(entity)?;
   104	        B::remove(self, entity)
   105	    }
   106	
   107	    pub fn get<T: Component>(&self, entity: Entity) -> Option<&T> {
   108	        if !self.contains(entity) {
   109	            return None;
   110	        }
   111	        self.archetype_component::<T>(entity)
   112	    }
   113	
   114	    pub fn get_mut<T: Component>(&mut self, entity: Entity) -> Option<Mut<'_, T>> {
   115	        if !self.contains(entity) {
   116	            return None;
   117	        }
   118	        self.mark_component_modified_by_id(entity, TypeId::of::<T>(), T::component_name());
   119	        let value = self.archetype_component_mut_untracked::<T>(entity)?;
   120	        Some(Mut { value })
   121	    }
   122	
   123	    pub fn component_state<T: StatefulComponent>(&self, entity: Entity) -> Option<ComponentState> {
   124	        if !self.contains(entity) {
   125	            return None;
   126	        }
   127	        let (generation, version) = self.archetype_registry.component_state_by_id(
   128	            entity,
   129	            TypeId::of::<T>(),
   130	            &self.entity_locations,
   131	        )?;
   132	        Some(ComponentState {
   133	            generation,
   134	            version,
   135	        })
   136	    }
   137	
   138	    pub fn mark_stateful_changed<T: StatefulComponent>(&mut self, entity: Entity) -> bool {
   139	        if !self.has_component_by_type_id(entity, TypeId::of::<T>()) {
   140	            return false;
   141	        }
   142	        self.mark_component_modified_by_id(entity, TypeId::of::<T>(), T::component_name());
   143	        self.archetype_registry
   144	            .mark_component_stateful_changed_by_id(
   145	                entity,
   146	                TypeId::of::<T>(),
   147	                self.change_tick,
   148	                &self.entity_locations,
   149	            )
   150	    }
   151	
   152	    pub fn require<T: Component>(&self, entity: Entity) -> Result<&T, EntityError> {
   153	        self.get::<T>(entity).ok_or(EntityError::MissingComponent {
   154	            entity,
   155	            component: type_name::<T>(),
   156	        })
   157	    }
   158	
   159	    pub fn require_mut<T: Component>(&mut self, entity: Entity) -> Result<Mut<'_, T>, EntityError> {
   160	        self.get_mut::<T>(entity)
   161	            .ok_or(EntityError::MissingComponent {
   162	                entity,
   163	                component: type_name::<T>(),
   164	            })
   165	    }
   166

   168	        self.ensure_entity_exists(entity)?;
   169	        Ok(EntityRef {
   170	            world: self,
   171	            entity,
   172	        })
   173	    }

   176	        self.ensure_entity_exists(entity)?;
   177	        Ok(EntityMut {
   178	            world: self,
   179	            entity,
   180	        })
   181	    }

   183	    pub fn query_state<Q: QuerySpec, F: QueryFilter>(&self) -> QueryState<Q, F> {
   184	        QueryState::new(self)
   185	    }

   189	    }

   191	    pub fn insert_resource<R: Resource>(&mut self, resource: R) {
   192	        let type_id = TypeId::of::<R>();
   193	        let kind = if self.resources.contains_key(&type_id) {
   194	            ResourceChangeKind::Modified
   195	        } else {
   196	            ResourceChangeKind::Inserted
   197	        };
   198	        self.resources.insert(type_id, Box::new(resource));
   199	        self.record_resource_change(type_id, type_name::<R>(), kind);
   200	    }
   201	
   202	    pub fn has_resource<R: Resource>(&self) -> bool {
   203	        self.resources.contains_key(&TypeId::of::<R>())
   204	    }
   205	
   206	    pub fn resource<R: Resource>(&self) -> Result<&R, ResourceError> {
   207	        self.resources
   208	            .get(&TypeId::of::<R>())
   209	            .and_then(|res| res.downcast_ref::<R>())
   210	            .ok_or(ResourceError::Missing {
   211	                resource: type_name::<R>(),
   212	            })
   213	    }
   214	
   215	    pub fn resource_by_type_id(&self, type_id: TypeId) -> Option<&dyn Any> {
   216	        self.resources
   217	            .get(&type_id)
   218	            .map(|resource| resource.as_ref())
   219	    }
   220	
   221	    pub fn resource_mut<R: Resource>(&mut self) -> Result<&mut R, ResourceError> {
   222	        let type_id = TypeId::of::<R>();
   223	        if !self.resources.contains_key(&type_id) {
   224	            return Err(ResourceError::Missing {
   225	                resource: type_name::<R>(),
   226	            });
   227	        }
   228	        self.record_resource_change(type_id, type_name::<R>(), ResourceChangeKind::Modified);
   229	        let value = self
   230	            .resources
   231	            .get_mut(&type_id)
   232	            .and_then(|res| res.downcast_mut::<R>())
   233	            .ok_or(ResourceError::Missing {
   234	                resource: type_name::<R>(),
   235	            })?;
   236	        Ok(value)
   237	    }
   238	
   239	    pub fn remove_resource<R: Resource>(&mut self) -> Option<R> {
   240	        let type_id = TypeId::of::<R>();
   241	        let removed = self
   242	            .resources
   243	            .remove(&type_id)
   244	            .and_then(|res| res.downcast::<R>().ok().map(|boxed| *boxed));
   245	        if removed.is_some() {
   246	            self.record_resource_change(type_id, type_name::<R>(), ResourceChangeKind::Removed);
   247	        }
   248	        removed
   249	    }
   250	
   251	    pub fn current_change_tick(&self) -> u64 {
   252	        self.change_tick
   253	    }
   254	
   255	    #[doc(hidden)]
   256	    pub fn __entity_archetype_location(&self, entity: Entity) -> Option<(usize, usize)> {
   257	        self.entity_locations
   258	            .get(entity)
   259	            .map(|location| (location.archetype_id.index(), location.row))
   260	    }
   261	
   262	    #[doc(hidden)]
   263	    pub fn __entity_archetype_component_count(&self, entity: Entity) -> Option<usize> {
   264	        let location = self.entity_locations.get(entity)?;
   265	        self.archetype_registry
   266	            .component_count(location.archetype_id)
   267	    }
   268	
   269	    #[doc(hidden)]
   270	    pub fn __entity_component_ticks<T: Component>(&self, entity: Entity) -> Option<(u64, u64)> {
   271	        self.archetype_component_metadata::<T>(entity)
   272	    }
   273	
   274	    /// Type-level reporting helper.
   275	    /// This is intentionally separate from `Changed<T>` query semantics, which are driven by
   276	    /// archetype row metadata (`changed_tick`) during query/filter evaluation.
   277	    pub fn component_changed_since<T: Component>(&self, tick: u64) -> bool {
   278	        self.component_change_ticks
   279	            .get(&TypeId::of::<T>())
   280	            .is_some_and(|changed| *changed > tick)
   281	    }
   282	
   283	    /// Type-level reporting helper for resources.
   284	    pub fn resource_changed_since<R: Resource>(&self, tick: u64) -> bool {
   285	        self.resource_change_ticks
   286	            .get(&TypeId::of::<R>())
   287	            .is_some_and(|changed| *changed > tick)
   288	    }
   289	
   290	    /// Change-history reporting API.
   291	    /// This log is for introspection/reporting and is not used by query/filter change matching.
   292	    pub fn component_changes_since(&self, tick: u64) -> Vec<ComponentChangeRecord> {
   293	        self.component_change_log
   294	            .iter()
   295	            .filter(|change| change.tick > tick)
   296	            .cloned()
   297	            .collect()
   298	    }
   299	
   300	    /// Resource change-history reporting API.
   301	    pub fn resource_changes_since(&self, tick: u64) -> Vec<ResourceChangeRecord> {
   302	        self.resource_change_log
   303	            .iter()
   304	            .filter(|change| change.tick > tick)
   305	            .cloned()
   306	            .collect()
   307	    }
   308	
   309	    pub fn ensure_component_index<T: Component, K: Ord + Clone + 'static>(
   310	        &mut self,
   311	        extractor: fn(&T) -> K,
   312	    ) -> bool {
   313	        self.ensure_component_index_named::<T, K>(DEFAULT_COMPONENT_INDEX_NAME, extractor)
   314	    }
   315	}

===== FILE: ./src/world/world_events_impl.rs =====
     1	// Owner: ecs World - Event Channel APIs
     2	use super::event_channels::{
     3	    EventChannelConfig, EventChannelStats, EventChannelStorage, EventLifetime, EventObserver,
     4	    EventObserverNotification, ObserverTrigger, OverflowPolicy,
     5	};
     6	use super::world_struct::World;
     7	use std::any::TypeId;
     8	
     9	impl World {
    10	    pub fn has_event_channel<T: 'static>(&self) -> bool {
    11	        self.event_channels.contains_key(&TypeId::of::<T>())
    12	    }
    13	
    14	    pub fn ensure_event_channel<T: 'static>(&mut self) -> bool {
    15	        let type_id = TypeId::of::<T>();
    16	        if self.event_channels.contains_key(&type_id) {
    17	            return false;
    18	        }
    19	        self.event_channels
    20	            .insert(type_id, EventChannelStorage::new::<T>());
    21	        true
    22	    }
    23	
    24	    pub fn configure_event_channel<T: 'static>(&mut self, config: EventChannelConfig) {
    25	        let type_id = TypeId::of::<T>();
    26	        let channel = self
    27	            .event_channels
    28	            .entry(type_id)
    29	            .or_insert_with(EventChannelStorage::new::<T>);
    30	        channel.config = config;
    31	    }
    32	
    33	    pub fn emit_event<T: 'static>(&mut self, event: T) {
    34	        let type_id = TypeId::of::<T>();
    35	        let (event_type_name, emitted_count) = {
    36	            let channel = self
    37	                .event_channels
    38	                .entry(type_id)
    39	                .or_insert_with(EventChannelStorage::new::<T>);
    40	            let config = channel.config;
    41	            let event_type_name = channel.event_type_name;
    42	            let mut dropped = false;
    43	            let mut accepted = false;
    44	            let mut removed_from_front = 0usize;
    45	
    46	            {
    47	                let events = channel.events_mut::<T>();
    48	                let before = events.len();
    49	                match config.capacity {
    50	                    None => {
    51	                        events.push(event);
    52	                        accepted = true;
    53	                    }
    54	                    Some(capacity) => {
    55	                        if capacity == 0 {
    56	                            dropped = true;
    57	                            if matches!(config.overflow, OverflowPolicy::Panic) {
    58	                                panic!(
    59	                                    "event channel overflow for {event_type_name} with capacity=0"
    60	                                );
    61	                            }
    62	                        } else if before < capacity {
    63	                            events.push(event);
    64	                            accepted = true;
    65	                        } else {
    66	                            match config.overflow {
    67	                                OverflowPolicy::DropOldest => {
    68	                                    events.remove(0);
    69	                                    removed_from_front = 1;
    70	                                    events.push(event);
    71	                                    dropped = true;
    72	                                    accepted = true;
    73	                                }
    74	                                OverflowPolicy::DropNewest => {
    75	                                    dropped = true;
    76	                                }
    77	                                OverflowPolicy::Panic => {
    78	                                    panic!(
    79	                                        "event channel overflow for {event_type_name} at capacity={capacity}"
    80	                                    );
    81	                                }
    82	                            }
    83	                        }
    84	                    }
    85	                }
    86	            }
    87	            if removed_from_front > 0 {
    88	                channel.advance_sequence_for_removed(removed_from_front);
    89	            }
    90	
    91	            channel.emitted = channel.emitted.saturating_add(1);
    92	            if dropped {
    93	                channel.dropped = channel.dropped.saturating_add(1);
    94	            }
    95	            if accepted {
    96	                channel.next_sequence = channel.next_sequence.saturating_add(1);
    97	            }
    98	
    99	            (event_type_name, usize::from(accepted))
   100	        };
   101	        if emitted_count > 0 {
   102	            self.trigger_observers(
   103	                type_id,
   104	                event_type_name,
   105	                ObserverTrigger::OnEmit,
   106	                emitted_count,
   107	            );
   108	        }
   109	    }
   110	
   111	    pub fn read_events<T: 'static>(&self) -> &[T] {
   112	        self.event_channels
   113	            .get(&TypeId::of::<T>())
   114	            .map(|channel| channel.events_ref::<T>())
   115	            .unwrap_or(&[])
   116	    }
   117	
   118	    pub(crate) fn read_events_since<T: 'static>(&self, sequence: u64) -> (&[T], u64) {
   119	        let Some(channel) = self.event_channels.get(&TypeId::of::<T>()) else {
   120	            return (&[], 0);
   121	        };
   122	        (
   123	            channel.events_ref_since::<T>(sequence),
   124	            channel.next_sequence,
   125	        )
   126	    }
   127	
   128	    pub fn drain_events<T: 'static>(&mut self) -> Vec<T> {
   129	        let type_id = TypeId::of::<T>();
   130	        let (drained, event_type_name, drained_count) = {
   131	            let Some(channel) = self.event_channels.get_mut(&type_id) else {
   132	                return Vec::new();
   133	            };
   134	            let event_type_name = channel.event_type_name;
   135	            let drained = std::mem::take(channel.events_mut::<T>());
   136	            let drained_count = drained.len();
   137	            if drained_count > 0 {
   138	                channel.advance_sequence_for_removed(drained_count);
   139	                channel.drained = channel.drained.saturating_add(drained_count as u64);
   140	            }
   141	            (drained, event_type_name, drained_count)
   142	        };
   143	        if drained_count > 0 {
   144	            self.trigger_observers(
   145	                type_id,
   146	                event_type_name,
   147	                ObserverTrigger::OnDrain,
   148	                drained_count,
   149	            );
   150	        }
   151	        drained
   152	    }
   153	
   154	    pub fn clear_events<T: 'static>(&mut self) -> usize {
   155	        let Some(channel) = self.event_channels.get_mut(&TypeId::of::<T>()) else {
   156	            return 0;
   157	        };
   158	        let removed = channel.clear_any();
   159	        channel.drained = channel.drained.saturating_add(removed as u64);
   160	        removed
   161	    }
   162	
   163	    pub fn event_count<T: 'static>(&self) -> usize {
   164	        self.event_channels
   165	            .get(&TypeId::of::<T>())
   166	            .map(|channel| channel.events_ref::<T>().len())
   167	            .unwrap_or(0)
   168	    }
   169	
   170	    pub fn event_channel_stats<T: 'static>(&self) -> Option<EventChannelStats> {
   171	        self.event_channels
   172	            .get(&TypeId::of::<T>())
   173	            .map(|channel| EventChannelStats {
   174	                emitted: channel.emitted,
   175	                drained: channel.drained,
   176	                dropped: channel.dropped,
   177	                pending: channel.events_ref::<T>().len(),
   178	            })
   179	    }
   180	
   181	    pub fn observe_events<T: 'static>(
   182	        &mut self,
   183	        observer_id: impl Into<String>,
   184	        trigger: ObserverTrigger,
   185	    ) -> bool {
   186	        let observer_id = observer_id.into();
   187	        let created = !self.event_observers.contains_key(&observer_id);
   188	        self.event_observers.insert(
   189	            observer_id.clone(),
   190	            EventObserver {
   191	                observer_id,
   192	                event_type: TypeId::of::<T>(),
   193	                trigger,
   194	                invocations: 0,
   195	            },
   196	        );
   197	        created
   198	    }
   199	
   200	    pub fn remove_event_observer(&mut self, observer_id: &str) -> bool {
   201	        self.event_observers.remove(observer_id).is_some()
   202	    }
   203	
   204	    pub fn event_observer_invocations(&self, observer_id: &str) -> Option<u64> {
   205	        self.event_observers
   206	            .get(observer_id)
   207	            .map(|observer| observer.invocations)
   208	    }
   209	
   210	    pub fn drain_event_observer_notifications(&mut self) -> Vec<EventObserverNotification> {
   211	        std::mem::take(&mut self.event_observer_notifications)
   212	    }
   213	
   214	    pub fn drain_events_map<T: 'static, U, F>(&mut self, map: F) -> Vec<U>
   215	    where
   216	        F: FnMut(T) -> U,
   217	    {
   218	        self.drain_events::<T>().into_iter().map(map).collect()
   219	    }
   220	
   221	    pub fn drain_events_filter<T: 'static, F>(&mut self, mut predicate: F) -> Vec<T>
   222	    where
   223	        F: FnMut(&T) -> bool,
   224	    {
   225	        self.drain_events::<T>()
   226	            .into_iter()
   227	            .filter(|event| predicate(event))
   228	            .collect()
   229	    }
   230	
   231	    pub fn finish_event_frame(&mut self) {
   232	        let mut end_of_frame_triggers: Vec<(TypeId, &'static str, usize)> = Vec::new();
   233	        for (type_id, channel) in &mut self.event_channels {
   234	            let pending = channel.events_len_any();
   235	            if pending > 0 {
   236	                end_of_frame_triggers.push((*type_id, channel.event_type_name, pending));
   237	            }
   238	            if matches!(channel.config.lifetime, EventLifetime::FrameTransient) && pending > 0 {
   239	                let removed = channel.clear_any();
   240	                channel.drained = channel.drained.saturating_add(removed as u64);
   241	            }
   242	        }
   243	        for (event_type, event_type_name, pending) in end_of_frame_triggers {
   244	            self.trigger_observers(
   245	                event_type,
   246	                event_type_name,
   247	                ObserverTrigger::EndOfFrame,
   248	                pending,
   249	            );
   250	        }
   251	    }
   252	}

     1	// Owner: ecs World - Internal Mutation and Change Tracking
     2	use super::change_tracking::{
     3	    ComponentChangeKind, ComponentChangeRecord, ComponentMeta, RemovedComponentRecord,
     4	    ResourceChangeKind, ResourceChangeRecord,
     5	};
     6	use super::event_channels::{EventObserverNotification, ObserverTrigger};
     7	use super::world_struct::World;
     8	use crate::component::Component;
     9	use crate::entity::Entity;

    17	    #[doc(hidden)]
    18	    pub fn __register_component<T: Component>(&mut self) {
    19	        self.ensure_component_registered::<T>();
    20	    }
    21	
    22	    #[doc(hidden)]
    23	    pub fn __insert_component<T: Component>(
    24	        &mut self,
    25	        entity: Entity,
    26	        component: T,
    27	    ) -> Result<(), EntityError> {
    28	        self.ensure_entity_exists(entity)?;
    29	        self.ensure_component_registered::<T>();
    30	        let kind = if self.contains_component::<T>(entity) {
    31	            ComponentChangeKind::Modified
    32	        } else {
    33	            ComponentChangeKind::Added
    34	        };
    35	        let component_type = TypeId::of::<T>();
    36	        self.record_component_change(entity, component_type, T::component_name(), kind);
    37	        let tick = self.change_tick;
    38	        let inserted = if matches!(kind, ComponentChangeKind::Added) {
    39	            self.archetype_registry.add_component::<T>(
    40	                entity,
    41	                component,
    42	                tick,
    43	                &mut self.entity_locations,
    44	            )
    45	        } else {
    46	            self.archetype_registry.update_component::<T>(
    47	                entity,
    48	                component,
    49	                tick,
    50	                &self.entity_locations,
    51	            )
    52	        };
    53	        assert!(
    54	            inserted,
    55	            "archetype component insert/update must succeed for live entity"
    56	        );
    57	        Ok(())
    58	    }
    59	
    60	    #[doc(hidden)]
    61	    pub fn __remove_component<T: Component>(&mut self, entity: Entity) -> Result<T, EntityError> {
    62	        self.ensure_entity_exists(entity)?;
    63	        let value = self
    64	            .archetype_registry
    65	            .remove_component::<T>(entity, &mut self.entity_locations)
    66	            .ok_or(EntityError::MissingComponent {
    67	                entity,
    68	                component: type_name::<T>(),
    69	            })?;
    70	        self.record_component_change(
    71	            entity,
    72	            TypeId::of::<T>(),
    73	            T::component_name(),
    74	            ComponentChangeKind::Removed,
    75	        );
    76	        Ok(value)
    77	    }
    78	
    79	    pub(crate) fn matching_entities_into(
    80	        &self,
    81	        required_present: &[TypeId],
    82	        excluded: &[TypeId],
    83	        out: &mut Vec<Entity>,
    84	    ) {
    85	        let start = Instant::now();
    86	        let _ = self
    87	            .archetype_registry
    88	            .collect_matching_entities(required_present, excluded, out);
    89	        let count = out.len() as u64;
    90	        telemetry::record_query_matching(start.elapsed().as_nanos() as u64, count, count);
    91	    }
    92

   117	
   118	    pub(super) fn has_component_by_type_id(&self, entity: Entity, type_id: TypeId) -> bool {
   119	        let Some(location) = self.entity_locations.get(entity) else {
   120	            return false;
   121	        };
   122	        self.archetype_registry
   123	            .component_types(location.archetype_id)
   124	            .is_some_and(|component_types| component_types.binary_search(&type_id).is_ok())
   125	    }
   126	
   127	    pub(crate) fn entity_matches_component_constraints(
   128	        &self,
   129	        entity: Entity,
   130	        required_present: &[TypeId],
   131	        excluded: &[TypeId],
   132	    ) -> bool {
   133	        self.contains(entity)
   134	            && required_present
   135	                .iter()
   136	                .all(|type_id| self.has_component_by_type_id(entity, *type_id))
   137	            && excluded
   138	                .iter()
   139	                .all(|type_id| !self.has_component_by_type_id(entity, *type_id))
   140	    }
   141	
   142	    pub(super) fn contains_component<T: Component>(&self, entity: Entity) -> bool {
   143	        self.has_component_by_type_id(entity, TypeId::of::<T>())
   144	    }
   145	
   146	    pub(crate) fn component_changed_for_entity_since<T: Component>(
   147	        &self,
   148	        entity: Entity,
   149	        tick: u64,
   150	    ) -> bool {
   151	        let start = Instant::now();
   152	        let changed = self
   153	            .archetype_component_metadata::<T>(entity)
   154	            .is_some_and(|(_added_tick, changed_tick)| changed_tick > tick);
   155	        telemetry::record_changed_check(start.elapsed().as_nanos() as u64);
   156	        changed
   157	    }
   158	
   159	    pub(crate) fn component_added_for_entity_since<T: Component>(
   160	        &self,
   161	        entity: Entity,
   162	        tick: u64,
   163	    ) -> bool {
   164	        let start = Instant::now();
   165	        let added = self
   166	            .archetype_component_metadata::<T>(entity)
   167	            .is_some_and(|(added_tick, _changed_tick)| added_tick > tick);
   168	        telemetry::record_added_check(start.elapsed().as_nanos() as u64);
   169	        added
   170	    }
   171	
   172	    pub(crate) fn mark_component_modified_by_id(

   177	    ) {

   179	            entity,
   180	            component_type,

   183	        );
   184	        let _ = self.archetype_registry.mark_component_changed_by_id(
   185	            entity,
   186	            component_type,
   187	            self.change_tick,

   192	    fn mark_component_type_changed_by_id(&mut self, type_id: TypeId) {
   193	        self.change_tick = self.change_tick.saturating_add(1);
   194	        self.component_change_ticks
   195	            .insert(type_id, self.change_tick);
   196	        self.mark_component_indexes_dirty(type_id);
   197	    }
   198	
   199	    pub(super) fn record_component_change(
   200	        &mut self,
   201	        entity: Entity,
   202	        component_type: TypeId,
   203	        component_name: &'static str,
   204	        kind: ComponentChangeKind,
   205	    ) {
   206	        self.mark_component_type_changed_by_id(component_type);
   207	        self.component_change_log.push(ComponentChangeRecord {
   208	            tick: self.change_tick,
   209	            entity,
   210	            component_type,
   211	            component_name,
   212	            kind,
   213	        });
   214	        if matches!(kind, ComponentChangeKind::Removed) {
   215	            self.removed_component_records
   216	                .entry(component_type)
   217	                .or_default()
   218	                .push(RemovedComponentRecord {
   219	                    tick: self.change_tick,
   220	                    entity,
   221	                });
   222	        }
   223	    }
   224	
   225	    pub(crate) fn begin_stage_command_flush(&mut self) {
   226	        self.removed_component_records.clear();
   227	    }
   228	
   229	    pub(crate) fn removed_component_records_current_window(
   230	        &self,
   231	        component_type: TypeId,
   232	        out: &mut Vec<(Entity, u64)>,
   233	    ) {
   234	        out.clear();
   235	        let Some(records) = self.removed_component_records.get(&component_type) else {
   236	            return;
   237	        };
   238	        out.extend(records.iter().map(|record| (record.entity, record.tick)));
   239	    }

   245	        // Safety: pointers are produced by archetype-owned typed columns and remain valid.
   246	        Some(unsafe { &*ptr })
   247	    }

   256	        // Safety: pointers are produced by archetype-owned typed columns and remain valid.

   261	        &self,

   265	            .archetype_registry

   267	        Some((metadata.added_tick, metadata.changed_tick))

   270	    fn ensure_component_registered<T: Component>(&mut self) {
   271	        self.archetype_registry.register_component_type::<T>();
   272	        self.component_registry
   273	            .entry(TypeId::of::<T>())
   274	            .or_insert_with(|| {
   275	                let id = self.next_component_id;
   276	                self.next_component_id = self.next_component_id.saturating_add(1);
   277	                ComponentMeta {
   278	                    _id: id,
   279	                    name: T::component_name(),
   280	                }
   281	            });
   282	    }

   284	    pub(super) fn ensure_entity_exists(&self, entity: Entity) -> Result<(), EntityError> {
   285	        if self.contains(entity) {
   286	            Ok(())
   287	        } else {
   288	            Err(EntityError::NoSuchEntity { entity })
   289	        }
   290	    }
   291	
   292	    pub(super) fn record_resource_change(
   293	        &mut self,
   294	        resource_type: TypeId,
   295	        resource_name: &'static str,
   296	        kind: ResourceChangeKind,
   297	    ) {
   298	        self.change_tick = self.change_tick.saturating_add(1);
   299	        self.resource_change_ticks
   300	            .insert(resource_type, self.change_tick);
   301	        self.resource_change_log.push(ResourceChangeRecord {
   302	            tick: self.change_tick,
   303	            resource_type,
   304	            resource_name,
   305	            kind,
   306	        });
   307	    }
   308	
   309	    pub(super) fn trigger_observers(
   310	        &mut self,
   311	        event_type: TypeId,
   312	        event_type_name: &'static str,
   313	        trigger: ObserverTrigger,
   314	        event_count: usize,
   315	    ) {
   316	        for observer in self.event_observers.values_mut() {
   317	            if observer.event_type != event_type || observer.trigger != trigger {
   318	                continue;
   319	            }
   320	            observer.invocations = observer.invocations.saturating_add(1);
   321	            self.event_observer_notifications
   322	                .push(EventObserverNotification {
   323	                    observer_id: observer.observer_id.clone(),
   324	                    trigger: trigger.clone(),
   325	                    event_type: event_type_name,
   326	                    event_count,
   327	                });
   328	        }
   329	    }
   330	
   331	    pub(super) fn mark_component_indexes_dirty(&mut self, component_type: TypeId) {
   332	        let mut indexes = self.component_indexes.borrow_mut();
   333	        for (index_key, index) in indexes.iter_mut() {
   334	            if index_key.component_type == component_type {
   335	                index.mark_dirty();
   336	            }
   337	        }
   338	    }
   339	
   340	    pub(super) fn remove_entity_from_spatial_indexes(&mut self, entity: Entity) {
   341	        for index in self.spatial_indexes.values_mut() {
   342	            index.remove(entity);
   343	        }
   344	    }
   345	}

===== END FILE: ./src/world/world_internal_impl.rs =====

===== FILE: ./src/world/world_spatial_impl.rs =====
     1	// Owner: ecs World - Spatial Index APIs
     2	use super::world_struct::World;
     3	use crate::entity::Entity;
     4	use crate::errors::SpatialIndexError;
     5	use crate::indexing::{DEFAULT_SPATIAL_INDEX_NAME, SpatialHashConfig, SpatialHashIndex};
     6	use geometry::Aabb3;
     7	
     8	fn normalized_index_name(name: impl Into<String>) -> String {
     9	    let mut name = name.into();
    10	    name = name.trim().to_string();
    11	    if name.is_empty() {
    12	        name = DEFAULT_SPATIAL_INDEX_NAME.to_string();
    13	    }
    14	    name
    15	}
    16	
    17	impl World {
    18	    pub fn ensure_spatial_hash_index(
    19	        &mut self,
    20	        config: SpatialHashConfig,
    21	    ) -> Result<bool, SpatialIndexError> {
    22	        self.ensure_spatial_hash_index_named(DEFAULT_SPATIAL_INDEX_NAME, config)
    23	    }
    24	
    25	    pub fn ensure_spatial_hash_index_named(
    26	        &mut self,
    27	        name: impl Into<String>,
    28	        config: SpatialHashConfig,
    29	    ) -> Result<bool, SpatialIndexError> {
    30	        let name = normalized_index_name(name);
    31	        if self.spatial_indexes.contains_key(&name) {
    32	            return Ok(false);
    33	        }
    34	        let index = SpatialHashIndex::new(config)?;
    35	        self.spatial_indexes.insert(name, Box::new(index));
    36	        Ok(true)
    37	    }
    38	
    39	    pub fn spatial_insert(
    40	        &mut self,
    41	        entity: Entity,
    42	        bounds: Aabb3,
    43	    ) -> Result<(), SpatialIndexError> {
    44	        self.spatial_insert_named(DEFAULT_SPATIAL_INDEX_NAME, entity, bounds)
    45	    }
    46	
    47	    pub fn spatial_insert_named(
    48	        &mut self,
    49	        name: impl Into<String>,
    50	        entity: Entity,
    51	        bounds: Aabb3,
    52	    ) -> Result<(), SpatialIndexError> {
    53	        self.ensure_entity_exists(entity)?;
    54	        let name = normalized_index_name(name);
    55	        let index = self
    56	            .spatial_indexes
    57	            .get_mut(&name)
    58	            .ok_or(SpatialIndexError::MissingIndex { name })?;
    59	        index.insert(entity, bounds)
    60	    }
    61	
    62	    pub fn spatial_update(
    63	        &mut self,
    64	        entity: Entity,
    65	        bounds: Aabb3,
    66	    ) -> Result<(), SpatialIndexError> {
    67	        self.spatial_update_named(DEFAULT_SPATIAL_INDEX_NAME, entity, bounds)
    68	    }
    69	
    70	    pub fn spatial_update_named(
    71	        &mut self,
    72	        name: impl Into<String>,
    73	        entity: Entity,
    74	        bounds: Aabb3,
    75	    ) -> Result<(), SpatialIndexError> {
    76	        self.ensure_entity_exists(entity)?;
    77	        let name = normalized_index_name(name);
    78	        let index = self
    79	            .spatial_indexes
    80	            .get_mut(&name)
    81	            .ok_or(SpatialIndexError::MissingIndex { name })?;
    82	        index.update(entity, bounds)
    83	    }
    84	
    85	    pub fn spatial_remove(&mut self, entity: Entity) -> Result<bool, SpatialIndexError> {
    86	        self.spatial_remove_named(DEFAULT_SPATIAL_INDEX_NAME, entity)
    87	    }
    88	
    89	    pub fn spatial_remove_named(
    90	        &mut self,
    91	        name: impl Into<String>,
    92	        entity: Entity,
    93	    ) -> Result<bool, SpatialIndexError> {
    94	        self.ensure_entity_exists(entity)?;
    95	        let name = normalized_index_name(name);
    96	        let index = self
    97	            .spatial_indexes
    98	            .get_mut(&name)
    99	            .ok_or(SpatialIndexError::MissingIndex { name })?;
   100	        Ok(index.remove(entity))
   101	    }
   102	
   103	    pub fn spatial_query_aabb(&self, bounds: Aabb3) -> Result<Vec<Entity>, SpatialIndexError> {
   104	        self.spatial_query_aabb_named(DEFAULT_SPATIAL_INDEX_NAME, bounds)
   105	    }
   106	
   107	    pub fn spatial_query_aabb_named(
   108	        &self,
   109	        name: impl Into<String>,
   110	        bounds: Aabb3,
   111	    ) -> Result<Vec<Entity>, SpatialIndexError> {
   112	        let name = normalized_index_name(name);
   113	        let index = self
   114	            .spatial_indexes
   115	            .get(&name)
   116	            .ok_or(SpatialIndexError::MissingIndex { name })?;
   117	        index.query_aabb(bounds)
   118	    }
   119	}

     1	// Owner: ecs World - World State and Default Construction

    15	    pub(super) allocator: EntityAllocator,
    16	    pub(super) alive_entities: BTreeSet<Entity>,
    17	    pub(super) component_registry: HashMap<TypeId, ComponentMeta>,
    18	    pub(super) next_component_id: u32,

    22	    pub(super) event_observer_notifications: Vec<EventObserverNotification>,
    23	    pub(super) component_indexes:
    24	        RefCell<HashMap<ComponentIndexKey, Box<dyn ComponentIndexStorage>>>,
