    29	    pub(super) component_change_ticks: HashMap<TypeId, u64>,
    30	    pub(super) resource_change_ticks: HashMap<TypeId, u64>,
    31	    pub(super) component_change_log: Vec<ComponentChangeRecord>,
    32	    pub(super) removed_component_records: HashMap<TypeId, Vec<RemovedComponentRecord>>,
    33	    pub(super) resource_change_log: Vec<ResourceChangeRecord>,
    34	}

     1	use ecs::prelude::*;
     2	use scheduler::ScheduleLabel;
     3	
     4	#[derive(ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
     5	struct Position {
     6	    x: f32,
     7	    y: f32,
     8	}
     9	
    10	#[derive(ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
    11	struct Velocity {
    12	    x: f32,
    13	    y: f32,
    14	}
    15	
    16	#[derive(ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
    17	struct Simulated;
    18	
    19	#[derive(ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
    20	struct DeltaTime(pub f32);
    21	
    22	#[derive(ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
    23	struct Frame(pub u64);
    24	
    25	fn tick(
    26	    mut query: Query<(&mut Position, &Velocity), With<Simulated>>,
    27	    dt: Res<DeltaTime>,
    28	    mut frame: ResMut<Frame>,
    29	) {
    30	    for (pos, vel) in query.iter() {
    31	        pos.x += vel.x * dt.0;
    32	        pos.y += vel.y * dt.0;
    33	    }
    34	    frame.0 += 1;
    35	}
    36	
    37	fn event_system(mut writer: EventWriter<u32>, reader: EventReader<u32>) {
    38	    writer.send(1);
    39	    let _ = reader.iter().count();
    40	}
    41	
    42	#[test]
    43	fn docs_gameplay_signatures_compile() {
    44	    let _ = tick as fn(
    45	        Query<(&mut Position, &Velocity), With<Simulated>>,
    46	        Res<DeltaTime>,
    47	        ResMut<Frame>,
    48	    );
    49	    let _ = event_system as fn(EventWriter<u32>, EventReader<u32>);
    50	}
    51	
    52	#[test]
    53	fn docs_runtime_query_snippet_runs() {
    54	    let mut world = World::new();
    55	    world.spawn((
    56	        Position { x: 1.0, y: 2.0 },
    57	        Velocity { x: 0.5, y: -1.0 },
    58	        Simulated,
    59	    ));
    60	    world.insert_resource(DeltaTime(0.5));
    61	    world.insert_resource(Frame(1));
    62	
    63	    let query = world
    64	        .query_state::<(&mut Position, &Velocity), ()>()
    65	        .with::<Simulated>();
    66	    for (position, velocity) in query.iter(&mut world) {
    67	        position.x += velocity.x;
    68	        position.y += velocity.y;
    69	    }
    70	
    71	    assert_eq!(world.resource::<Frame>().unwrap().0, 1);
    72	}

    83	#[test]
    84	fn docs_runtime_execution_snippet_runs() {
    85	    fn advance(mut query: Query<&mut Position>, dt: Res<DeltaTime>, mut frame: ResMut<Frame>) {
    86	        for position in query.iter() {
    87	            position.x += dt.0;
    88	            position.y += dt.0;
    89	        }
    90	        frame.0 += 1;
    91	    }
    92	
    93	    let mut world = World::new();
    94	    world.spawn(Position { x: 0.0, y: 0.0 });
    95	    world.insert_resource(DeltaTime(0.25));
    96	    world.insert_resource(Frame(0));
    97	
    98	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
    99	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, advance);
   100	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   101	
   102	    let pos = world.query_state::<&Position, ()>().single(&world).unwrap();
   103	    assert_eq!(pos.x, 0.25);
   104	    assert_eq!(world.resource::<Frame>().unwrap().0, 1);
   105	}

   107	#[test]
   108	fn docs_change_filter_snippet_runs() {
   109	    let mut world = World::new();
   110	    let entity = world.spawn(Position { x: 0.0, y: 0.0 });
   111	    let changed_positions = world.query_state::<(Entity, &Position), Changed<Position>>();
   112	
   113	    let first: Vec<_> = changed_positions
   114	        .iter(&world)
   115	        .map(|(entity, _)| entity)
   116	        .collect();
   117	    assert_eq!(first, vec![entity]);
   118	    assert!(changed_positions.iter(&world).next().is_none());
   119	
   120	    world.require_mut::<Position>(entity).unwrap().x = 1.0;
   121	    let second: Vec<_> = changed_positions
   122	        .iter(&world)
   123	        .map(|(entity, _)| entity)
   124	        .collect();
   125	    assert_eq!(second, vec![entity]);
   126	}

    81	#[test]
    82	fn explicit_remove_is_not_visible_before_flush_and_visible_after_flush() {
    83	    fn queue_remove_once(mut gate: ResMut<Gate>, target: Res<Target>, mut commands: Commands) {
    84	        if gate.0 {
    85	            return;
    86	        }
    87	        commands.remove::<A>(target.0);
    88	        gate.0 = true;
    89	    }
    90	
    91	    fn observe_same_stage(mut orphaned: QueryOrphaned<A>, mut counts: ResMut<StageCounts>) {
    92	        counts.same_stage.push(orphaned.iter().count());
    93	    }
    94	
    95	    fn observe_post_stage(mut orphaned: QueryOrphaned<A>, mut counts: ResMut<StageCounts>) {
    96	        counts.post_stage.push(orphaned.iter().count());
    97	    }
    98	
    99	    let mut world = World::new();
   100	    let entity = world.spawn(A(1));
   101	    world.insert_resource(Target(entity));
   102	    world.insert_resource(Gate(false));
   103	    world.insert_resource(StageCounts::default());
   104	
   105	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   106	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, queue_remove_once.in_set(QueueSet));
   107	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, observe_same_stage.in_set(QueueSet));
   108	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(
   109	        &mut world,
   110	        observe_post_stage.in_set(ObserveSet).after(QueueSet),
   111	    );
   112	
   113	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   114	
   115	    let counts = world.resource::<StageCounts>().unwrap();
   116	    assert_eq!(counts.same_stage, vec![0]);
   117	    assert_eq!(counts.post_stage, vec![1]);
   118	}
   119

   154	fn orphaned_records_are_visible_only_for_one_stage_window() {
   155	    fn queue_remove_once(mut gate: ResMut<Gate>, target: Res<Target>, mut commands: Commands) {
   156	        if gate.0 {
   157	            return;
   158	        }
   159	        commands.remove::<A>(target.0);
   160	        gate.0 = true;
   161	    }

   164	        counts.post_stage.push(orphaned.iter().count());
   165	    }
   166	
   167	    fn observe_late_stage(mut orphaned: QueryOrphaned<A>, mut counts: ResMut<StageCounts>) {
   168	        counts.late_stage.push(orphaned.iter().count());
   169	    }

   195	#[test]
   196	fn multiple_removals_in_one_stage_are_reported() {
   197	    fn queue_remove_pair_once(
   198	        mut gate: ResMut<Gate>,
   199	        targets: Res<TargetPair>,
   200	        mut commands: Commands,
   201	    ) {
   202	        if gate.0 {
   203	            return;
   204	        }
   205	        commands.remove::<A>(targets.0);
   206	        commands.remove::<A>(targets.1);
   207	        gate.0 = true;
   208	    }
   209	
   210	    fn observe_entities(mut orphaned: QueryOrphaned<A>, mut history: ResMut<EntityHistory>) {
   211	        let mut entities = orphaned
   212	            .iter()
   213	            .map(|record| record.entity())
   214	            .collect::<Vec<_>>();
   215	        entities.sort_unstable();
   216	        history.0.push(entities);
   217	    }
   218	
   219	    let mut world = World::new();
   220	    let first = world.spawn(A(10));
   221	    let second = world.spawn(A(11));
   222	    world.insert_resource(TargetPair(first, second));
   223	    world.insert_resource(Gate(false));
   224	    world.insert_resource(EntityHistory::default());
   225	
   226	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   227	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, queue_remove_pair_once.in_set(QueueSet));
   228	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(
   229	        &mut world,
   230	        observe_entities.in_set(ObserveSet).after(QueueSet),
   231	    );
   232	
   233	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   234	
   235	    let mut expected = vec![first, second];
   236	    expected.sort_unstable();
   237	    assert_eq!(world.resource::<EntityHistory>().unwrap().0, vec![expected]);
   238	}

   240	#[test]
   241	fn query_orphaned_is_component_type_isolated() {
   242	    fn queue_type_specific_removes_once(
   243	        mut gate: ResMut<Gate>,
   244	        targets: Res<TargetPair>,
   245	        mut commands: Commands,
   246	    ) {
   247	        if gate.0 {
   248	            return;
   249	        }
   250	        commands.remove::<A>(targets.0);
   251	        commands.remove::<B>(targets.1);
   252	        gate.0 = true;
   253	    }
   254	
   255	    fn observe_type_isolation(
   256	        mut orphaned_a: QueryOrphaned<A>,
   257	        mut orphaned_b: QueryOrphaned<B>,
   258	        mut counts: ResMut<TypeIsolationCounts>,
   259	    ) {
   260	        counts.a_entities = orphaned_a.iter().map(|record| record.entity()).collect();
   261	        counts.b_entities = orphaned_b.iter().map(|record| record.entity()).collect();
   262	    }
   263	
   264	    let mut world = World::new();
   265	    let entity_a = world.spawn((A(4), B(14)));
   266	    let entity_b = world.spawn((A(5), B(15)));
   267	    world.insert_resource(TargetPair(entity_a, entity_b));
   268	    world.insert_resource(Gate(false));
   269	    world.insert_resource(TypeIsolationCounts::default());
   270	
   271	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   272	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(
   273	        &mut world,
   274	        queue_type_specific_removes_once.in_set(QueueSet),
   275	    );
   276	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(
   277	        &mut world,
   278	        observe_type_isolation.in_set(ObserveSet).after(QueueSet),
   279	    );
   280	
   281	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   282	
   283	    let counts = world.resource::<TypeIsolationCounts>().unwrap();
   284	    assert_eq!(counts.a_entities, vec![entity_a]);
   285	    assert_eq!(counts.b_entities, vec![entity_b]);
   286	}

   288	#[test]
   289	fn orphaned_entries_do_not_repeat_across_later_runs() {
   290	    fn queue_remove_once(mut gate: ResMut<Gate>, target: Res<Target>, mut commands: Commands) {
   291	        if gate.0 {
   292	            return;
   293	        }
   294	        commands.remove::<A>(target.0);
   295	        gate.0 = true;
   296	    }
   297	
   298	    fn observe_post_stage(mut orphaned: QueryOrphaned<A>, mut counts: ResMut<StageCounts>) {
   299	        counts.post_stage.push(orphaned.iter().count());
   300	    }
   301	
   302	    let mut world = World::new();
   303	    let entity = world.spawn(A(6));
   304	    world.insert_resource(Target(entity));
   305	    world.insert_resource(Gate(false));
   306	    world.insert_resource(StageCounts::default());
   307	
   308	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   309	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, queue_remove_once.in_set(QueueSet));
   310	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(
   311	        &mut world,
   312	        observe_post_stage.in_set(ObserveSet).after(QueueSet),
   313	    );
   314	
   315	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   316	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   317	
   318	    let counts = world.resource::<StageCounts>().unwrap();
   319	    assert_eq!(counts.post_stage, vec![1, 0]);
   320	}

   322	#[test]
   323	fn repeated_iter_calls_return_same_window_snapshot() {
   324	    fn queue_remove_once(mut gate: ResMut<Gate>, target: Res<Target>, mut commands: Commands) {
   325	        if gate.0 {
   326	            return;
   327	        }
   328	        commands.remove::<A>(target.0);
   329	        gate.0 = true;
   330	    }
   331	
   332	    fn observe_twice(mut orphaned: QueryOrphaned<A>, mut counts: ResMut<DoubleReadCounts>) {
   333	        let first = orphaned.iter().count();
   334	        let second = orphaned.iter().count();
   335	        counts.0.push((first, second));
   336	    }
   337	
   338	    let mut world = World::new();
   339	    let entity = world.spawn(A(7));
   340	    world.insert_resource(Target(entity));
   341	    world.insert_resource(Gate(false));
   342	    world.insert_resource(DoubleReadCounts::default());
   343	
   344	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   345	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, queue_remove_once.in_set(QueueSet));
   346	    runtime
   347	        .add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, observe_twice.in_set(ObserveSet).after(QueueSet));
   348	
   349	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   350	
   351	    let counts = world.resource::<DoubleReadCounts>().unwrap();
   352	    assert_eq!(counts.0, vec![(1, 1)]);
   353	}

   355	#[test]
   356	fn remove_then_reinsert_in_one_flush_still_reports_orphaned_removal() {
   357	    fn queue_remove_then_reinsert_once(
   358	        mut gate: ResMut<Gate>,
   359	        target: Res<Target>,
   360	        mut commands: Commands,
   361	    ) {
   362	        if gate.0 {
   363	            return;
   364	        }
   365	        commands.remove::<A>(target.0);
   366	        commands.insert(target.0, A(99));
   367	        gate.0 = true;
   368	    }
   369	
   370	    fn observe_window(
   371	        mut orphaned: QueryOrphaned<A>,
   372	        mut live: Query<&A>,
   373	        mut snapshot: ResMut<WindowSnapshot>,
   374	    ) {
   375	        snapshot.orphaned.push(orphaned.iter().count());
   376	        snapshot.live.push(live.iter().count());
   377	    }
   378	
   379	    let mut world = World::new();
   380	    let entity = world.spawn(A(8));
   381	    world.insert_resource(Target(entity));
   382	    world.insert_resource(Gate(false));
   383	    world.insert_resource(WindowSnapshot::default());
   384	
   385	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   386	    runtime
   387	        .add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, queue_remove_then_reinsert_once.in_set(QueueSet));
   388	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(
   389	        &mut world,
   390	        observe_window.in_set(ObserveSet).after(QueueSet),
   391	    );
   392	
   393	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   394	
   395	    let snapshot = world.resource::<WindowSnapshot>().unwrap();
   396	    assert_eq!(snapshot.orphaned, vec![1]);
   397	    assert_eq!(snapshot.live, vec![1]);
   398	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(entity).unwrap().0, 99);
   399	}

   401	#[test]
   402	fn previous_run_orphaned_window_is_visible_in_next_run_first_stage_only() {
   403	    fn queue_remove_once(mut gate: ResMut<Gate>, target: Res<Target>, mut commands: Commands) {
   404	        if gate.0 {
   405	            return;
   406	        }
   407	        commands.remove::<A>(target.0);
   408	        gate.0 = true;
   409	    }
   410	
   411	    fn observe_same_stage(mut orphaned: QueryOrphaned<A>, mut counts: ResMut<StageCounts>) {
   412	        counts.same_stage.push(orphaned.iter().count());
   413	    }
   414	
   415	    let mut world = World::new();
   416	    let entity = world.spawn(A(9));
   417	    world.insert_resource(Target(entity));
   418	    world.insert_resource(Gate(false));
   419	    world.insert_resource(StageCounts::default());
   420	
   421	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   422	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(
   423	        &mut world,

   426	            observe_same_stage.in_set(QueueSet),
   427	        ),
   428	    );
   429	
   430	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   431	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();

   433

   435	    assert_eq!(counts.same_stage, vec![0, 1, 0]);
   436	}

   438	#[test]
   439	fn query_orphaned_does_not_conflict_with_live_mut_query_access() {
   440	    fn mutate_live(mut query: Query<&mut A>) {
   441	        for value in query.iter() {
   442	            value.0 += 1;
   443	        }
   444	    }
   445	
   446	    fn observe_orphaned(mut orphaned: QueryOrphaned<A>, mut counts: ResMut<StageCounts>) {
   447	        counts.same_stage.push(orphaned.iter().count());
   448	    }
   449	
   450	    let mut world = World::new();
   451	    let entity = world.spawn(A(3));
   452	    world.insert_resource(StageCounts::default());
   453	
   454	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   455	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, (mutate_live, observe_orphaned));
   456	
   457	    let plan = runtime.plan_for::<Update>().unwrap().clone();
   458	    assert_eq!(plan.conflicts.len(), 0);
   459	    assert_eq!(plan.stages.len(), 1);
   460	    assert_eq!(plan.stages[0].system_indices.len(), 2);
   461	
   462	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   463	
   464	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(entity).unwrap().0, 4);
   465	    assert_eq!(world.resource::<StageCounts>().unwrap().same_stage, vec![0]);
   466	}

   468	#[test]
   469	fn batch_remove_and_despawn_preserve_orphaned_stage_window_semantics() {
   470	    fn queue_batch_once(mut gate: ResMut<Gate>, targets: Res<TargetPair>, mut commands: Commands) {
   471	        if gate.0 {
   472	            return;
   473	        }
   474	        commands.batch(|batch| {
   475	            batch.remove::<A>(targets.0);
   476	            batch.despawn(targets.1);
   477	        });
   478	        gate.0 = true;
   479	    }
   480	
   481	    fn observe_same_stage(mut orphaned: QueryOrphaned<A>, mut counts: ResMut<StageCounts>) {
   482	        counts.same_stage.push(orphaned.iter().count());
   483	    }
   484	
   485	    fn observe_post_stage(mut orphaned: QueryOrphaned<A>, mut counts: ResMut<StageCounts>) {
   486	        counts.post_stage.push(orphaned.iter().count());
   487	    }
   488	
   489	    let mut world = World::new();
   490	    let remove_only = world.spawn((A(20), B(1)));
   491	    let despawn_target = world.spawn((A(21), B(2)));
   492	    world.insert_resource(TargetPair(remove_only, despawn_target));
   493	    world.insert_resource(Gate(false));
   494	    world.insert_resource(StageCounts::default());
   495	
   496	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   497	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, queue_batch_once.in_set(QueueSet));
   498	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, observe_same_stage.in_set(QueueSet));
   499	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(
   500	        &mut world,
   501	        observe_post_stage.in_set(ObserveSet).after(QueueSet),
   502	    );
   503	
   504	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   505	
   506	    let counts = world.resource::<StageCounts>().unwrap();
   507	    assert_eq!(counts.same_stage, vec![0]);
   508	    assert_eq!(counts.post_stage, vec![2]);
   509	}

    50	#[test]
    51	fn dominant_query_forms_remain_correct_with_archetype_matching() {
    52	    let mut world = World::new();
    53	    let e1 = world.spawn((A(1), B(10)));
    54	    let e2 = world.spawn(A(2));
    55	    let e3 = world.spawn((A(3), B(30)));
    56	
    57	    for a in world.query_state::<&mut A, ()>().iter(&mut world) {
    58	        a.0 += 1;
    59	    }
    60	
    61	    for (a, b) in world.query_state::<(&mut A, &B), ()>().iter(&mut world) {
    62	        a.0 += b.0;
    63	    }
    64	
    65	    for (a, b) in world.query_state::<(&mut A, &mut B), ()>().iter(&mut world) {
    66	        a.0 += b.0;
    67	        b.0 += 1;
    68	    }
    69	
    70	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(e1).unwrap().0, 22);
    71	    assert_eq!(world.require::<B>(e1).unwrap().0, 11);
    72	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(e2).unwrap().0, 3);
    73	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(e3).unwrap().0, 64);
    74	    assert_eq!(world.require::<B>(e3).unwrap().0, 31);
    75	}

    77	#[test]
    78	fn changed_added_and_remove_reinsert_semantics_are_preserved() {
    79	    let mut world = World::new();
    80	    let entity = world.spawn(A(5));
    81	
    82	    let added = world.query_state::<(Entity, &A), Added<A>>();
    83	    assert_eq!(
    84	        added
    85	            .iter(&world)
    86	            .map(|(entity, _)| entity)
    87	            .collect::<Vec<_>>(),
    88	        vec![entity]
    89	    );
    90	    assert!(added.iter(&world).next().is_none());
    91	
    92	    let changed = world.query_state::<(Entity, &A), Changed<A>>();
    93	    assert_eq!(
    94	        changed
    95	            .iter(&world)
    96	            .map(|(entity, _)| entity)
    97	            .collect::<Vec<_>>(),
    98	        vec![entity]
    99	    );
   100	    assert!(changed.iter(&world).next().is_none());
   101	
   102	    let _: A = world.remove(entity).unwrap();
   103	    assert!(added.iter(&world).next().is_none());
   104	    assert!(changed.iter(&world).next().is_none());
   105	
   106	    world.insert(entity, A(9)).unwrap();
   107	    assert_eq!(
   108	        added
   109	            .iter(&world)
   110	            .map(|(entity, _)| entity)
   111	            .collect::<Vec<_>>(),
   112	        vec![entity]
   113	    );
   114	    assert_eq!(
   115	        changed
   116	            .iter(&world)
   117	            .map(|(entity, _)| entity)
   118	            .collect::<Vec<_>>(),
   119	        vec![entity]
   120	    );
   121	}

   123	#[test]
   124	fn reused_query_state_observes_new_matching_archetypes_and_fallback_forms() {
   125	    let mut world = World::new();
   126	    let evolving = world.spawn(A(7));
   127	    let hidden = world.spawn((A(8), Disabled));
   128	
   129	    let dominant = world.query_state::<(&mut A, &B), ()>();
   130	    assert!(dominant.iter(&mut world).next().is_none());
   131	    world.insert(evolving, B(2)).unwrap();
   132	
   133	    let mut seen = Vec::new();
   134	    for (a, b) in dominant.iter(&mut world) {
   135	        a.0 += b.0;
   136	        seen.push(a.0);
   137	    }
   138	    assert_eq!(seen, vec![9]);
   139	
   140	    let fallback = world
   141	        .query_state::<(Entity, &A), ()>()
   142	        .without::<Disabled>();
   143	    let visible: Vec<_> = fallback
   144	        .iter(&world)
   145	        .map(|(entity, a)| (entity, a.0))
   146	        .collect();
   147	    assert_eq!(visible, vec![(evolving, 9)]);
   148	    assert!(visible.iter().all(|(entity, _)| *entity != hidden));
   149	}

   264	fn reused_single_mut_query_state_stays_correct_across_archetype_migration() {
   265	    let mut world = World::new();
   266	    let entity = world.spawn(A(10));
   267	    let query = world.query_state::<&mut A, ()>();
   268	    let changed = world.query_state::<(Entity, &A), Changed<A>>();
   269	
   270	    assert_eq!(
   271	        changed
   272	            .iter(&world)
   273	            .map(|(entity, _)| entity)
   274	            .collect::<Vec<_>>(),

   276	    );

   278

   296	            .iter(&world)
   297	            .map(|(entity, _)| entity)
   298	            .collect::<Vec<_>>(),
   299	        vec![entity]
   300	    );
   301	
   302	    let _: B = world.remove(entity).unwrap();
   303	    for value in query.iter(&mut world) {
   304	        value.0 += 4;
   305	    }
   306	    assert_eq!(
   307	        changed
   308	            .iter(&world)
   309	            .map(|(entity, _)| entity)
   310	            .collect::<Vec<_>>(),
   311	        vec![entity]
   312	    );
   313	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(entity).unwrap().0, 17);
   314	}

   317	fn tuple_mut_read_query_updates_only_mutable_side_change_tracking() {
   318	    let mut world = World::new();
   319	    let entity = world.spawn((A(5), B(7)));
   320	    let changed_a = world.query_state::<(Entity, &A), Changed<A>>();
   321	    let changed_b = world.query_state::<(Entity, &B), Changed<B>>();
   322	
   323	    assert_eq!(
   324	        changed_a
   325	            .iter(&world)
   326	            .map(|(entity, _)| entity)
   327	            .collect::<Vec<_>>(),
   328	        vec![entity]
   329	    );
   330	    assert_eq!(
   331	        changed_b
   332	            .iter(&world)
   333	            .map(|(entity, _)| entity)
   334	            .collect::<Vec<_>>(),
   335	        vec![entity]
   336	    );
   337	    assert!(changed_a.iter(&world).next().is_none());
   338	    assert!(changed_b.iter(&world).next().is_none());
   339	
   340	    let (a_added_before, a_changed_before) = world
   341	        .__entity_component_ticks::<A>(entity)
   342	        .expect("A ticks should exist");
   343	    let (b_added_before, b_changed_before) = world
   344	        .__entity_component_ticks::<B>(entity)
   345	        .expect("B ticks should exist");
   346	
   347	    for (a, b) in world.query_state::<(&mut A, &B), ()>().iter(&mut world) {
   348	        a.0 += b.0;
   349	    }
   350	
   351	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(entity).unwrap().0, 12);
   352	    assert_eq!(world.require::<B>(entity).unwrap().0, 7);
   353	    assert_eq!(
   354	        changed_a
   355	            .iter(&world)
   356	            .map(|(entity, _)| entity)
   357	            .collect::<Vec<_>>(),
   358	        vec![entity]
   359	    );
   360	    assert!(changed_b.iter(&world).next().is_none());
   361	
   362	    let (a_added_after, a_changed_after) = world
   363	        .__entity_component_ticks::<A>(entity)
   364	        .expect("A ticks should exist");
   365	    let (b_added_after, b_changed_after) = world
   366	        .__entity_component_ticks::<B>(entity)
   367	        .expect("B ticks should exist");
   368	    assert_eq!(a_added_after, a_added_before);
   369	    assert!(a_changed_after > a_changed_before);
   370	    assert_eq!(b_added_after, b_added_before);
   371	    assert_eq!(b_changed_after, b_changed_before);
   372	}

   374	#[test]
   375	fn tuple_mut_read_query_preserves_pairing_across_component_migration() {
   376	    let mut world = World::new();
   377	    let first = world.spawn((A(1), B(10)));
   378	    let second = world.spawn((A(2), B(20)));
   379	    let query = world.query_state::<(&mut A, &B), ()>();
   380	
   381	    let (first_b_added_before, first_b_changed_before) = world
   382	        .__entity_component_ticks::<B>(first)
   383	        .expect("B ticks should exist");
   384	
   385	    for (a, b) in query.iter(&mut world) {
   386	        a.0 += b.0;
   387	    }
   388	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(first).unwrap().0, 11);
   389	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(second).unwrap().0, 22);
   390	
   391	    world.insert(first, C(99)).unwrap();
   392	    for (a, b) in query.iter(&mut world) {
   393	        a.0 += b.0;
   394	    }
   395	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(first).unwrap().0, 21);
   396	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(second).unwrap().0, 42);
   397	
   398	    let _: C = world.remove(first).unwrap();
   399	    for (a, b) in query.iter(&mut world) {
   400	        a.0 += b.0;
   401	    }
   402	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(first).unwrap().0, 31);
   403	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(second).unwrap().0, 62);
   404	    assert_eq!(world.require::<B>(first).unwrap().0, 10);
   405	    assert_eq!(world.require::<B>(second).unwrap().0, 20);
   406	
   407	    let (first_b_added_after, first_b_changed_after) = world
   408	        .__entity_component_ticks::<B>(first)
   409	        .expect("B ticks should exist");
   410	    assert_eq!(first_b_added_after, first_b_added_before);
   411	    assert_eq!(first_b_changed_after, first_b_changed_before);
   412	}

   415	fn tuple_double_mut_query_updates_changed_ticks_for_both_components() {
   416	    let mut world = World::new();
   417	    let entity = world.spawn((A(4), B(9)));
   418	    let changed_a = world.query_state::<(Entity, &A), Changed<A>>();
   419	    let changed_b = world.query_state::<(Entity, &B), Changed<B>>();

   442	        .__entity_component_ticks::<B>(entity)
   443	        .expect("B ticks should exist");

   448	    }

   462	            .map(|(entity, _)| entity)
   463	            .collect::<Vec<_>>(),
   464	        vec![entity]
   465	    );
   466	
   467	    let (a_added_after, a_changed_after) = world
   468	        .__entity_component_ticks::<A>(entity)
   469	        .expect("A ticks should exist");
   470	    let (b_added_after, b_changed_after) = world
   471	        .__entity_component_ticks::<B>(entity)
   472	        .expect("B ticks should exist");
   473	    assert_eq!(a_added_after, a_added_before);
   474	    assert!(a_changed_after > a_changed_before);
   475	    assert_eq!(b_added_after, b_added_before);
   476	    assert!(b_changed_after > b_changed_before);
   477	}

   479	#[test]
   480	fn tuple_double_mut_query_preserves_pairing_across_component_migration() {
   481	    let mut world = World::new();
   482	    let first = world.spawn((A(1), B(10)));
   483	    let second = world.spawn((A(2), B(20)));
   484	    let query = world.query_state::<(&mut A, &mut B), ()>();
   485	
   486	    for (a, b) in query.iter(&mut world) {
   487	        let old_a = a.0;
   488	        let old_b = b.0;
   489	        a.0 = old_a + old_b;
   490	        b.0 = old_b - old_a;
   491	    }
   492	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(first).unwrap().0, 11);
   493	    assert_eq!(world.require::<B>(first).unwrap().0, 9);
   494	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(second).unwrap().0, 22);
   495	    assert_eq!(world.require::<B>(second).unwrap().0, 18);
   496	
   497	    world.insert(first, C(99)).unwrap();
   498	    for (a, b) in query.iter(&mut world) {
   499	        let old_a = a.0;
   500	        let old_b = b.0;
   501	        a.0 = old_a + old_b;
   502	        b.0 = old_b - old_a;
   503	    }
   504	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(first).unwrap().0, 20);
   505	    assert_eq!(world.require::<B>(first).unwrap().0, -2);
   506	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(second).unwrap().0, 40);
   507	    assert_eq!(world.require::<B>(second).unwrap().0, -4);
   508	
   509	    let _: C = world.remove(first).unwrap();
   510	    for (a, b) in query.iter(&mut world) {
   511	        let old_a = a.0;
   512	        let old_b = b.0;
   513	        a.0 = old_a + old_b;
   514	        b.0 = old_b - old_a;
   515	    }
   516	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(first).unwrap().0, 18);
   517	    assert_eq!(world.require::<B>(first).unwrap().0, -22);
   518	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(second).unwrap().0, 36);
   519	    assert_eq!(world.require::<B>(second).unwrap().0, -44);
   520	}

   522	#[test]
   523	fn reused_double_mut_query_state_stays_correct_across_archetype_migration() {
   524	    let mut world = World::new();
   525	    let entity = world.spawn((A(3), B(7)));
   526	    let query = world.query_state::<(&mut A, &mut B), ()>();
   527	    let changed_a = world.query_state::<(Entity, &A), Changed<A>>();
   528	    let changed_b = world.query_state::<(Entity, &B), Changed<B>>();
   529	
   530	    assert_eq!(
   531	        changed_a
   532	            .iter(&world)
   533	            .map(|(entity, _)| entity)
   534	            .collect::<Vec<_>>(),
   535	        vec![entity]
   536	    );
   537	    assert_eq!(
   538	        changed_b
   539	            .iter(&world)
   540	            .map(|(entity, _)| entity)
   541	            .collect::<Vec<_>>(),
   542	        vec![entity]
   543	    );
   544	    assert!(changed_a.iter(&world).next().is_none());
   545	    assert!(changed_b.iter(&world).next().is_none());
   546	
   547	    for (a, b) in query.iter(&mut world) {
   548	        a.0 += 1;
   549	        b.0 += 2;
   550	    }
   551	    assert_eq!(
   552	        changed_a
   553	            .iter(&world)
   554	            .map(|(entity, _)| entity)
   555	            .collect::<Vec<_>>(),
   556	        vec![entity]
   557	    );
   558	    assert_eq!(
   559	        changed_b
   560	            .iter(&world)
   561	            .map(|(entity, _)| entity)
   562	            .collect::<Vec<_>>(),
   563	        vec![entity]
   564	    );
   565	
   566	    world.insert(entity, C(1)).unwrap();
   567	    for (a, b) in query.iter(&mut world) {
   568	        a.0 += 1;
   569	        b.0 += 2;
   570	    }
   571	    assert_eq!(
   572	        changed_a
   573	            .iter(&world)
   574	            .map(|(entity, _)| entity)
   575	            .collect::<Vec<_>>(),
   576	        vec![entity]
   577	    );
   578	    assert_eq!(
   579	        changed_b
   580	            .iter(&world)
   581	            .map(|(entity, _)| entity)
   582	            .collect::<Vec<_>>(),
   583	        vec![entity]
   584	    );
   585	
   586	    let _: C = world.remove(entity).unwrap();
   587	    for (a, b) in query.iter(&mut world) {
   588	        a.0 += 1;
   589	        b.0 += 2;
   590	    }
   591	    assert_eq!(
   592	        changed_a
   593	            .iter(&world)
   594	            .map(|(entity, _)| entity)
   595	            .collect::<Vec<_>>(),
   596	        vec![entity]
   597	    );
   598	    assert_eq!(
   599	        changed_b
   600	            .iter(&world)
   601	            .map(|(entity, _)| entity)
   602	            .collect::<Vec<_>>(),
   603	        vec![entity]
   604	    );
   605	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(entity).unwrap().0, 6);
   606	    assert_eq!(world.require::<B>(entity).unwrap().0, 13);
   607	}

   610	fn changed_filter_tracks_require_mut_using_archetype_metadata_ticks() {
   611	    let mut world = World::new();
   612	    let entity = world.spawn(A(5));
   613	    let changed = world.query_state::<(Entity, &A), Changed<A>>();
   614	
   615	    assert_eq!(
   616	        changed
   617	            .iter(&world)
   618	            .map(|(entity, _)| entity)
   619	            .collect::<Vec<_>>(),
   620	        vec![entity]
   621	    );
   622	    assert!(changed.iter(&world).next().is_none());
   623	
   624	    let (added_before, changed_before) = world
   625	        .__entity_component_ticks::<A>(entity)
   626	        .expect("A ticks should exist");
   627	
   628	    world.require_mut::<A>(entity).unwrap().0 += 1;
   629	
   630	    assert_eq!(
   631	        changed
   632	            .iter(&world)
   633	            .map(|(entity, _)| entity)
   634	            .collect::<Vec<_>>(),
   635	        vec![entity]
   636	    );
   637	
   638	    let (added_after, changed_after) = world
   639	        .__entity_component_ticks::<A>(entity)
   640	        .expect("A ticks should exist");
   641	    assert_eq!(added_after, added_before);
   642	    assert!(changed_after > changed_before);
   643	}

   645	#[test]
   646	fn optional_forms_remain_correct_after_migration_churn() {
   647	    let mut world = World::new();
   648	    let first = world.spawn((A(1), B(10)));
   649	    let second = world.spawn(A(2));
   650	    let third = world.spawn((A(3), C(30)));
   651	    let query_a = world.query_state::<(Entity, &A), ()>();
   652	    let query_b = world.query_state::<(Entity, Option<&B>), ()>();
   653	    let query_c = world.query_state::<(Entity, Option<&C>), ()>();
   654	
   655	    let mut baseline_a: Vec<_> = query_a
   656	        .iter(&world)
   657	        .map(|(entity, a)| (entity, a.0))
   658	        .collect();
   659	    baseline_a.sort_unstable_by_key(|(entity, _)| *entity);
   660	    let mut baseline_b: Vec<_> = query_b
   661	        .iter(&world)
   662	        .map(|(entity, b)| (entity, b.map(|v| v.0)))
   663	        .collect();
   664	    baseline_b.sort_unstable_by_key(|(entity, _)| *entity);
   665	    let mut baseline_c: Vec<_> = query_c
   666	        .iter(&world)
   667	        .map(|(entity, c)| (entity, c.map(|v| v.0)))
   668	        .collect();
   669	    baseline_c.sort_unstable_by_key(|(entity, _)| *entity);
   670	
   671	    assert_eq!(baseline_a, vec![(first, 1), (second, 2), (third, 3),]);
   672	    assert_eq!(
   673	        baseline_b,
   674	        vec![(first, Some(10)), (second, None), (third, None),]
   675	    );
   676	    assert_eq!(
   677	        baseline_c,
   678	        vec![(first, None), (second, None), (third, Some(30)),]
   679	    );
   680	
   681	    let _: B = world.remove(first).unwrap();
   682	    world.insert(second, (B(20), C(200))).unwrap();
   683	    world.insert(first, C(100)).unwrap();
   684	    let _: C = world.remove(third).unwrap();
   685	    world.insert(third, B(30)).unwrap();
   686	
   687	    let mut after_a: Vec<_> = query_a
   688	        .iter(&world)
   689	        .map(|(entity, a)| (entity, a.0))
   690	        .collect();
   691	    after_a.sort_unstable_by_key(|(entity, _)| *entity);
   692	    let mut after_b: Vec<_> = query_b
   693	        .iter(&world)
   694	        .map(|(entity, b)| (entity, b.map(|v| v.0)))
   695	        .collect();
   696	    after_b.sort_unstable_by_key(|(entity, _)| *entity);
   697	    let mut after_c: Vec<_> = query_c
   698	        .iter(&world)
   699	        .map(|(entity, c)| (entity, c.map(|v| v.0)))
   700	        .collect();
   701	    after_c.sort_unstable_by_key(|(entity, _)| *entity);
   702	
   703	    assert_eq!(after_a, vec![(first, 1), (second, 2), (third, 3),]);
   704	    assert_eq!(
   705	        after_b,
   706	        vec![(first, None), (second, Some(20)), (third, Some(30)),]
   707	    );
   708	    assert_eq!(
   709	        after_c,
   710	        vec![(first, Some(100)), (second, Some(200)), (third, None),]
   711	    );
   712	}

   749	#[test]
   750	fn added_filter_respects_command_flush_boundary_between_stages() {
   751	    fn queue_spawn_once(mut gate: ResMut<QuerySpawnGate>, mut commands: Commands) {
   752	        if gate.0 {
   753	            return;
   754	        }
   755	        commands.spawn(A(42));
   756	        gate.0 = true;
   757	    }
   758	
   759	    fn observe_added(mut query: Query<&A, Added<A>>, mut counts: ResMut<QueryAddedCounts>) {
   760	        counts.0.push(query.iter().count());
   761	    }
   762	
   763	    let mut world = World::new();
   764	    world.insert_resource(QuerySpawnGate(false));
   765	    world.insert_resource(QueryAddedCounts(Vec::new()));
   766	
   767	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   768	    runtime.add_systems::<QueryUpdate, _, _>(&mut world, queue_spawn_once.in_set(QueueSet));
   769	    runtime.add_systems::<QueryUpdate, _, _>(
   770	        &mut world,
   771	        observe_added.in_set(ObserveSet).after(QueueSet),
   772	    );
   773	
   774	    runtime.run_schedule::<QueryUpdate>(&mut world).unwrap();
   775	    runtime.run_schedule::<QueryUpdate>(&mut world).unwrap();
   776	
   777	    assert_eq!(world.resource::<QueryAddedCounts>().unwrap().0, vec![1, 0]);
   778	}

    48	#[test]
    49	fn runtime_executes_1_2_and_8_param_systems() {
    50	    fn bump_frame(mut frame: ResMut<Frame>) {
    51	        frame.0 += 1;
    52	    }
    53	
    54	    fn integrate_positions(mut query: Query<&mut Position>, dt: Res<DeltaTime>) {
    55	        for position in query.iter() {
    56	            position.0 += dt.0;
    57	        }
    58	    }
    59	
    60	    fn full_tick(
    61	        mut query: Query<(&mut Position, Option<&Velocity>)>,
    62	        dt: Res<DeltaTime>,
    63	        mut frame: ResMut<Frame>,
    64	        mut score: ResMut<Score>,
    65	        mut commands: Commands,
    66	        reader: EventReader<DamageEvent>,
    67	        mut writer: EventWriter<SpawnEvent>,
    68	        bonus: Res<Bonus>,
    69	    ) {
    70	        for (position, velocity) in query.iter() {
    71	            position.0 += dt.0 + bonus.0 + velocity.map_or(0.0, |v| v.0);
    72	        }
    73	        frame.0 += 10;
    74	        score.0 += reader.iter().map(|event| event.0 as u64).sum::<u64>();
    75	        writer.send(SpawnEvent);
    76	        commands.spawn(Marker);
    77	    }
    78	
    79	    let mut world = World::new();
    80	    world.spawn((Position(1.0), Velocity(2.0)));
    81	    world.spawn(Position(2.0));
    82	    world.insert_resource(Frame(0));
    83	    world.insert_resource(Score(0));
    84	    world.insert_resource(DeltaTime(0.5));
    85	    world.insert_resource(Bonus(1.0));
    86	    world.emit_event(DamageEvent(3));
    87	    world.emit_event(DamageEvent(4));
    88	
    89	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
    90	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, (bump_frame, integrate_positions, full_tick));
    91	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
    92	
    93	    let positions: Vec<_> = world
    94	        .query_state::<&Position, ()>()
    95	        .iter(&world)
    96	        .map(|position| position.0)
    97	        .collect();
    98	    assert_eq!(positions, vec![5.0, 4.0]);
    99	    assert_eq!(world.resource::<Frame>().unwrap().0, 11);
   100	    assert_eq!(world.resource::<Score>().unwrap().0, 7);
   101	    assert_eq!(world.event_count::<SpawnEvent>(), 1);
   102	    assert_eq!(world.query_state::<&Marker, ()>().iter(&world).count(), 1);
   103	}
   104	
   105	static INIT_STATE_CALLS: AtomicUsize = AtomicUsize::new(0);
   106	static EXTRACT_CALLS: AtomicUsize = AtomicUsize::new(0);
   107	
   108	struct CachedCounter(usize);
   109	
   110	impl<'w> SystemParam<'w> for CachedCounter {
   111	    type State = usize;
   112	
   113	    fn init_state(_world: &mut World) -> Result<Self::State, SystemParamError> {
   114	        INIT_STATE_CALLS.fetch_add(1, Ordering::SeqCst);
   115	        Ok(0)
   116	    }
   117	
   118	    fn access(_state: &Self::State) -> QueryAccess {
   119	        QueryAccess::default()
   120	    }
   121	
   122	    unsafe fn extract(
   123	        state: &'w mut Self::State,
   124	        _world: *mut World,
   125	        _commands: *mut Commands,
   126	    ) -> Result<Self, SystemParamError> {
   127	        *state += 1;
   128	        EXTRACT_CALLS.fetch_add(1, Ordering::SeqCst);
   129	        Ok(CachedCounter(*state))
   130	    }
   131	}
   132	
   133	#[test]
   134	fn runtime_caches_system_param_state_across_runs() {
   135	    fn cached(counter: CachedCounter, mut frame: ResMut<Frame>) {
   136	        frame.0 += counter.0 as u64;
   137	    }
   138	
   139	    let init_before = INIT_STATE_CALLS.load(Ordering::SeqCst);
   140	    let extract_before = EXTRACT_CALLS.load(Ordering::SeqCst);
   141	
   142	    let mut world = World::new();
   143	    world.insert_resource(Frame(0));
   144	
   145	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   146	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, cached);
   147	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   148	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   149	
   150	    assert_eq!(
   151	        INIT_STATE_CALLS.load(Ordering::SeqCst) - init_before,
   152	        1,
   153	        "state should initialize exactly once per registered system",
   154	    );
   155	    assert_eq!(
   156	        EXTRACT_CALLS.load(Ordering::SeqCst) - extract_before,
   157	        2,
   158	        "state should extract once per run",
   159	    );
   160	    assert_eq!(world.resource::<Frame>().unwrap().0, 3);
   161	}
   162	
   163	#[test]
   164	fn runtime_reports_extraction_errors_cleanly() {
   165	    fn requires_missing_resource(_missing: Res<MissingRes>) {}
   166	
   167	    let mut world = World::new();
   168	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   169	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, requires_missing_resource);
   170	
   171	    let err = runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap_err();
   172	    let message = format!("{err:#}");
   173	    assert!(message.contains("runtime setup failed"), "{message}");
   174	    assert!(message.contains("does not exist"), "{message}");
   175	}

   177	#[test]
   178	fn scheduler_conflict_model_respects_reads_writes_and_events() {
   179	    fn read_frame_a(_frame: Res<Frame>) {}
   180	    fn read_frame_b(_frame: Res<Frame>) {}
   181	    fn read_frame_view(_frame: ResView<Frame>) {}
   182	    fn write_frame(_frame: ResMut<Frame>) {}
   183	    fn read_events_a(_events: EventReader<DamageEvent>) {}
   184	    fn read_events_b(_events: EventReader<DamageEvent>) {}
   185	    fn write_events(_events: EventWriter<DamageEvent>) {}
   186	
   187	    let mut world = World::new();
   188	    world.insert_resource(Frame(0));
   189	
   190	    let mut read_runtime = Runtime::new();
   191	    read_runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, (read_frame_a, read_frame_b));
   192	    let read_plan = read_runtime.plan_for::<Update>().unwrap().clone();
   193	    assert!(read_plan.conflicts.is_empty());
   194	    assert_eq!(read_plan.stages.len(), 1);
   195	    assert_eq!(read_plan.stages[0].system_indices.len(), 2);
   196	
   197	    let mut read_alias_runtime = Runtime::new();
   198	    read_alias_runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, (read_frame_a, read_frame_view));
   199	    let read_alias_plan = read_alias_runtime.plan_for::<Update>().unwrap().clone();
   200	    assert!(read_alias_plan.conflicts.is_empty());
   201	    assert_eq!(read_alias_plan.stages.len(), 1);
   202	    assert_eq!(read_alias_plan.stages[0].system_indices.len(), 2);
   203	
   204	    let mut read_write_runtime = Runtime::new();
   205	    read_write_runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, (read_frame_a, write_frame));
   206	    let read_write_plan = read_write_runtime.plan_for::<Update>().unwrap().clone();
   207	    assert_eq!(read_write_plan.conflicts.len(), 1);
   208	    assert!(read_write_plan.stages.len() >= 2);
   209	
   210	    let mut read_view_write_runtime = Runtime::new();
   211	    read_view_write_runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, (read_frame_view, write_frame));
   212	    let read_view_write_plan = read_view_write_runtime
   213	        .plan_for::<Update>()
   214	        .unwrap()
   215	        .clone();
   216	    assert_eq!(read_view_write_plan.conflicts.len(), 1);
   217	    assert!(read_view_write_plan.stages.len() >= 2);
   218	
   219	    let mut event_read_runtime = Runtime::new();
   220	    event_read_runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, (read_events_a, read_events_b));
   221	    let event_read_plan = event_read_runtime.plan_for::<Update>().unwrap().clone();
   222	    assert!(event_read_plan.conflicts.is_empty());
   223	    assert_eq!(event_read_plan.stages.len(), 1);
   224	    assert_eq!(event_read_plan.stages[0].system_indices.len(), 2);
   225	
   226	    let mut event_write_runtime = Runtime::new();
   227	    event_write_runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, (read_events_a, write_events));
   228	    let event_write_plan = event_write_runtime.plan_for::<Update>().unwrap().clone();
   229	    assert_eq!(event_write_plan.conflicts.len(), 1);
   230	}

   113	fn run_order_log() -> &'static Mutex<Vec<&'static str>> {
   114	    static LOG: OnceLock<Mutex<Vec<&'static str>>> = OnceLock::new();
   115	    LOG.get_or_init(|| Mutex::new(Vec::new()))
   116	}
   117	
   118	fn push_run_order(label: &'static str) {
   119	    run_order_log().lock().unwrap().push(label);
   120	}
   121	
   122	fn clear_run_order() {
   123	    run_order_log().lock().unwrap().clear();
   124	}
   125	
   126	fn snapshot_run_order() -> Vec<&'static str> {
   127	    run_order_log().lock().unwrap().clone()
   128	}
   129	
   130	#[test]
   131	fn runtime_honors_in_set_before_and_after_ordering() {
   132	    fn run_before_set() {
   133	        push_run_order("before");
   134	    }
   135	
   136	    fn run_in_set() {
   137	        push_run_order("in_set");
   138	    }
   139	
   140	    fn run_after_set() {
   141	        push_run_order("after");
   142	    }
   143	
   144	    clear_run_order();
   145	    let mut world = World::new();
   146	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   147	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, run_in_set.in_set(GameplaySet));
   148	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, run_before_set.before(GameplaySet));
   149	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, run_after_set.after(GameplaySet));
   150	
   151	    let plan = runtime.plan_for::<Update>().unwrap().clone();
   152	    assert_eq!(plan.stages.len(), 3);
   153	    assert_eq!(plan.stages[0].system_indices.len(), 1);
   154	    assert_eq!(plan.stages[1].system_indices.len(), 1);
   155	    assert_eq!(plan.stages[2].system_indices.len(), 1);
   156	
   157	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   158	    assert_eq!(snapshot_run_order(), vec!["before", "in_set", "after"]);
   159	}

   200	    fn enqueue_first(mut commands: Commands) {
   201	        commands.spawn(Marker(1));
   202	    }
   203	
   204	    fn enqueue_second(mut commands: Commands) {
   205	        commands.spawn(Marker(2));
   206	    }
   207	
   208	    fn observe_stage_visibility(mut seen: ResMut<SeenCount>, mut query: Query<&Marker>) {
   209	        seen.0 = query.iter().count() as u32;
   210	    }
   211	
   212	    let mut world = World::new();
   213	    world.insert_resource(SeenCount(99));
   214	
   215	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   216	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(
   217	        &mut world,

   219	    );
   220

   222	    assert_eq!(plan.conflicts.len(), 0);

   225

   227

   230	        .query_state::<&Marker, ()>()

   241	    }

   243	    fn observe_followup_stage(mut seen: ResMut<SeenCount>, mut query: Query<&Marker>) {

   325	#[test]
   326	fn batch_commands_apply_in_deterministic_insertion_order() {
   327	    let mut world = World::new();
   328	    let mut commands = world.commands();
   329	    commands.batch(|batch| {
   330	        batch.spawn(Marker(1));
   331	        batch.defer(SpawnMarkerDeferred(2));
   332	        batch.queue(|world| {
   333	            world.spawn(Marker(3));
   334	            Ok(())
   335	        });
   336	    });
   337	
   338	    commands.apply(&mut world).unwrap();
   339	
   340	    let values: Vec<_> = world
   341	        .query_state::<&Marker, ()>()
   342	        .iter(&world)
   343	        .map(|marker| marker.0)
   344	        .collect();
   345	    assert_eq!(values, vec![1, 2, 3]);
   346	}

   349	fn batch_commands_do_not_mutate_before_stage_flush() {

   351	        commands.batch(|batch| {
   352	            batch.spawn(Marker(9));
   353	        });
   354	    }

   356	    fn observe_same_stage(mut seen: ResMut<SeenCount>, mut query: Query<&Marker>) {

   399	fn batch_supports_mixed_command_kinds() {

   402	    let mut commands = world.commands();

   404	        batch.queue(move |world| {
   405	            world.insert(entity, Extra(5))?;
   406	            Ok(())
   407	        });

   420	    let mut commands = world.commands();

   429	        result,

   432	        ))
   433	    ));

   435	    let values: Vec<_> = world
   436	        .query_state::<&Marker, ()>()
   437	        .iter(&world)
   438	        .map(|marker| marker.0)
   439	        .collect();
   440	    assert_eq!(values, vec![0, 10]);

   494	#[test]
   495	fn typed_commands_follow_stage_boundary_visibility_contract() {
   496	    fn enqueue_stage_typed(target: Res<TargetEntity>, mut commands: Commands) {
   497	        commands.defer(InsertExtraDeferred {
   498	            entity: target.0,
   499	            value: 17,
   500	        });
   501	    }
   502	
   503	    fn observe_followup_stage(mut seen: ResMut<SeenCount>, mut query: Query<&Extra>) {
   504	        seen.0 = query.iter().count() as u32;
   505	    }
   506	
   507	    let mut world = World::new();
   508	    let target = world.spawn(Marker(1));
   509	    world.insert_resource(TargetEntity(target));
   510	    world.insert_resource(SeenCount(0));
   511	
   512	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   513	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, enqueue_stage_typed.in_set(GameplaySet));
   514	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(
   515	        &mut world,
   516	        observe_followup_stage
   517	            .in_set(PostGameplaySet)
   518	            .after(GameplaySet),
   519	    );
   520	
   521	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   522	
   523	    assert_eq!(world.resource::<SeenCount>().unwrap().0, 1);
   524	    assert_eq!(world.require::<Extra>(target).unwrap().0, 17);
   525	}

   527	static NEXT_MARKER_ID: AtomicU32 = AtomicU32::new(0);
   528	
   529	#[test]
   530	fn borrowed_command_owner_is_stable_across_repeated_runs() {
   531	    fn enqueue_a(mut commands: Commands) {
   532	        let id = NEXT_MARKER_ID.fetch_add(1, Ordering::SeqCst);
   533	        commands.spawn(Marker(id));
   534	    }
   535	
   536	    fn enqueue_b(mut commands: Commands) {
   537	        let id = NEXT_MARKER_ID.fetch_add(1, Ordering::SeqCst);
   538	        commands.spawn(Marker(id));
   539	    }
   540	
   541	    NEXT_MARKER_ID.store(0, Ordering::SeqCst);
   542	
   543	    let mut world = World::new();
   544	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   545	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, (enqueue_a, enqueue_b));
   546	
   547	    for _ in 0..20 {
   548	        runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   549	    }
   550	
   551	    let mut ids: Vec<u32> = world
   552	        .query_state::<&Marker, ()>()
   553	        .iter(&world)
   554	        .map(|marker| marker.0)
   555	        .collect();
   556	    ids.sort_unstable();
   557	    assert_eq!(ids.len(), 40);
   558	    assert_eq!(ids, (0..40).collect::<Vec<_>>());
   559	}

   561	#[test]
   562	fn failed_schedule_drops_stage_deferred_commands_instead_of_replaying_next_run() {
   563	    fn enqueue_then_fail_once(
   564	        mut gate: ResMut<SpawnGate>,
   565	        mut commands: Commands,
   566	    ) -> anyhow::Result<()> {
   567	        if gate.0 {
   568	            return Ok(());
   569	        }
   570	        commands.spawn(Marker(99));
   571	        gate.0 = true;
   572	        anyhow::bail!("intentional failure");
   573	    }
   574	
   575	    let mut world = World::new();
   576	    world.insert_resource(SpawnGate(false));
   577	
   578	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   579	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, enqueue_then_fail_once);
   580	
   581	    assert!(runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).is_err());
   582	    assert_eq!(world.query_state::<&Marker, ()>().iter(&world).count(), 0);
   583	
   584	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   585	    assert_eq!(world.query_state::<&Marker, ()>().iter(&world).count(), 0);
   586	}

   588	#[test]
   589	#[should_panic(expected = "commands param escaped its system execution scope")]
   590	fn escaped_commands_panics_after_system_scope() {
   591	    fn stash_commands_once(mut escaped: ResMut<EscapedCommands>, commands: Commands) {
   592	        if escaped.0.is_none() {
   593	            escaped.0 = Some(commands);
   594	        }
   595	    }
   596	
   597	    let mut world = World::new();
   598	    world.insert_resource(EscapedCommands(None));
   599	
   600	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   601	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, stash_commands_once);
   602	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   603	
   604	    let mut escaped = world.remove_resource::<EscapedCommands>().unwrap();
   605	    let mut commands = escaped.0.take().expect("commands should have been stashed");
   606	    commands.spawn(Marker(1));
   607	}
   608	
   609	static PARAM_INIT_CALLS: AtomicUsize = AtomicUsize::new(0);
   610	static PARAM_EXTRACT_CALLS: AtomicUsize = AtomicUsize::new(0);
   611	
   612	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]
   613	struct StatefulParam(u32);
   614	
   615	impl<'w> SystemParam<'w> for StatefulParam {
   616	    type State = u32;
   617	
   618	    fn init_state(_world: &mut World) -> Result<Self::State, SystemParamError> {
   619	        PARAM_INIT_CALLS.fetch_add(1, Ordering::SeqCst);
   620	        Ok(0)
   621	    }
   622	
   623	    fn access(_state: &Self::State) -> QueryAccess {
   624	        QueryAccess::default()
   625	    }
   626	
   627	    unsafe fn extract(
   628	        state: &'w mut Self::State,
   629	        _world: *mut World,
   630	        _commands: *mut Commands,
   631	    ) -> Result<Self, SystemParamError> {
   632	        *state = state.saturating_add(1);
   633	        PARAM_EXTRACT_CALLS.fetch_add(1, Ordering::SeqCst);
   634	        Ok(StatefulParam(*state))
   635	    }
   636	}
   637	
   638	#[test]
   639	fn cached_system_param_state_reuse_is_stable_over_many_runs() {
   640	    fn accumulate_state(counter: StatefulParam, mut seen: ResMut<SeenCount>) {
   641	        seen.0 = seen.0.saturating_add(counter.0);
   642	    }
   643	
   644	    let init_before = PARAM_INIT_CALLS.load(Ordering::SeqCst);
   645	    let extract_before = PARAM_EXTRACT_CALLS.load(Ordering::SeqCst);
   646	
   647	    let mut world = World::new();
   648	    world.insert_resource(SeenCount(0));
   649	
   650	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   651	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, accumulate_state);
   652	
   653	    for _ in 0..5 {
   654	        runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   655	    }
   656	
   657	    assert_eq!(PARAM_INIT_CALLS.load(Ordering::SeqCst) - init_before, 1);
   658	    assert_eq!(
   659	        PARAM_EXTRACT_CALLS.load(Ordering::SeqCst) - extract_before,
   660	        5
   661	    );
   662	    assert_eq!(world.resource::<SeenCount>().unwrap().0, 15);
   663	}

   665	#[test]
   666	fn flush_stage_structural_migration_is_visible_in_followup_stage() {
   667	    fn queue_migration(mut step: ResMut<Step>, target: Res<TargetEntity>, mut commands: Commands) {
   668	        match step.0 {
   669	            0 => commands.insert(target.0, Extra(7)),
   670	            1 => commands.remove::<Extra>(target.0),
   671	            2 => commands.insert(target.0, Extra(11)),
   672	            _ => {}
   673	        }
   674	        step.0 = step.0.saturating_add(1);
   675	    }
   676	
   677	    fn observe_marker_extra(
   678	        mut history: ResMut<CountHistory>,
   679	        mut query: Query<(&Marker, &Extra)>,
   680	    ) {
   681	        history.0.push(query.iter().count());
   682	    }
   683	
   684	    let mut world = World::new();
   685	    let target = world.spawn(Marker(1));
   686	    world.insert_resource(TargetEntity(target));
   687	    world.insert_resource(Step(0));
   688	    world.insert_resource(CountHistory(Vec::new()));
   689	
   690	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   691	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, queue_migration.in_set(GameplaySet));
   692	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(
   693	        &mut world,
   694	        observe_marker_extra
   695	            .in_set(PostGameplaySet)
   696	            .after(GameplaySet),
   697	    );
   698	
   699	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   700	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   701	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   702	
   703	    assert_eq!(world.resource::<CountHistory>().unwrap().0, vec![1, 0, 1]);
   704	    assert_eq!(world.require::<Extra>(target).unwrap().0, 11);
   705	}

   707	#[test]
   708	fn system_order_controls_added_and_changed_visibility() {
   709	    fn queue_spawn_once(mut gate: ResMut<SpawnGate>, mut commands: Commands) {
   710	        if gate.0 {
   711	            return;
   712	        }
   713	        commands.spawn(Marker(5));
   714	        gate.0 = true;
   715	    }
   716	
   717	    fn mutate_markers(mut query: Query<&mut Marker>) {
   718	        for marker in query.iter() {
   719	            marker.0 = marker.0.saturating_add(1);
   720	        }
   721	    }
   722	
   723	    fn observe_added_changed(
   724	        mut added: Query<&Marker, Added<Marker>>,
   725	        mut changed: Query<&Marker, Changed<Marker>>,
   726	        mut history: ResMut<AddedChangedHistory>,
   727	    ) {
   728	        history
   729	            .0
   730	            .push((added.iter().count(), changed.iter().count()));
   731	    }
   732	
   733	    let mut world = World::new();
   734	    world.insert_resource(SpawnGate(false));
   735	    world.insert_resource(AddedChangedHistory(Vec::new()));
   736	
   737	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   738	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, queue_spawn_once.in_set(GameplaySet));
   739	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(
   740	        &mut world,
   741	        mutate_markers.in_set(PostGameplaySet).after(GameplaySet),
   742	    );
   743	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(
   744	        &mut world,
   745	        observe_added_changed
   746	            .in_set(LateObserveSet)
   747	            .after(PostGameplaySet),
   748	    );
   749	
   750	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   751	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   752	
   753	    assert_eq!(
   754	        world.resource::<AddedChangedHistory>().unwrap().0,
   755	        vec![(1, 1), (0, 1)]
   756	    );
   757	}

   759	#[test]
   760	fn event_heavy_mixed_workload_with_structural_churn_remains_stable() {
   761	    fn churn_and_emit(
   762	        mut step: ResMut<Step>,
   763	        target: Res<TargetEntity>,
   764	        mut commands: Commands,
   765	        mut writer: EventWriter<DamageEvent>,
   766	    ) {
   767	        step.0 = step.0.saturating_add(1);
   768	        for offset in 0..4 {
   769	            writer.send(DamageEvent(
   770	                step.0.saturating_mul(10).saturating_add(offset),
   771	            ));
   772	        }
   773	        if step.0 % 2 == 1 {
   774	            commands.remove::<Toggle>(target.0);
   775	        } else {
   776	            commands.insert(target.0, Toggle);
   777	        }
   778	    }
   779	
   780	    fn observe_events_and_presence(
   781	        reader: EventReader<DamageEvent>,
   782	        mut query: Query<&Toggle>,
   783	        mut events: ResMut<EventHistory>,
   784	        mut presence: ResMut<PresenceHistory>,
   785	    ) {
   786	        events.0.push(reader.iter().count());
   787	        presence.0.push(query.iter().count());
   788	    }
   789	
   790	    let mut world = World::new();
   791	    world.configure_event_channel::<DamageEvent>(EventChannelConfig {
   792	        capacity: None,
   793	        overflow: OverflowPolicy::DropOldest,
   794	        lifetime: EventLifetime::FrameTransient,
   795	        tracing: EventTracingPolicy::Disabled,
   796	    });
   797	    let target = world.spawn((Marker(0), Toggle));
   798	    world.insert_resource(TargetEntity(target));
   799	    world.insert_resource(Step(0));
   800	    world.insert_resource(EventHistory(Vec::new()));
   801	    world.insert_resource(PresenceHistory(Vec::new()));
   802	
   803	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   804	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, churn_and_emit.in_set(GameplaySet));
   805	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(
   806	        &mut world,
   807	        observe_events_and_presence
   808	            .in_set(PostGameplaySet)
   809	            .after(GameplaySet),
   810	    );
   811	
   812	    for _ in 0..4 {
   813	        runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   814	        world.finish_event_frame();
   815	    }
   816	
   817	    assert_eq!(
   818	        world.resource::<EventHistory>().unwrap().0,
   819	        vec![4, 4, 4, 4]
   820	    );
   821	    assert_eq!(
   822	        world.resource::<PresenceHistory>().unwrap().0,
   823	        vec![0, 1, 0, 1]
   824	    );
   825	}

   827	#[test]
   828	fn deferred_commands_keep_secondary_indexes_correct_after_apply() {
   829	    fn queue_index_updates(
   830	        mut step: ResMut<Step>,
   831	        target: Res<TargetEntity>,
   832	        mut commands: Commands,
   833	    ) {
   834	        match step.0 {
   835	            0 => commands.insert(target.0, IndexedName("renamed".to_string())),
   836	            1 => commands.remove::<IndexedName>(target.0),
   837	            2 => commands.insert(target.0, IndexedName("restored".to_string())),
   838	            _ => {}
   839	        }
   840	        step.0 = step.0.saturating_add(1);
   841	    }
   842	
   843	    let mut world = World::new();
   844	    world.ensure_component_index::<IndexedName, String>(|name| name.0.clone());
   845	    let target = world.spawn(IndexedName("initial".to_string()));
   846	    let other = world.spawn(IndexedName("other".to_string()));
   847	    world.insert_resource(TargetEntity(target));
   848	    world.insert_resource(Step(0));
   849	
   850	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   851	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, queue_index_updates);
   852	
   853	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   854	    assert_eq!(
   855	        world.find_entity_by_index::<IndexedName, String>(&"renamed".to_string()),
   856	        Some(target)
   857	    );
   858	    assert_eq!(
   859	        world.find_entity_by_index::<IndexedName, String>(&"initial".to_string()),
   860	        None
   861	    );
   862	    assert_eq!(
   863	        world.find_entity_by_index::<IndexedName, String>(&"other".to_string()),
   864	        Some(other)
   865	    );
   866	
   867	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   868	    assert_eq!(
   869	        world.find_entity_by_index::<IndexedName, String>(&"renamed".to_string()),
   870	        None
   871	    );
   872	    assert_eq!(
   873	        world.find_entity_by_index::<IndexedName, String>(&"other".to_string()),
   874	        Some(other)
   875	    );
   876	
   877	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   878	    assert_eq!(
   879	        world.find_entity_by_index::<IndexedName, String>(&"restored".to_string()),
   880	        Some(target)
   881	    );
   882	}

   884	#[test]
   885	fn event_channel_iter_new_reads_only_unseen_events_across_runs() {
   886	    fn produce_once(mut step: ResMut<Step>, mut writer: EventWriter<DamageEvent>) {
   887	        if step.0 == 0 {
   888	            writer.send(DamageEvent(7));
   889	        }
   890	        step.0 = step.0.saturating_add(1);
   891	    }
   892	
   893	    fn consume_unread(mut channel: EventChannel<DamageEvent>, mut history: ResMut<EventHistory>) {
   894	        history.0.push(channel.iter_new().count());
   895	    }
   896	
   897	    let mut world = World::new();
   898	    world.insert_resource(Step(0));
   899	    world.insert_resource(EventHistory(Vec::new()));
   900	
   901	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   902	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, produce_once.in_set(GameplaySet));
   903	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(
   904	        &mut world,
   905	        consume_unread.in_set(PostGameplaySet).after(GameplaySet),
   906	    );
   907	
   908	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   909	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   910	
   911	    assert_eq!(world.resource::<EventHistory>().unwrap().0, vec![1, 0]);
   912	    assert_eq!(world.event_count::<DamageEvent>(), 1);
   913	}
   914	
   915	#[test]
   916	fn event_channel_iter_new_survives_drop_oldest_overflow() {
   917	    fn emit_each_run(mut step: ResMut<Step>, mut writer: EventWriter<DamageEvent>) {
   918	        step.0 = step.0.saturating_add(1);
   919	        writer.send(DamageEvent(step.0));
   920	    }
   921	
   922	    fn consume_unread(mut channel: EventChannel<DamageEvent>, mut history: ResMut<EventHistory>) {
   923	        history.0.push(channel.iter_new().count());
   924	    }
   925	
   926	    let mut world = World::new();
   927	    world.configure_event_channel::<DamageEvent>(EventChannelConfig {
   928	        capacity: Some(1),
   929	        overflow: OverflowPolicy::DropOldest,
   930	        lifetime: EventLifetime::Manual,
   931	        tracing: EventTracingPolicy::Disabled,
   932	    });
   933	    world.insert_resource(Step(0));
   934	    world.insert_resource(EventHistory(Vec::new()));
   935	
   936	    let mut runtime = Runtime::new();
   937	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(&mut world, emit_each_run.in_set(GameplaySet));
   938	    runtime.add_systems::<Update, _, _>(
   939	        &mut world,
   940	        consume_unread.in_set(PostGameplaySet).after(GameplaySet),
   941	    );
   942	
   943	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   944	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   945	    runtime.run_schedule::<Update>(&mut world).unwrap();
   946	
   947	    assert_eq!(world.resource::<EventHistory>().unwrap().0, vec![1, 1, 1]);
   948	    assert_eq!(world.event_count::<DamageEvent>(), 1);
   949	    assert_eq!(world.read_events::<DamageEvent>(), &[DamageEvent(3)]);
   950	}

     1	use ecs::prelude::*;
     2	use std::panic::{AssertUnwindSafe, catch_unwind};
     3	
     4	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
     5	struct A(i32);
     6	
     7	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
     8	struct B(i32);
     9	
    10	#[test]
    11	fn same_type_double_mut_query_panics() {
    12	    let mut world = World::new();
    13	    world.spawn(A(1));
    14	
    15	    let query = world.query_state::<(&mut A, &mut A), ()>();
    16	    let panic_result = catch_unwind(AssertUnwindSafe(|| {
    17	        let _ = query.iter(&mut world).next();
    18	    }));
    19	    assert!(panic_result.is_err());
    20	}
    21	
    22	#[test]
    23	fn same_type_mut_read_query_panics() {
    24	    let mut world = World::new();
    25	    world.spawn(A(1));
    26	
    27	    let query = world.query_state::<(&mut A, &A), ()>();
    28	    let panic_result = catch_unwind(AssertUnwindSafe(|| {
    29	        let _ = query.iter(&mut world).next();
    30	    }));
    31	    assert!(panic_result.is_err());
    32	}
    33	
    34	#[test]
    35	fn optional_mut_query_handles_present_absent_and_repeated_iteration() {
    36	    let mut world = World::new();
    37	    let with_b = world.spawn((A(1), B(10)));
    38	    let without_b = world.spawn(A(2));
    39	
    40	    let query = world.query_state::<(&mut A, Option<&mut B>), ()>();
    41	
    42	    for (a, maybe_b) in query.iter(&mut world) {
    43	        a.0 += 1;
    44	        if let Some(b) = maybe_b {
    45	            b.0 += a.0;
    46	        }
    47	    }
    48	
    49	    for (a, maybe_b) in query.iter(&mut world) {
    50	        a.0 += 1;
    51	        if let Some(b) = maybe_b {
    52	            b.0 += a.0;
    53	        }
    54	    }
    55	
    56	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(with_b).unwrap().0, 3);
    57	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(without_b).unwrap().0, 4);
    58	    assert_eq!(world.require::<B>(with_b).unwrap().0, 15);
    59	}

    56	
    57	    let changed = world.query_state::<(Entity, &StatefulHealth), Changed<StatefulHealth>>();

    89	            .component_state::<StatefulHealth>(entity)
    90	            .expect("state must exist")
    91	            .version,
    92	        1
    93	    );

    95	        changed
    96	            .iter(&world)
    97	            .map(|(entity, _)| entity)
    98	            .collect::<Vec<_>>(),
    99	        vec![entity]
   100	    );
   101	}

     1	use ecs::prelude::*;
     2	use scheduler::ScheduleLabel;
     3	
     4	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
     5	struct A(i32);
     6	
     7	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
     8	struct B(i32);
     9	
    10	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
    11	struct C(i32);
    12	
    13	#[derive(Debug, PartialEq, Eq, ecs::Component, ecs::Resource)]
    14	struct SeenCounts(Vec<usize>);
    15	
    16	#[derive(Copy, Clone)]
    17	struct Update;
    18	
    19	impl ScheduleLabel for Update {
    20	    fn name() -> &'static str {
    21	        "Update"
    22	    }
    23	}
    24	
    25	fn queue_spawn(mut commands: Commands) {
    26	    commands.spawn(A(1));
    27	}
    28	
    29	fn record_a_count(mut query: Query<&A>, mut counts: ResMut<SeenCounts>) {
    30	    counts.0.push(query.iter().count());
    31	}
    32	
    33	#[test]
    34	fn archetype_location_tracking_updates_on_insert_remove_and_despawn() {
    35	    let mut world = World::new();
    36	    let first = world.spawn(A(1));
    37	    let second = world.spawn(A(2));
    38	
    39	    let first_before = world
    40	        .__entity_archetype_location(first)
    41	        .expect("first entity should be tracked");
    42	    let second_before = world
    43	        .__entity_archetype_location(second)
    44	        .expect("second entity should be tracked");
    45	    assert_eq!(world.__entity_archetype_component_count(first), Some(1));
    46	    assert_eq!(world.__entity_archetype_component_count(second), Some(1));
    47	    assert_eq!(first_before.0, second_before.0);
    48	    assert_eq!(first_before.1, 0);
    49	    assert_eq!(second_before.1, 1);
    50	
    51	    world.insert(first, B(10)).unwrap();
    52	
    53	    let first_after_insert = world
    54	        .__entity_archetype_location(first)
    55	        .expect("first entity should still be tracked");
    56	    let second_after_insert = world
    57	        .__entity_archetype_location(second)
    58	        .expect("second entity should still be tracked");
    59	    assert_eq!(world.__entity_archetype_component_count(first), Some(2));
    60	    assert_eq!(world.__entity_archetype_component_count(second), Some(1));
    61	    assert_ne!(first_after_insert.0, second_after_insert.0);
    62	    assert_eq!(second_after_insert.1, 0);
    63	
    64	    let _: B = world.remove(first).unwrap();
    65	    let first_after_remove = world
    66	        .__entity_archetype_location(first)
    67	        .expect("first entity should still be tracked");
    68	    assert_eq!(world.__entity_archetype_component_count(first), Some(1));
    69	    assert_eq!(first_after_remove.0, second_after_insert.0);
    70	
    71	    world.despawn(second).unwrap();
    72	    assert!(world.__entity_archetype_location(second).is_none());
    73	    assert_eq!(
    74	        world
    75	            .__entity_archetype_location(first)
    76	            .expect("remaining entity should be tracked")
    77	            .1,
    78	        0
    79	    );
    80	}

    83	fn command_flush_boundary_remains_stage_based() {

    96	#[test]
    97	fn archetype_value_and_metadata_stay_aligned_across_migration() {
    98	    let mut world = World::new();
    99	    let first = world.spawn(A(11));
   100	    let second = world.spawn(A(22));
   101	
   102	    let (added_before, changed_before) = world
   103	        .__entity_component_ticks::<A>(first)
   104	        .expect("ticks should exist for inserted component");
   105	    assert_eq!(added_before, changed_before);
   106	
   107	    world.insert(first, B(5)).unwrap();
   108	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(first).unwrap().0, 11);
   109	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(second).unwrap().0, 22);
   110	    let (added_after_insert, changed_after_insert) = world
   111	        .__entity_component_ticks::<A>(first)
   112	        .expect("ticks should remain aligned after migration");
   113	    assert_eq!(added_after_insert, added_before);
   114	    assert_eq!(changed_after_insert, changed_before);
   115	
   116	    for value in world.query_state::<&mut A, ()>().iter(&mut world) {
   117	        value.0 += 1;
   118	    }
   119	    let (added_after_mut, changed_after_mut) = world
   120	        .__entity_component_ticks::<A>(first)
   121	        .expect("ticks should exist after mutable query");
   122	    assert_eq!(added_after_mut, added_before);
   123	    assert!(changed_after_mut > changed_after_insert);
   124	
   125	    let _: B = world.remove(first).unwrap();
   126	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(first).unwrap().0, 12);
   127	    let (added_after_remove, changed_after_remove) = world
   128	        .__entity_component_ticks::<A>(first)
   129	        .expect("ticks should stay aligned after remove migration");
   130	    assert_eq!(added_after_remove, added_before);
   131	    assert_eq!(changed_after_remove, changed_after_mut);
   132	}

   152	#[test]
   153	fn repeated_swap_remove_repair_holds_across_chained_migrations() {
   154	    let mut world = World::new();
   155	    let first = world.spawn(A(1));
   156	    let second = world.spawn(A(2));
   157	    let third = world.spawn(A(3));
   158	
   159	    assert_eq!(
   160	        world
   161	            .__entity_archetype_location(third)
   162	            .expect("third should be tracked")
   163	            .1,
   164	        2
   165	    );
   166	
   167	    world.insert(first, B(10)).unwrap();
   168	    assert_eq!(
   169	        world
   170	            .__entity_archetype_location(third)
   171	            .expect("third should remain tracked")
   172	            .1,
   173	        0
   174	    );
   175	    assert_eq!(
   176	        world
   177	            .__entity_archetype_location(second)
   178	            .expect("second should remain tracked")
   179	            .1,
   180	        1
   181	    );
   182	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(third).unwrap().0, 3);
   183	
   184	    world.insert(second, B(20)).unwrap();
   185	    assert_eq!(
   186	        world
   187	            .__entity_archetype_location(third)
   188	            .expect("third should remain tracked")
   189	            .1,
   190	        0
   191	    );
   192	
   193	    let _: B = world.remove(first).unwrap();
   194	    assert_eq!(
   195	        world
   196	            .__entity_archetype_location(third)
   197	            .expect("third should remain tracked")
   198	            .1,
   199	        0
   200	    );
   201	    assert_eq!(
   202	        world
   203	            .__entity_archetype_location(first)
   204	            .expect("first should move back into A archetype")
   205	            .1,
   206	        1
   207	    );
   208	
   209	    let _: B = world.remove(second).unwrap();
   210	    let first_location = world
   211	        .__entity_archetype_location(first)
   212	        .expect("first should be tracked");
   213	    let second_location = world
   214	        .__entity_archetype_location(second)
   215	        .expect("second should be tracked");
   216	    let third_location = world
   217	        .__entity_archetype_location(third)
   218	        .expect("third should be tracked");
   219	    assert_eq!(first_location.0, second_location.0);
   220	    assert_eq!(second_location.0, third_location.0);
   221	    assert_eq!(third_location.1, 0);
   222	    assert_eq!(first_location.1, 1);
   223	    assert_eq!(second_location.1, 2);
   224	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(first).unwrap().0, 1);
   225	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(second).unwrap().0, 2);
   226	    assert_eq!(world.require::<A>(third).unwrap().0, 3);
   227	}
